Alvor and Sigrid's House

**Alvor and Sigrid's House** is a medium-sized home in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). It is home to the local blacksmith, [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor"), and his family.

*"I'm bored standing around, papa. I could take over for you..."*

The building encompasses both the house and a smithing area outside and to the side of the house.

The house consists of one area only, *[Alvor and Sigrid's House](#Alvor_and_Sigrid.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Alvor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alvor "Skyrim:Alvor") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")  [Dorthe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorthe "Skyrim:Dorthe")  [Sigrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigrid "Skyrim:Sigrid")  [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") † |

**†** Only if you side with him in [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound").

## Related Quests

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Blacksmithing Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmithing_Tutorial "Skyrim:Blacksmithing Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Exterior

All the tools to make and temper weapons and armor are here, namely a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). There are five [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and five [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot") under the workbench. On the table by the tanning rack are some gauntlets, boots, a helmet, a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet"). Around the corner from the workbench is a display rack with an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword").

## Alvor and Sigrid's House

Ground floor

Cellar

There are two floors to the house: the first floor and the cellar. They are split into areas discernible by the furniture, with the stairs to the cellar by the far left wall. The first floor is split into two areas: the bedroom and the kitchen. The bedroom contains two beds, two chairs by a table, a wardrobe, and a chest. The double bed is Alvor and Sigrid's, and the single bed is Dorthe's. There is a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and some [loose coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the table, as well as a copy of *[A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Gentleman%27s_Guide_to_Whiterun "Skyrim:A Gentleman's Guide to Whiterun")*. Next to this table is a cupboard, which has a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron") on top. At the foot of the double bed is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items. [Stump](/wiki/Skyrim:Stump "Skyrim:Stump") can sometimes be found sleeping on the rug between the beds, after following Dorthe home. The other side of the room is a mix between a dining room and kitchen; by the fire is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), and above the fire is a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"). Next to the fire is an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), and three [dead rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Opposite the fire is a dining table with an [Eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), three pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two [chicken eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and a piece of [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). There is a basket next to the table with two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") in it. Next to this is a cupboard containing [sliced Eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), an [Eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), an [Eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and a single [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). Hanging from the roof near this are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

The cellar is both a social and living area for the family, and a storage room for any extra weapons and armor that Alvor has made. Moving from the stairs there is a small table with a chair, a weapons table to the right, an L-shaped "bar", shelves behind the bar, a chair by an end table, and a wardrobe and chest by the far wall. On the weapons table are three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"). On the woodpile next to the table is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). On top of the end table are two [blacksmith's potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion"), while the chest has leveled items in it. There is a cupboard next to this, with an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") on top of it. On the bar you can find [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), an [iron cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") under the bar. Behind the bar is a cupboard containing clutter. Hanging under the stairs is a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and a dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). There is also a small table containing a piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread").

## Notes

- The front door has a novice-level lock. The house is locked most of the time, so it does not make a very good temporary home for the player despite Alvor's proffered hospitality. Furthermore, if you manage to get inside the house after midnight you are not welcome and may be told to leave.
- The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alvor%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Alvor's House") to the house is carried by Alvor, Sigrid, and Dorthe.
- If you befriend Alvor during Before the Storm, the iron and steel ingots beside the workbench will be free to take.
- The armor sitting on the table in the work area will respawn, and will also be leveled. The iron and steel ingots beside the workbench will also respawn.

## Bugs

- Dorthe's bed isn't a child's bed, allowing her to sleep in the parents' bed, causing one of them to stay up all night.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. Her bed wasn't marked as a child's bed, which forced her AI to pick the nearest one available.

Alvor

**Alvor** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") who lives in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). He lives with his wife [Sigrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigrid "Skyrim:Sigrid") and his daughter [Dorthe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorthe "Skyrim:Dorthe"), and he is the uncle of [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar"). Hadvar will send you to him after he helps you escape from your execution at [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). Alvor, for his part, will direct you to [Jarl Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). After he offers you help, he allows you to take most of the items in his house as well as the ingots near his [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). If asked, Alvor will [task you](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmithing_Tutorial "Skyrim:Blacksmithing Tutorial") with creating some basic weapons and apparel using various tools as an introduction to [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing").

Alvor lives a peaceful existence in the village of Riverwood. As town blacksmith, he works his forge every day between 8am and 8pm then spends an hour dining with Dorthe and Sigrid inside the house. At 9pm he visits the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") where he socializes for two hours with the other regulars. At 11pm he returns to his family and spends an hour wandering around until he finally goes to bed at midnight for six hours of sleep. The only exception to this routine occurs if you follow Hadvar during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"). He will then sit at his forge 24 hours a day, waiting for you to arrive.

He wears a [blacksmith's apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Apron#0005b69f "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Apron") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b69e "Skyrim:Shoes"). He carries a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alvor%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Alvor's House") to his house.

## Related Quests

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Blacksmithing Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmithing_Tutorial "Skyrim:Blacksmithing Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When you approach him he will politely greet you with:

:   *"Ain't every day we get visitors in Riverwood."*
:   *"Whatever you need. By Ysmir, if it's simple and strong, I can forge it."*
:   *"You lookin' for a new blade?"*
:   *"I could forge you a warhammer that would crush a giant's head like a walnut."*
:   *"You the sneaky type? Got some nice daggers around here somewhere..."*

Additionally, if you are playing as an elf, he will say:

:   *"Iron and steel mostly. I might even have some of your fancy Elven pieces lying around somewhere..."*

For all other races, he will change the greeting to:

:   *"Iron or steel is what you need. Leave that fancy Elven stuff to the Elves."*

When spoken to directly:

:   **What can you tell me about Riverwood?**
:   *"Gerdur's family first settled here as wood cutters a few generations ago. She and Hod run the mill. I make a decent living sharpening axes and fixing the sawmill."*

:   **Can I use your forge?**
:   *"I see no harm in it, if you have the skill. The grindstone will improve your weapons. Use the table to improve your armor. If you've got the raw materials, you can use the forge to make something new."*

If you choose to follow Hadvar during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), Alvor will have a lot more dialogue options. See [this section](#Before_the_Storm) for details.

## Conversations

*"Woman, you'll be the death of me yet."*

*"Can I make something now, papa?"*

While everything looks peaceful on the outside, Alvor faces several problems with his wife, specifically on how Dorthe should be raised. Every day Dorthe visits Alvor near his forge at 4pm, learning the trade, and spends the rest of her time with local prankster [Frodnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Frodnar "Skyrim:Frodnar"). Sigrid is worried to no end and wants Dorthe to act more like a girl, causing the couple to have several discussions:

**Alvor**: *"Sigrid! Love of my life! When you get a spare moment, I could use some water."*
**Sigrid**: *"Don't you sweet talk me, Alvor. Not after last night. I'll bring you water when I'm done with my other chores."*
**Alvor**: *"Woman, you'll be the death of me yet. Fine, take your time. I'll just die of thirst in the heat of this forge."*

**Sigrid**: *"I've got some fresh cabbage. I'm thinking of making some apple cabbage stew."*
**Alvor**: *"Dorthe won't eat that. Are you trying to starve the child?"*
**Sigrid**: *"She needs to learn to eat what I serve her. I swear, you spoil that child rotten. Besides, it's one of your favorites."*
**Alvor**: *"Ay, it is. I suppose it won't hurt the girl to eat it this once. And speaking of spoiling Dorthe, who made her a new doll last week?"*
**Sigrid**: *"Just never you mind about that."*

**Dorthe**: *"You really think I can be a blacksmith someday, papa? As good as Eorlund Gray-Mane? Or maybe... even as good as you?"*
**Alvor**: *"Oh, I know it! You keep working hard, like you been doing, and you could be the greatest blacksmith Skyrim has ever seen."*
**Dorthe**: *"He he. Thanks, papa."*

When Dorthe hangs out near the forge, she will often try and convince Alvor to let her take over. She will choose between three lines of dialogue and Alvor will do the same:

| Speaker | Conversation |
| --- | --- |
| **Dorthe** | *"Can I make something now, papa?"* |
| *"Is it time yet? Time for me to make my sword? Or maybe... an axe?"* |
| *"I'm bored standing around, papa. I could take over for you..."* |
| **Alvor** | *"Later, little one. I need to finish what I'm working on. But keep watching. Watch, and learn."* |
| *"He he. Not just yet, Dorthe. I need to keep forging, and you need to keep watching."* |
| *"Patience, Dorthe. You'll get some time at the forge, I promise you. But not right now. You need to keep watching me. That's how you'll learn."* |
| **Dorthe** | *"Don't worry, I am."* |
| *"All right. But I am getting a bit tired of waiting."* |
| *"Yes, sir."* |

## Quest-Related Events

### Before the Storm

If you escaped [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") with [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") soldier [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar"), you will be pointed towards Alvor in Riverwood, who turns out to be Hadvar's uncle. You can choose to run ahead and talk to Alvor before Hadvar reaches him, or you can wait for Hadvar to catch up. If you run ahead and tell Alvor that Hadvar sent you:

:   **Hadvar said you could help me out.**
:   *"Hadvar? How do you know him?"*

    :   **He's a friend. He promised you could help.**
    :   *"I'd be glad to help a friend of Hadvar. But you didn't answer my question - how do you know him?"*
    :   **He helped me escape from prison.**
    :   *"Did he, now? That doesn't sound like my nephew at all. I doubt he'd be mixed up with the likes of you."*

Then you can tell him the [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack on Helgen and your heroic escape along with [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") or end the conversation by selecting "Never mind":

:   **A dragon attacked Helgen and destroyed it. Hadvar and I escaped together.**
:   *"What? A dragon? In Helgen? That explains what I saw earlier... flying down the valley from the south... I was hoping I was wrong about what I thought it was..."*
:   **Never mind.** (only available if the player talks to Alvor before Hadvar arrives, not available if the player intercept the conversation)
:   *"Suit yourself. I hate to turn away any friend of Hadvar, but in times like these... you understand if I can't just take your word for it."*

The first option leads to:

:   **It was a dragon. Hadvar will tell you the same thing.**
:   **That dragon flew off this way. You must have seen it.**
:   *"You're right, I saw it. Didn't want to believe my own eyes, is all."*

Either option leads to Alvor's same rest response:

:   *"A dragon... here in Skyrim. What's this world coming to? First the war, now dragons... trouble loves company, they say... The Jarl needs to know if there's a dragon on the loose. Riverwood is defenseless... We need to get word to [Jarl Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") to send whatever soldiers he can. If you'll do that for me, I'll be in your debt."*

This will provide your next objective of the quest.

In either case, when Hadvar finally reaches Riverwood, they will have a brief conversation near Alvor's forge. Some of the dialogue lines will differ if you already told Alvor everything before Hadvar arrived:

*"Shor's bones, what happened to you, boy?"*

*"A dragon? That's... ridiculous. You aren't drunk, are you boy?"*

**Hadvar**: *"Uncle Alvor! Hello!"*
**Alvor**: *"Hadvar? What are you doing here? Are you on leave from..."* **OR** *"Hadvar, thank Talos! Your friend told me about Helgen..."*
**Alvor**: *"Shor's bones, what happened to you, boy? Are you in some kind of trouble?"*
**Hadvar**: *"Shh.. Uncle, please. Keep your voice down. I'm fine. But we should go inside to talk."*
**Alvor**: *"What's going on? And who's this?"*
**Hadvar**: *"He's/ She's a friend. Saved my life in fact. Come on, I'll explain everything, but we need to go inside."*
**Alvor**: *"Okay, okay. Come inside, then. Sigrid will get you something to eat and you can tell me all about it."* **OR** *"Come on inside. Sigrid will get you something to eat and you can tell us what happened."*

There's another case if you talk to Alvor before Hadvar finishes his conversation with Alvor:

:   **Do you have any supplies I could take?**
:   *"Of course. Take what you need. But what's all this about? What are you two doing here?"*

then open the item swapping interface, after the player closes the interface, the dialogues are almost the same as talking to Alvor before Hadvar arrives except the option "Never mind".

If Hadvar finishes his conversation with Alvor without player's interception, and the player follows them inside, Alvor will summon his wife with the words *"Sigrid! We have company!"* and will then take a seat opposite Hadvar.

**Sigrid**: *"Hadvar! We've been so worried about you! Come, you two must be hungry. Sit down and I'll get you something to eat."*
**Alvor**: *"Now, then, boy. What's the big mystery? What are you doing here, looking like you lost an argument with a cave bear?"* **OR** *"Now, then, boy. Helgen was destroyed? How did you get away?"*
**Hadvar**: *"I don't know where to start. You know I was assigned to General Tullius's guard. We were stopped in Helgen when we were attacked... by a dragon."*
**Alvor**: *"A dragon? That's... ridiculous. You aren't drunk, are you boy?"* **OR** *"When your friend told me, I didn't believe it at first either."*
**Sigrid**: *"Husband. Let him tell his story."* **OR** *"Mara's mercy! A dragon... in Helgen? Why, it could be here at any moment!"*
**Alvor**: *"I'm sure Riverwood will be all right, dear. When the Jarl learns what's happened, he's sure to send soldiers. Go on, Hadvar. Let's hear the rest of it."* (only show up if the player told Alvor about the dragon ahead of Hadvar)
**Hadvar**: *"Not much more to tell. This dragon flew over and just wrecked the whole place. Mass confusion. I don't know if anyone else got out alive. I doubt I'd have made it out myself if not for my friend here. I need to get back to Solitude and let them know what's happened. I thought you could help us out. Food, supplies, a place to stay."*
**Alvor**: *"Of course! Any friend of Hadvar's is a friend of mine. I'm glad to help however I can."*

Alvor will then seek you out and repeat: *"Like I said, I'm glad to help in any way I can. Help yourself to whatever you need, within reason. But I need your help. We need your help."* You can then look through his inventory for supplies; once you're done, he will continue: *"The Jarl needs to know if there's a dragon on the loose. Riverwood is defenseless... We need to get word to Jarl Balgruuf in Whiterun to send whatever soldiers he can. If you'll do that for me, I'll be in your debt."*

He will then provide a wealth of information, including the easiest route to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"): *"Cross the river and then head north. You'll see it, just past the falls. When you get to Whiterun just keep going up. When you get to the top of the hill, you're at Dragonsreach, the Jarl's palace."* He will also tell you about [Jarl Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"): *"Jarl Balgruuf? He rules Whiterun Hold. A good man, perhaps a bit over-cautious, but these are dangerous times. So far he's managed to stay out of the war. I'm afraid it can't last, though."* He will then introduce the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") by explaining the jarl's political stance: *"I don't think he likes either Ulfric or Elisif much. Who can blame him? But I've no doubt he'll prove loyal to the Empire in the end. He's no traitor."* When asked about his own stance on the conflict, Alvor will reply: *"Of course. Skyrim has always been part of the Empire. That doesn't mean I support everything the Empire's been doing lately, but Nords have never been fair-weather friends."* He will also explain about [Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"): *"Ah, I forget you're new to Skyrim. Jarl Elisif, I should say, although only because she was married to Jarl Torryg when he was murdered. Ulfric murdered Torygg, you know. Walked right into his palace in Solitude and killed him. Shouted him to death, if you believe the stories. That's what started this whole war. The Empire couldn't ignore that. Once the jarls start killing each other, we're back to the bad old days."* On the civil war as a whole, he will provide his personal opinion: *"People are rightly stirred up about the damn Thalmor being allowed to roam around arresting people, just for worshipping Talos. But was it worth tearing Skyrim apart, and maybe destroying the Empire? No, Ulfric will have a lot to answer for in the end. Nords have always supported the Empire, and the Empire has always been good for Skyrim."* When you ask him why the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") have a right to arrest [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worshippers, he will say: *"It's from that treaty that ended the Great War, remember, when the Emperor was forced by the Thalmor to outlaw Talos worship. We didn't pay much attention to it when I was a boy - everyone still had their little shrine to Talos. But then Ulfric and his "Sons of Skyrim" started agitating about it, and sure enough the Emperor had to crack down. Dragging people off in the middle of the night... one of the main causes of this war, if you ask me."* With these words, he will leave the house and return to his regular duties again.

# Skyrim:Amaund Motierre

## Overview

| Amaund Motierre (RefID: 0003B43B) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Amaund_Motierre "Lore:Amaund Motierre")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") | | |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Bard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bard_(class) "Skyrim:Bard (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0003B43B | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0003B43A |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 73 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 63 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 59 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") | | |

| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes, until [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") | | |
| Voice Type | [Unique](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique "Category:Skyrim-Voice-Unique") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DBAmaundMotierreFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DBAmaundMotierreFaction "Skyrim:DBAmaundMotierreFaction") | | |

Amaund Motierre

**Amaund Motierre** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") of questionable background and employment, first encountered within [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") with his bodyguard [Rexus](/wiki/Skyrim:Rexus "Skyrim:Rexus"). He plays a major role in the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") questline, during which he hires them to assassinate the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)"). Upon meeting Motierre, you are given a note with vague instructions for three separate killings. It is then revealed that these contracts will set the stage for the death of the Emperor, the main contract for which the Dark Brotherhood has been hired.

Motierre is a cautious man, refusing to divulge any information about himself or his aims. He also refuses to outright reveal the names of the first three targets in his note, instead offering a necklace to cover the costs of investigating the vague instructions therein. [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") identifies the necklace as being uniquely made for members of the Emperor's [Elder Council](/wiki/Lore:Elder_Council "Lore:Elder Council"), which leads [Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") to deduce Motierre's motives: *"Motierre, you naughty, naughty boy. Hiring the Dark Brotherhood to help you rise beyond your station. Delicious."* After completion of the contract, Motierre expresses his profound gratitude, saying that you have done the Empire a greater service than you might realize.

He wears [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee80 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee82 "Skyrim:Clothing"). When he moves to the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"), he also carries a [flawless garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Garnet "Skyrim:Flawless Garnet"), a [flawless ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Ruby "Skyrim:Flawless Ruby"), a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"), an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), and a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond").

## Related Quests

- **[The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken")**: Meet Amaund Motierre inside [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") and learn who he wants assassinated.
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.

### The Silence Has Been Broken

Motierre in the tomb

When met at [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") during the quest, Motierre will greet you upon sight:

:   *"By the almighty Divines. You've come. You've actually come. This dreadful Black Sacrament thing... it worked."*

You will be presented with three dialogue options:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **The Night Mother heard your pleas, Motierre.** | *"Yes, um.... So it would seem. Well, I won't waste your time. I would like to arrange a contract. Several, actually. I daresay, the work I'm offering has more significance than anything your organization has experienced in, well, centuries."* |
| **You have opened the door to darkness, little man.** | *"Oh, I know. I know. But I'm so glad you're here. Please, allow me to state my business. Surely your time is as valuable as my own. I would like to arrange a contract. Several, actually. I daresay, the most important work your organization has had in, well... centuries."* |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"Right, then. You prefer to listen, is that it? Well, you must represent the Dark Brotherhood. I certainly wasn't expecting anyone else. So I'll cut to the chase. I would like to arrange a contract. Several, actually. I daresay, the most important work your organization has had in, well... centuries."* |

All will lead to:

:   **Go on.**
:   *"As I said, I want you to kill several people. You'll find the targets, as well as their manners of elimination, quite varied. I'm sure someone of your disposition will probably even find it enjoyable. But you should know that these killings are but a means to an end. For they pave the way to the most important target. The real reason I'm speaking with a cutthroat in the bowels of this detestable crypt. For I seek the assassination of... ...the Emperor."*

Once again, you will have three responses to choose from:

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **Leaders rise and fall. Business is business.** | *"Oh, wonderful. You don't know how happy I am to hear you say that. So much has led to this day. So much planning, and maneuvering. It's as if the very stars have finally aligned. But I digress. Here, take these to your, um... superior. Rexus. The items."* |
| **You want us to kill... the Emperor? Of Tamriel?** | *"That is correct. What I ask is no small thing, of course. But you represent the Dark Brotherhood. This is... what you do? No? You must understand. So much has led to this day. So much planning, and maneuvering. Now, it's as if the very stars have finally aligned. But I digress. Here, take these. They need to be delivered to your, um... superior. Rexus. The items."* |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"It's a shocking request, I know. But it is inside the purview of what you Dark Brotherhood types do. Isn't it? If history is to be believed? You must understand. So much has led to this day. So much planning, and maneuvering. Now you're here, as if the very stars have finally aligned. But I digress. Here, let me give you these. They are to be delivered to your, um... superior. Rexus. The items."* |

Regardless of how you choose to respond, Amaund will end with:

:   *"Rexus will now give you two items which must be passed along to your superior. The [sealed letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre%27s_Sealed_Letter "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre's Sealed Letter") will explain everything that needs to be done. The amulet is quite valuable - you can use it to pay for any and all expenses."*

If approached again:

:   *"Is there... something else you need?"*

:   **Who are you, Motierre? Who are you, really?**
:   *"I performed the Black Sacrament, contacted you people, because I thought you guaranteed discretion. Is this no longer so?"*

:   **Why do this? Why have the Emperor assassinated?**
:   *"In the year 3E 41, Emperor Pelagius Septim was murdered in the Temple of the One in the Imperial City. Cut down by a Dark Brotherhood assassin. His killing ushered in, shall we say, a necessary change in Imperial policy. There are those now who wish for a similar change. I am sorry, but that's all I'm at liberty to say."*

:   **We'll require... significant compensation. Can you pay the price?**
:   *"Oh, my furtive friend. When Emperor Titus Mede II lies dead, there will be gold... a fortune in gold. But so much more! It is said that the Dark Brotherhood, in recent years, has been in decline. That you lack the power, wealth, and respect of days past. Is it not so? If you do this, if you kill the Emperor... Oh, how the masses will fear and respect you."*

:   **This is a complex contract. I need more details.**
:   *"The logistics of such an endeavor will be staggering, I know. There will be several minor assassinations necessary. Leading up to the... main target. As I mentioned, the amulet I gave you is exceptionally valuable, and will certainly cover the costs of all these other unpleasantries. The sealed letter explains everything else, in detail. It should be delivered to your superior. Whomever that may be."*

:   **You do realize this is treason...**
:   *"You think I don't know that? If anyone learned of this meeting, my corpse would swing over Solitude for a decade! But what I ask of you... it must be done. There is too much at stake."*

:   **You can trust your servant to keep this secret?**
:   *"Oh, Rexus is no mere servant. He has been with the Motierre family since I was a child. I trust the man with my life."*

### Hail Sithis!

When spoken to after [the attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate") on the [Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary"), Amaund will be shocked to see you:

:   *"What is it? I said I didn't wish to... be disturbed."*
:   **We have unfinished business, Motierre. / Sithis is due a soul. Wouldn't you agree? / (Remain silent)**
:   *"By the gods. You... you're alive! But I had heard... your Sanctuary... Please! You mustn't think I had anything to do with that! I wanted the Emperor dead! The true Emperor! I still do! It was [Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro")! He..."*
:   **The Emperor. The real Emperor. Where is he?**
:   *"You mean, after all that's transpired, the Dark Brotherhood will still... honor the contract? Why, this is astounding news! Wonderful news! The Emperor is still in Skyrim, but not for long. He's onboard his ship, the [Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah"), moored offshore in the [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") Inlet. But you must hurry! If you can get onboard that ship. Kill Titus Mede II, as contracted... I will reveal the location of the dead drop that holds your payment."*
:   **Commander Maro. Where is he?**
:   *"Ah, yes, I can imagine you'd want to settle that score. Last I heard he was at the Solitude Docks, conducting the Emperor's departure."*
:   **This ship, the Katariah. How will I get onboard?**
:   *"Well, I don't know. It's in the Solitude Inlet - that's the channel just north of the docks. I suppose you should go to the docks and... swim?"*
:   **What kind of security should I expect?**
:   *"Surely you're joking? This is the true Emperor, not some half-Septim lookalike. He'll be surrounded by elite bodyguards, I'm sure. You'll have your work cut out for you. Still... everyone assumes the Dark Brotherhood has been completely destroyed. They may be a bit more lax than usual."*

As you leave he will say:

:   *"Please, make haste. The Emperor's ship won't stay moored forever. We won't get a chance like this again."*

If approached again:

:   *"Don't you have all the information you need? Please, the Emperor isn't going to kill himself. Hmph. Now wouldn't that be a blessing..."*

Amaund will be very pleased once the contract is complete:

:   *"Aha! You're back!"*
:   **Titus Mede II lies dead.**
:   *"I know! I know! I received the news not moments ago! Ha ha! This is glorious! My friend, you may not realize it, but you have served the Empire, indeed all of Tamriel, in ways you cannot possibly imagine. Ah, but you care little for politics, am I right? You want money! And money you shall have! Your payment waits for you at a dead drop. It is inside an urn, in the very chamber where we first met, in Volunruud. Now please, go. Collect your money, and let us never look upon one another again. Our business, thank the gods, is concluded."*

When spoken to again, he will be bothered:

:   *"Your payment awaits. And don't worry, I'm not stupid enough to betray you."*
:   **Actually, Motierre, there is one more thing...**
:   *"And what might that be?"*

You can choose to continue with one of three options:

:   **Just a favor... for an honorable man.**
:   *"You assassins and your riddles. It really does get very annoying, you know. Now if you'll excuse me..."*
:   **Today is the luckiest day of your life.**
:   *"Ha! Well, I certainly do feel that way. Now, if, um... you'll get going?"*
:   **(Remain silent)**
:   *"Yes? No? Nothing? Very well, then. If you'll just... get going now..."*

Whichever your reply, Motierre will dismiss you with:

:   *"Oh, for the love of Mara, would you please just go?"*

After this point, he will remain in the Bannered Mare for the duration of the Hail Sithis! quest. Once the quest is complete, he will leave Skyrim for good. If you decide to kill him instead as the Emperor requested, he will say as he dies:

:   *"But... we had a deal..."*

## Notes

- He is voiced by [Alexander Brandon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Brandon "wikipedia:Alexander Brandon").
- If you ask [Babette](/wiki/Skyrim:Babette "Skyrim:Babette") about your contract during [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken"), she will say *"The man you need to speak with, his name is Motierre? That's a very old and powerful Breton family, firmly established in Cyrodiil. Most curious..."* One member of this family, [Francois Motierre](/wiki/Oblivion:Francois_Motierre "Oblivion:Francois Motierre"), was part of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Oblivion:Dark_Brotherhood "Oblivion:Dark Brotherhood") questline in [Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion") and another, [Mirabelle Motierre](/wiki/Online:Mirabelle_Motierre "Online:Mirabelle Motierre"), was part of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Online:Dark_Brotherhood "Online:Dark Brotherhood") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").
- You can kill Amaund—either through your own volition or as the Emperor's last wish—in order to claim a small amount of gems, worth a considerable amount of money.
- There are two different versions of Amaund Motierre:
  - The version found in Volunruud during [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken") has a baseID of `0003b43a` and a refID of `0003b43b`. He has tied long hair with no beard.
  - The version at The Bannered Mare has a baseID of `0004e64f` and a refID of `0004fa2f`. This one looks slightly more unkempt and haggard, as he is starting to grow a beard and his hair is shorter and not as finely groomed.

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [New Gnisis Cornerclub Services](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub_Services "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub Services"); [TownWindhelmFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownWindhelmFaction "Skyrim:TownWindhelmFaction"); [WindhelmCornerclubInnkeeperFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WindhelmCornerclubInnkeeperFaction "Skyrim:WindhelmCornerclubInnkeeperFaction") | | |

Ambarys Rendar working at the New Gnisis Cornerclub

**Ambarys Rendar** is the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") innkeeper at the [New Gnisis Cornerclub](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Gnisis_Cornerclub "Skyrim:New Gnisis Cornerclub") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). A true supporter of the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), Ambarys flies several Imperial banners on the second floor of the Cornerclub, and keeps a set of [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"). He despises the [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") population of the city, a hatred he will frequently vocalize. He runs the cornerclub with the assistance of his employee, [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil"), who shares his hatred of the Nords. He traveled to the city as a refugee during the [Red Year](/wiki/Lore:Red_Year "Lore:Red Year"), but did not realize the hostile reaction the local Nords would have to the Dunmer refugees. He intends to return to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") as soon as he has the money to do so.

Ambarys will work at the cornerclub for all of the hours of the day. He will never sleep or deviate from his work.

Ambarys wears a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes"). He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") to defend himself. Besides that, he carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

Nords visiting the New Gnisis Cornerclub will not get a warm welcome from Ambarys. He will sarcastically say:

:   *"Oh splendid, another Nord."*
:   *"Come slumming to the Gray Quarter, have you?"*

He will have a much kinder comment for Dunmer customers:

:   *"Welcome, brother/sister. Please, enjoy yourself."*

He will also insult the Nord population at large with the claim that:

:   *"It's not the cold of Skyrim that gets to me. It's the stink from the people."*

Ambarys might also vocalize his plans to leave Windhelm behind him for his homeland:

:   *"When I've made enough money, I'm going to return to Morrowind in high style."*

He will make remarks relating to the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") about whoever controls Windhelm. While [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") holds the city, he will say:

:   *"Things have been a lot worse around here since Ulfric took over."*

If the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") defeats the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and seize Windhelm he will instead have a much cheerier outlook on the situation:

:   *"At long last, Windhelm is free. No longer must we suffer persecution at the hands of Ulfric Stormcloak."*

When asked for rumors, he may point you to [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino").

:   **Heard any rumors lately?**
:   *"I was walking by the old Aretino Residence, heard the little boy, Aventus? He was chanting. It was the Black Sacrament, I tell ya."*

He will also give his personal view about magic, should he be asked about it:

:   **Where can I learn more about magic?**
:   *"[The College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") is the only place in Skyrim open-minded enough to teach magic.
    Although [Ulfric's court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving") has been known to take on apprentices once in a while."*

When ending a conversation with Ambarys, he will tell you to talk to him again if you require a drink:

:   *"If you need another drink, I'll be right here."*

He will also invite you to spend some time at the bar with the remark:

:   *"Have a seat, there should be plenty of space."*

During [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") he might make a remark about how he does not care for the women who have died:

:   *"Apparently some Nord women were murdered. Not sure why I should care."*
:   **There have been murders in Windhelm?**
:   *"None of that matters to me. Until someone takes a Dunmer, I let Windhelm deal with its own problems."*

You can also ask him about how the Dunmer are treated in Windhelm.

:   **How are the dark elves treated in Windhelm?**
:   *"Well you see where we have to live. This forgotten alley. All the filth from the upper quarters flows downhill, like they say.
    Good luck getting one of the guards to help with anything.
    I tried to get Ulfric to even come down here to see the squalor, but the High Lord of His Mightiness couldn't find the time."*
:   **Why are there so many dark elves here?**
:   *"Where else would we be?
    When the Red Mountain burned, you could scarcely breathe in Morrowind. So we came west.
    Windhelm is the first city on that road, and here we are. If we had known the Nords would be so unwelcoming, we may have kept walking."*

One of Suvaris Atheron's brothers, [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron"), will mention that he respects Ambarys. When you ask [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") why he does not return to Morrowind, he will say that Ambarys is one of a few reasons that he stays.

### Conversations

Ambarys harassing Suvaris

Ambarys Rendar will occasionally pester [Suvaris Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Suvaris_Atheron "Skyrim:Suvaris Atheron") about her work for the Nords. He might ask her about her work for the Cruel-Seas, despite her working for the Shatter-Shields (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

:   **Ambarys:** *"What's new with the Cruel-Seas*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, Suvaris? Have they given you one of those helmets with the horns on them yet?"*
:   **Suvaris:** *"What do you want from me? I work for them ok? We're not friends. They pay me, and I get the job done. That's it."*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Touchy. Maybe some Dunmer lives in you yet."*
:   **Suvaris:** *"Either pour another drink or keep moving, Ambarys."*

Ambarys will also ask Suvaris if she finds it belittling working for a Nord family:

:   **Ambarys:** *"Don't you ever find it demeaning, working for that Nord family?"*
:   **Suvaris:** *"Look, Ambarys, I just came here for a drink. I don't need any trouble."*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Fine, then. I guess some Dunmer are content to be their pets."*
:   **Suvaris:** *"Here's what's going to happen. I'm going to pretend I didn't hear that, and you're going to leave me alone. Deal?"*

[Scouts-Many-Marshes](/wiki/Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes "Skyrim:Scouts-Many-Marshes") was originally supposed to visit the cornerclub, but his schedule never has him go there. While there, he could have held two conversations with Ambarys. One in which Scouts-Many-Marshes asks Ambarys about his opinion on the Nords:

:   **Marshes:** *"Why do the Nords bother you so much, Ambarys?"*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Why do you even need to ask? They treat your people as bad as they do mine."*
:   **Marshes:** *"I think that's just their way. The Nords don't like anybody who's not a Nord, but they're not bad people, deep down."*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Look around you. Don't you know what their little war is about? They want all non-Nords out of Skyrim. That means you and me."*
:   **Marshes:** *"Oh, I doubt that very much. Who would load their ships, then?"*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Just you wait and see."*

And another where Ambarys asks how much he is paid:

:   **Ambarys:** *"How much do they pay you per day?"*
:   **Marshes:** *"That's really none of your business..."*
:   **Ambarys:** *"How much?"*
:   **Marshes:** *"Eight septims per day, plus lodging."*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Eight septims for breaking your back, and then you live in squalor. How much is your dignity worth?"*
:   **Marshes:** *"If it's all the same to you, Scouts-Many-Marshes prefers to eat and drink in peace."*
:   **Ambarys:** *"Sorry, my scaly friend, you've come to the wrong place. Around here we don't ignore what's happening in the world."*

## Bugs

- Ambarys will claim that Suvaris works for the Cruel-Seas, despite her not working for them. This line of dialogue either confuses the Cruel-Seas for the Shatter-Shields or it confuses Suvaris for [Idesa Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Idesa_Sadri "Skyrim:Idesa Sadri"), a Dunmer in the employ of the Cruel-Seas.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.

- Ambarys will continue to talk about how Ulfric will not come to see the plight of the Dunmer and Argonians even if the Empire has retaken Windhelm and Ulfric is dead. **?**

# Skyrim:Amber and Madness Smithing

## Overview

Arcane Blacksmith's site

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Investigate the area north of [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch").
2. Kill [Evethra](/wiki/Skyrim:Evethra "Skyrim:Evethra").
3. Read [Evethra's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Evethra%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Evethra's Journal").

## Detailed Walkthrough

After defeating [Thoron](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoron "Skyrim:Thoron") for [Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order") (or by sneaking to avoid his detection while he is still alive), you can loot the items on his work table. The note *[Note on Amber and Madness Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_Amber_and_Madness_Ore "Skyrim:Note on Amber and Madness Ore")* will give you a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") to investigate the area north of Mistwatch.

Travel to Mistwatch, a tower just east of the Atronach Stone. In the geyser fields just north of the tower, you'll find a stone altar and the camp of the mad blacksmith [Evethra](/wiki/Skyrim:Evethra "Skyrim:Evethra"). Approach her and the objective will update to "Kill Evethra". Do so, then loot [her journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Evethra%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Evethra's Journal") along with the unique [Arcane Blacksmith's Apron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Blacksmith%27s_Apron "Skyrim:Arcane Blacksmith's Apron").

Read the journal to complete the quest and gain the ability to craft Amber/Madness items using the [Glass Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Smithing "Skyrim:Glass Smithing") and [Ebony Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Smithing "Skyrim:Ebony Smithing") perks respectively.

## Notes

- The [Shadowrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend "Skyrim:Shadowrend") [creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") takes place to the west in close proximity to this quest's location.
- Due to the large number of hostiles in the area, Evethra may leave her camp to fight [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"), [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"), or a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). She is marked [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") until you receive the objective to kill her, but can be difficult to locate because of this.
- Although when you read the journal there is a message "You can now create new equipment with Glass Smithing" and a similar one for Ebony Smithing, to forge the new items you need to use the "Misc" section of the menu, not the Glass or Ebony section.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_MiscQuest_AmberMadnessGear stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_MiscQuest_AmberMadnessGear`.

# Skyrim:Amren's House

## Overview

Amren's House

**Amren's House** is a residence in the Wind District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), located next to [Uthgerd's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Uthgerd%27s_House "Skyrim:Uthgerd's House") and across from the [House of Clan Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:House_of_Clan_Battle-Born "Skyrim:House of Clan Battle-Born"). It is the home of [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren"), his wife [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir"), and their daughter [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[One-handed (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "One-handed (Common)")  [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith")  [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir") |

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Amren's House

Saffir enjoying her reading time

Entering leads directly into a large room with a round wooden table and a couple of chairs with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and cheese on top of the table. Beside this is a flight of wooden stairs against the northeast wall leading up to a partially-floored upper floor. On your right is a cupboard, a [fish barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel"), and a food sack. On the cupboard's shelves are three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). If you have already completed the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)") to recover Amren's [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_Family_Sword "Skyrim:Amren's Family Sword"), this will also be found on a shelf. On top of the cupboard is a bottle of wine and loaf of bread, while on the fish barrel is a bowl containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage").

Under the stairs are more food sacks and a barrel, and in the eastern corner of the room is a small table and chairs with a bottle of wine and [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on top. Above the table are three [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") and four bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") hanging from a rack. In the middle of the southeast wall is a large fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front and a bottle of wine on the mantelpiece. Coming out from the middle of the southwest wall is a large double bed with an end table to the left holding a copy of *[Nords Arise!](/wiki/Skyrim:Nords_Arise! "Skyrim:Nords Arise!")* To the right of the bed is a dresser containing [fine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and common [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and a food sack on top. Climbing the stairs leads to [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith")'s sleeping area, with a single bed at the end, an end table to the right, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing leveled items at the foot of the bed. On the end table is a copy of *[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:The Holds of Skyrim")*.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Amren's House") to which is carried by Amren and Saffir.
- There is  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the left of the door near the ground due to Amren's high proficiency using [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons").
  - Due to the plants added in front of the house in the Special Edition, this shadowmark is no longer visible.
- After [returning Amren's family sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits)#Amren.27s_Family_Sword "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)"), all low level items in the house become free to take, and both beds become usable.

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionWhiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun"); [Favor204QuestGiverFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:Favor204QuestGiverFaction "Skyrim:Favor204QuestGiverFaction"); [One-Handed Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Trainer "Skyrim:One-Handed Trainer"); [Skill Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Trainer "Skyrim:Skill Trainer"); [TownWhiterunFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction "Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction"); [Whiterun Amren's House Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Amren%27s_House_Faction "Skyrim:Whiterun Amren's House Faction") | | |

Amren in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")

*"I just need to hire one, maybe two good men."*

**Amren** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerOneHandedJourneyman "Skyrim:TrainerOneHandedJourneyman") and the common [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") for [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"). He and his wife, [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir"), have a daughter named [Braith](/wiki/Skyrim:Braith "Skyrim:Braith"). They live in their [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") in the Wind District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

While his wife spends much of her time reading and his daughter bullies [Lars Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Lars_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Lars Battle-Born"), Amren patrols the streets of Whiterun, rarely sleeping. He begins patrolling at 2am and keeps going until he enters the house in the evening, at 7pm. He then spends four hours with the family, either eating, sleeping or wandering around. At 11pm he goes to the [Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman") for a few drinks before it is time to patrol again. On Tirdas and Turdas he breaks off from his normal routine at 10am and spends four hours inside [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"), either eating or wandering about. If Whiterun is attacked as part of the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), he will participate in rebuilding the city every day between 8am and 11am.

Amren wears [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor") and [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and has a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") equipped. He carries the [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Amren's House"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Quest-Related Events

Asking him about the argument he had with Saffir:

:   **What were you two arguing about?**
:   *"My Saffir doesn't like that I've been spending so much time looking for my father's old sword. He fed his entire family with the gold he made using that weapon. I'm not about to let it gather dust in some thief's trophy room."*

You can then offer to help or not:

:   **Do you need help finding the sword?**

    :   *"I tracked it to a group of bandits nearby. But I'm no fool. I'd need the Whiterun guards or maybe hire the Companions to get it. I don't know why I'm saying this, but if you find it out in your travels, I'd be grateful to you."*

:   **Sorry to hear that.**

    :   *"Not your concern, anyway."*

If spoken to again before finding his sword:

:   *"If you find that sword, please bring it to me."*

When you return with the sword, he will be happy:

:   **I have your sword.**
:   *"You found it? I've been looking for that blade for months. You took on all those bandits yourself? Thank you. Here, my father had a favorite sword and shield technique. Let me teach it to you, in honor of his memory."*

He will then provide one-point bonuses to your [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") and One-handed skills, then be on his way.

## Dialogue

When you approach him, he will make quite a few statements:

:   *"You tried mercenary work? It might suit you."*
:   *"Sometimes I miss the soldier's life, but when I hold my daughter in my arms, I know I made the right choice."*
:   *"My wife's a good woman. She can be a little hard-headed sometimes, but I love her just the same."*

If Saffir is dead:

:   *"My wife was a good woman. She could be a little hard-headed sometimes, but I loved her just the same. Gods I miss her."*

You can also ask the obvious question that he is not from Skyrim, which will make him answer, depending on your race. If you are a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") he will say:

:   **You're not from Skyrim, are you?**
:   *"Hmph. No, friend, that I'm not. But I get along with your kind well enough."*

If you are a Redguard, he was supposed to respond with the following, but doesn't due to a [bug](#Bugs):

:   *"Ha! And neither are you, eh? Good to see another Redguard. I like to think we bring a little heat to this frozen wasteland."*

If you are any other [race](/wiki/Skyrim:Races "Skyrim:Races") you will get:

:   *"No, I'm not. Looks like we've got something in common, then."*

In all three cases, he will continue with:

:   *"No, I'm a Redguard. My family hails from the Imperial Province. Ah, but I left home when I was just a lad. Been wandering ever since."*

If asked for training, he will reply, *"I can teach you a few things."*

## Conversations

The first time you enter Whiterun, you will find Amren and his wife outside [House Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane"), heftily debating Amren's priorities:

:   **Saffir**: *"I know your family's honor is important to you, but we can't afford it!"*
:   **Amren**: *"It took me weeks to find that thieves' den. I can't stop now, and I can't get the sword on my own."*
:   **Saffir**: *"So you're willing to starve your wife and daughter to reclaim some rusty old sword?"*
:   **Amren**: *"I just need to hire one, maybe two good men. You won't starve."*
:   **Saffir**:*" I'll put it plainly. You can claim your sword, or you can keep your wife. If you set foot outside the gate, I won't be here when you return."*
:   **Amren**: *"Saffir! Wait... I...."*

When he sets foot inside his house, his daughter Braith will often try to talk to him, hoping for some parental guidance:

:   **Braith**: *"Papa, the next time you go away, I want to come with you."*
:   **Amren**: *"When I go away, I go to war. That's no place for a little girl."*
:   **Braith**: *"Every knight needs a squire. I could help you with your sword, things like that."*
:   **Amren**: *"Nice try, blossom, but I'm not a knight, I'm a mercenary. The answer's still no. Besides, your mother would miss you too much."*
:   **Braith**: *"Yeah. Right."*

:   **Braith**: *"Papa, I want to talk to you..."*
:   **Amren**: *"Hmm? What about?"*
:   **Braith**: *"Well, there's this boy, and..."*
:   **Amren**: *"Listen, Braith... Why don't you talk to your mother about this, okay? There's a good girl."*

If Saffir is dead, Amren's last response during the above conversation will be different:

:   **Amren**: *"I wish your mother were still alive. She could answer you much better. Let me think on it and we'll talk later."*

## Notes

- Amren also appears in the card expansion *[Heroes of Skyrim](/wiki/Legends:Heroes_of_Skyrim "Legends:Heroes of Skyrim")* for *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")* as the card [Battlefield Scrounger](/wiki/Legends:Battlefield Scrounger).

## Bugs

- When asked the question "You're not from Skyrim, are you?", he is supposed to have three different dialogue responses, depending on your race. However, for the Redguard-specific dialogue, the game mistakenly checks if your race is Nord. Due to this, Redguard players will not have the correct dialogue option.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Amren has no sleep package, making it impossible for him to do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo") |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | [Leveled Gold](#Reward), Kharjo as a follower |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo")) |
| ID: | FreeformCaravansA |

Moon Amulet

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
2. Retrieve the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet").
3. Return to Kharjo.

### A Stolen Treasure

Kharjo is a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") caravan guard traveling with [Ahkari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahkari "Skyrim:Ahkari"). Due to the roving nature of his occupation he can be difficult to track down, but keep in mind that Ahkari's caravan makes stops just outside of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

When speaking to Kharjo, he will remark that the caravan was ambushed by a group of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). Normally, the Khajiit are able to scare away this type of nuisance, but this time the bandits made off with his [heirloom amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet"). The amulet was given to him by his mother when he was a cub, and is the only thing to keep him warm in this cold land. When you tell him that you will retrieve it for him, he is appreciative of your desire to help, but will also say that it is not enough to lose your life over. He will then send you to the [randomly determined](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") bandit hideout.

### Find the Amulet

This is a list of possible locations for the Amulet:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Solstheim](/wiki/Dragonborn:Solstheim "Dragonborn:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout") [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave") [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") | [Bilegulch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Bilegulch_Mine "Skyrim:Bilegulch Mine") [Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep") [Embershard Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Embershard_Mine "Skyrim:Embershard Mine") [Knifepoint Ridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Knifepoint_Ridge "Skyrim:Knifepoint Ridge") | [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") | [Orotheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Orotheim "Skyrim:Orotheim") [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") | [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt") | [Broken Helm Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow") [Faldar's Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldar%27s_Tooth "Skyrim:Faldar's Tooth") [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower") [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch") | [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp") [Redoran's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat") [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") [Valtheim Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Keep "Skyrim:Valtheim Keep") [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch") | [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") | [Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow") [Damphall Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Damphall_Mine "Skyrim:Damphall Mine") [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House") |

Acquiring the amulet will involve visiting the hideout in question. Track down, and either slay or sneak past its bandit inhabitants to take the amulet from the boss chest at the end of the dungeon. Return to Kharjo, but be aware that he may have moved or could be on the road while you are looking for him.

### Your Reward

Once you find him, Kharjo will be most pleased to have the Moon Amulet again. He will give you a leveled amount of gold and becomes a potential [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 400 |
| 10–19 | 600 |
| 20–29 | 800 |
| 30–39 | 1,000 |
| 40+ | 1,200 |

## Notes

- When looking for Kharjo, a good strategy is to simply use the "Wait" function outside of one of the cities where his caravan stops until he arrives.
- The Moon Amulet can be safely pickpocketed, looted, or traded from Kharjo after the quest.

## Bugs

- If the quest directs you to [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto"), [Cracked Tusk Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_Tusk_Keep "Skyrim:Cracked Tusk Keep"), or [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt"), check to see if you have already visited these locations on your map. These locations do not respawn, so if you have been there before, the Amulet cannot spawn there and you cannot complete the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, addresses this issue. However, there are reports that the bug may still occur even with the fix.
  - You will need to reload a previous save to get a different location from Kharjo.

## Quest Stages

| 20 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformCaravansA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformCaravansA`.

The Amulet of Bats and Amulet of The Gargoyle

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri").
2. Retrieve both of the Amulets of Night Power.
3. Return to Feran.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Talk to [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri") in [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") and he will tell you of two amulets which will augment your powers as a [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord"). He will direct you to two random locations, one containing the [Amulet of Bats](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Bats "Skyrim:Amulet of Bats") and the other containing the [Amulet of The Gargoyle](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_The_Gargoyle "Skyrim:Amulet of The Gargoyle"). The amulet may be in possession of a boss or in the chest at the end of a dungeon. Head to the two dungeons shown on your map, retrieve the amulets, and return to Feran, who will give you several [potions of blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Blood "Skyrim:Potion of Blood") as a reward.

## Notes

- It appears that two additional amulets, the [Amulet of Draining Grip](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Draining_Grip "Skyrim:Amulet of Draining Grip") and the [Amulet of Drain Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Drain_Magicka "Skyrim:Amulet of Drain Magicka"), may have been planned for this quest, but were later abandoned.

## Bugs

- Since the quest may choose a random corpse to place an amulet, it's sometimes possible for the corpse to have already vanished, leaving you stuck with a quest marker pointing to an empty location on the floor.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RV09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV09`.
