# Skyrim:An Axe to Find

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve an [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") |
| Location(s): | [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| Reward: | [Ancient Nordic Pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") **or** Leveled Gold |
| ID: | DLC2RR03Intro |

[Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") wants to prove a point

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
2. Retrieve his [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") from [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").
3. Return to Glover Mallory.

### That Foolish Old Man

The blacksmith of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory"), has plenty of problems, both with his affiliation with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and his messy [family affairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Paid_in_Full#One_Last_Thing "Skyrim:Paid in Full"). Additionally, he's got a problem with an eighty year old ex-miner who borrowed his [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe") and forgot to give it back. Locate Glover Mallory near his smithy in the center of town and he will ask, *"You haven't seen  [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius") have you? That foolish old man's taken my pickaxe again!"* He will then explain that it's not an ordinary pickaxe, but a rarity in [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). Since Glover has some shady business going on he will refuse to call the guards and will tell you, *"Um, I prefer to handle these things on my own. Look, if you see Crescius, tell him to give me that pickaxe back and I'll pay you for the trouble."* You can then ask what the pickaxe is good for and he will readily explain that it's the only tool able to crack [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") and that he traded that pickaxe with residents from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

### The Damn Fool

Seek out Crescius Caerellius. If you have yet to finish [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") you can find him around the clock inside [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") and you will have to initiate said quest before he will discuss the pickaxe. Otherwise, he will have returned to his daily routine and can be found either at home or in the mine. When you mention the pickaxe, he will immediately say, *"The damn fool doesn't even deserve to have it! The pickaxe was made for mining, not selling. I'll bet he stole it from the Skaal in the first place."*

Note: If you already have an Ancient Nordic Pickaxe in your inventory, you may not be able to open any dialogue with Crescius about it, preventing you from advancing the quest. If this happens, simply drop, store or sell the one in your inventory until after you have gotten beyond the above dialogue with him.

Once Crescius has enabled the dialogue about the pickaxe and responded to your inquiry as outlined above, you will have three reply options available, and the reward will differ depending on your decision:

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Result |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| *"It doesn't belong to you."* | *"Oh, very well. Here. Tell him I hope he drops the thing on his foot."* | | | | Return to Glover Mallory with the axe. |
| *"Fine, you keep it."* | *"Now you're finally talking some sense. A mining tool belongs in a mining family. Just tell him I lost it or something."* | | | | Return to Glover Mallory and lie. |
| *"Let me think about this."* | *"Good. Now let me get back to what I was doing."* | | | | Nothing. |

### The Two Rewards

If you chose the first option, return to Glover and tell him you have his pickaxe, which he will then let you keep as a reward: *"So you finally tracked down old Crescius, eh? Quite a character, isn't he. Tell you what. Since you went through all the trouble of finding it for me and all, you keep it."* He will then tell you why: *"I just wanted to remind that codger you can't just go around taking things from other people. Now that you've delivered the message, I'm satisfied. Besides, that pickaxe hasn't done me any good in years. Maybe you can put it to good use."* If you chose the second option, he will be quite bitter about the whole thing but will still hand you a leveled amount of gold: *"Blast! That careless old fool. Well, thanks for trying anyway. Here you go... for your trouble."*

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Notes

- The quest name is a play on the phrase "[ax to grind](http://wiktionary.org/wiki/ax_to_grind "wiktionary:ax to grind")".
- The Ancient Nordic Pickaxe you gain access to during this quest has a unique base ID ([xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")0206F2).
- Although Glover lets you keep the pickaxe as a reward for finishing the quest, you can choose not to return the pickaxe and keep it that way instead. It will remain in your inventory as a quest item, making it a useful, weightless pickaxe.
- If you return the pickaxe, Glover explains that he only wanted to teach Crescuis a lesson that stealing is wrong. This, however, is ironic due to his own connections with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- If you haven't triggered the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") beforehand, talking to Crescius will start it, making it unavoidable.
- If you let Crescius keep the pickaxe, you'll need to either buy one from [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") in the [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") or find one as random treasure on Solstheim before you can mine Stalhrim.

## Bugs

- Despite its unique base ID, the Ancient Nordic Pickaxe Crescius gives you during this quest cannot be upgraded at a grindstone.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, addresses this issue. It can now be improved with an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot").
- If you let Crescius keep the pickaxe but then pickpocket it from him later before the quest is finished, the objective to lie to Glover Mallory will be stuck in your journal forever.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| 25 |  | *Objective 30:* Tell Glover Mallory lie *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* about the Ancient Nordic Pickaxe |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RR03Intro stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RR03Intro`.

# Skyrim:An enemy's gratitude

## Overview

| ID: | WIKill04 |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Kill an NPC.
2. Receive a letter from a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier").
3. *(Conditional)* Visit the letter's sender for a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When you kill a person, it is possible you will be given a message from a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") from that person's enemy, claiming that they hated the person too and are glad you took care of them. If the [relationship](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") between the enemy and the victim was foe or worse, the person thanking you will request that you visit them for a reward through a [reward letter](/wiki/Skyrim:WIKill04RewardLetter "Skyrim:WIKill04RewardLetter"). Otherwise, they'll just send you a [letter of thanks](/wiki/Skyrim:WIKill04ThanksLetter "Skyrim:WIKill04ThanksLetter").

The reward is 50 gold for each [relationship rank](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition#Relationship_Rank "Skyrim:Disposition") below zero.

## Notes

- Rich enemies were supposed to give a reward of 200 gold per rank, but no NPCs in the game are flagged as rich.
- Version 4.3.7 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch") changes the letter's font to the handwritten font.

## Bugs

- It is possible for the Dragonborn to receive a letter from themselves, rendering it impossible to complete the quest normally.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=28980))
- It is possible for the person giving the reward to be killed and thus cause the quest to get stuck because you can no longer collect.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.4, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=29128))
- If the relationship between enemy and victim is -3 (enemy) or worse, the reward letter will be delivered, but the objective to collect the reward will not be given.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If letter is placed on a bookshelf may become blank and render the reward unobtainable.
- It's possible to get the letter even if you killed the enemy "in disguise", such as being transformed into a Werewolf or Vampire Lord, where NPCs aren't supposed to recognize you. **?**

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIKill04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIKill04`.

# Skyrim:Ancano

## Overview

Ancano

**Ancano** is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [elemental mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageElemental "Skyrim:CombatMageElemental") and an agent of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). He resides at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), where he serves as an "advisor" to the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren"). The College community demonstrates a palpable mistrust toward him due to his Thalmor allegiance. As the College quest line unfolds, it becomes increasingly clear that Ancano is involved in a sinister plot on behalf of the Thalmor; and that the discovery of a strange orb underneath [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal") is key to some ominous scheme.

While he claims to be the Thalmor advisor for Arch-Mage [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren"), Ancano seems to show up everywhere except consulting to the Arch-Mage. He spends all of his time inside the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"), carefully listening to everything that is going on. When he is not busy with his many [quest-related actions](#Quest-Related_Events), he sleeps in his room on the ground floor of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") between midnight and 4am.

He wears [Thalmor robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Robes "Skyrim:Thalmor Robes") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Boots "Skyrim:Thalmor Boots") and [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Gloves "Skyrim:Thalmor Gloves"). He knows a huge number of spells. From the school of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") he knows [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), [Incinerate](/wiki/Skyrim:Incinerate "Skyrim:Incinerate"), and [Thunderbolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Thunderbolt "Skyrim:Thunderbolt"). From the school of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") he knows [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), [Grand Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Grand Healing"), [Greater Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Greater_Ward "Skyrim:Greater Ward"), and [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward"). Lastly, he knows the [Conjure Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Frost Atronach") spell.

## Related Quests

- **[Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books")**: Find the books needed to identify the artifact found in [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal").
- **[Good Intentions](/wiki/Skyrim:Good_Intentions "Skyrim:Good Intentions")**: Find and consult the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
- **[Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen")**: Learn the location of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").
- **[The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus")**: Reclaim the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") and contain the Eye.

## Dialogue

He is unpleasant and patronizing and will greet you with a threat:

:   *"Another new Apprentice, I see. Are you of the sort that believe you're here to change the world? Or are you only in it for yourself? I assure you that I shall be watching you -- all of you -- very closely."*

At all other times, he will look at you in disgust and say:

:   *"I have many important things on my mind. Your concerns are not among them."*
:   *"Are you quite sure we need to be speaking?"*
:   *"I'm disappointed to say I've learned little during my time here."*
:   *"I had hoped your scholars would be on a level comparable with my own colleagues. They are not."*

He will, however, answer a few basic questions. On the Thalmor, he will say:

:   **I'd like to know more about the Thalmor.**
:   *"Now that [stability](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat") has been established between the [Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion") and the [Empire](/wiki/Lore:Empire "Lore:Empire"), we seek only to help Skyrim. To guide its people through this time of transition, to help lead them to a better future."*

:   **What is it you do here?**
:   *"I am an advisor to the Arch-Mage. The Thalmor wish to promote relations with your College. I am at the Arch-Mage's disposal if he requires advice."*

    :   **Does the Arch-Mage often ask for advice?**
    :   *"Perhaps not as often as he should. In time, I believe he will be more trusting."*

### First Lessons

*"The Arch-Mage has my thanks."*

After you have been led into College grounds by [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") during the quest [First Lessons](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Lessons "Skyrim:First Lessons"), you will witness a heated debate between Ancano and Master Wizard [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") in the courtyard:

**Mirabelle**: *"I believe I've made myself rather clear."*
**Ancano**: *"Yes of course. I'm simply trying to understand the reasoning behind the decision."*
**Mirabelle**: *"You may be used to the Empire bowing to your every whim, but I'm afraid you'll find the Thalmor receive no such treatment here. You are a guest of the College, here at the pleasure of the Arch-Mage. I hope you appreciate the opportunity."*
**Ancano**: *"Yes, of course. The Arch-Mage has my thanks."*
**Mirabelle**: *"Very good. Then we're done here."*

If approached, Ancano will then address you directly about the event:

:   *"Your superior and I were simply having a... discussion about my level of access to the College."*

:   :   **Your discussion sounded like an argument to me.**
    :   *"Well, perhaps that is why you're merely an Apprentice here."*

:   :   **Is there some kind of problem?**
    :   *"Nothing you need to concern yourself with. I shall be quite capable of observing everything that goes on here."*

Mirabelle Ervine will also occasionally walk up to Ancano at random times and curtly address him:

**Mirabelle**: *"I've had yet another complaint. Please stop barging in on experiments in progress."*
**Ancano**: *"My dear, I am merely observing the proceedings."*
**Mirabelle**: *"Well then 'observe' from a greater distance. You're making people uncomfortable."*

### Hitting the Books

*"You there. I have questions for you."*

After you return from [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal") and report to [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") about the strange Orb, thus starting the quest [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books"), [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") will seek you out to issue a warning about Ancano. After this warning, you can confront Ancano with the rumors floating through the College:

:   **There's a rumor that you're spying for the Thalmor.**
:   *"What? Preposterous, and just the sort of thing I would expect from mages who have nothing better to do with their time. I have made it quite clear that my only role here is as an advisor to the Arch-Mage. I would suggest that you not further spread this rumor."*

Faralda will prove to have been right when she told you she thought Ancano was looking for you: As soon as you have talked to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") about the missing books, Ancano will suddenly appear right behind you in the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") and start interrogating you about Saarthal:

:   *"You there. I have questions for you. You were in Saarthal, yes? It has come to my attention that something was found there."*

:   :   **Maybe...**
    :   *"I know full well that you have. Please do not insult my intelligence. Tolfdir is still there now, is he? I shall expect a full report when he returns."*

:   :   **Yes, we did. I just informed the Arch-Mage.**
    :   *"I am well aware. Tolfdir is still in Saarthal, is he? I shall be expecting a full report from him when he returns."*

Either leads to:

:   **How do you know anything about this?**
:   *"It is my job to know these things. My role as advisor to the Arch-Mage is aided by knowing everything that transpires here."*
:   **Why does this matter to you?**
:   *"Something was discovered in Saarthal that was significant enough that Tolfdir sent a new member of the College, alone, to deliver word. That sounds precisely like the sort of thing that should matter to everyone. Especially me. Thank you for your help. You may go now."*

He'll then leave you alone to take care of the rest of [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books").

### Good Intentions

*"I'm afraid I must intrude."*

The plot thickens as you are told to talk to Tolfdir, who will wander around the Orb in a fascinated state, rambling on. Before long, Ancano will show up and interrupt, causing a brief conversation with an insulted Tolfdir:

**Ancano**: *"I'm afraid I must intrude. It is urgent that I speak with your associate immediately."*
**Tolfdir**: *"Now, I... This is most inappropriate! We are involved in serious research here!"*
**Ancano**: *"Yes, I've no doubt of its gravity. This, however, is a matter that cannot wait."*
**Tolfdir**: *"Well, I'm quite sure I've never been interrupted like this before... the audacity!... I suppose we'll continue this at some later time, when we can avoid interruptions."*

While Tolfdir walks away, Ancano turns to you:

:   *"I need you to come with me immediately. Let's go."*
:   **I don't understand what's going on.**
:   *"Really? Well, allow me to clarify the situation. I'd like to know why there's someone claiming to be from the [Psijic Order](/wiki/Lore:Psijic_Order "Lore:Psijic Order") here in the College. More importantly, I'd like to know why he's asking for you specifically. So we're going to go have a little chat with him, and find out exactly what it is he wants."*
:   **Why are you so concerned about this?**
:   *"I'll be the one asking the questions. All you need to know is that the Psijic Order is a rogue organization, believing themselves to be above the law. They have clashed with the [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion") before, and I have no intention of allowing that to happen here."*
:   **Aren't you just an advisor here?**
:   *"Technically, that is true. But I still report to the Aldmeri Dominion, and I cannot ignore this situation. Don't worry, you can return to your petty squabbles and meaningless 'research' as soon as this matter is resolved."*

He then turns around and you will have no choice but to follow him towards the Arch-Mage's Quarters. On the way, he will instruct you:

:   *"Now, you are going to speak to this... Monk... and find out why he is here, and then he will be removed from College grounds."*
:   **What do you want me to say to this monk?**
:   *"Find out why he's here, and what he wants."*

Inside the [Arch-Mage's quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arch-Mage%27s_Quarters "Skyrim:Arch-Mage's Quarters"), Psijic Order member [Quaranir](/wiki/Skyrim:Quaranir "Skyrim:Quaranir") will quickly outsmart Ancano by appearing to cause time to slow, inside of which only you and he can talk. Quaranir will warn you emphatically about the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus") and how it will affect the College. He will also relate that his presence has caused suspicion, especially in Ancano. He will also explain why Ancano is suspicious about his presence if asked if he can be trusted. After telling you to go see the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain"), you will be returned to your own world and a confused Ancano will engage in conversation with Quaranir:

*"What? What trickery is this?"*

**Ancano**: *"Well? What is the meaning of this?"*
**Quaranir**: *"I'm sorry, I'm afraid I don't understand."*
**Ancano**: *"Don't play coy. You asked to see a specific member of the College. Here he/she is. Now what is it that you want?"*
**Quaranir**: *"There's been a misunderstanding. Clearly I should not be here. I shall simply take my leave."*
**Ancano**: *"What? What trickery is this? You're not going anywhere until I find out what you're up to!"*
**Quaranir**: *"I am not 'up to' anything. I apologize if I have offended in any way."*
**Ancano**: *"We will see about this..."*

Quaranir will then leave the College and Ancano will return to the Eye of Magnus. If confronted, he'll state:

:   *"I'm not sure what just happened but I assure you I will get to the bottom of it."*
:   **Get to the bottom of what?**
:   *"Whatever it is those Psijics are up to. They cannot be trusted. For all we know, he's here to scout out the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). I'm sure they want to undermine our efforts."*
:   **What efforts would they be undermining?**
:   *"This! This... Orb. The Eye of Magnus, whatever you want to call it. It's clearly powerful, and no doubt they want it for themselves! I expect to be informed if they make any future attempts to contact you."*

:   **Have you ever heard of the Augur of Dunlain?**
:   *"The what? No. No, I'm quite sure I have no idea what you're talking about. I suggest you mind your own business and return to whatever it is you do here."*

### Revealing the Unseen

Ancano and the [Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Lore:Eye_of_Magnus "Lore:Eye of Magnus")

*"Ancano! Stop this at once! I command you!"*

When you return from [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft") during the final stages of [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen"), you will find that both Quaranir and Augur of Dunlain's premonitions will come to pass: Ancano will finally consume himself in pursuit of power and knowledge. Under the influence of The Eye of Magnus, he will invoke a ward spell sealing off the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"). You will find Arch-Mage [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") and [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") excitedly discussing the barrier:

**Mirabelle**: *"I don't know. It's like a ward, but who's casting it? Ancano? How?"*
**Savos**: *"I don't care what it is, I want it down now! I want to know what he's doing in there!"*

When you approach the Arch-Mage and ask what is going on, he will respond: *"Ancano. He's in there, doing... something. We don't know what. We're trying to get in now. I will have his head for this, I assure you. Help take this down, will you? We're throwing everything we can at it."* When the barrier's down, Mirabelle will then rush into the room along with Savos, and if spoken to will enlist your help: *"We need to find out what Ancano's up to."* When you reach Ancano, he will be joined with the Eye of Magnus by some kind of spell, and will be invincible at this point. Savos, however, will try and take him on:

**Mirabelle**: *"What's going on?"*
**Savos**: *"Ancano! Stop this at once! I command you!"*
**Mirabelle**: *"Don't go near him!"*

When Savos Aren slowly approaches the possessed Thalmor, a sudden explosion from the Eye will turn everything white and knock you out. When you come to your senses, you will find Mirabelle leaned against a wall, seemingly hurt by the explosion. She will explain what happened: *"Ancano is doing something with that thing... the Eye. We can't stop him! I haven't seen Savos since the explosion. He must've been blown clear, and he may be injured. I need you to find the Arch-Mage, and I need you to do it quickly. Get moving!"* Ancano will now be completely immersed in some kind of magical field crackling about the Eye, and you can catch only glimpses of him through this.

### The Eye of Magnus

*"I am beyond your pathetic attempts at magic."*

When you return from Labyrinthian with [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus"), the entire College will be covered by the strange ward spell from the Eye. Tolfdir will meet you on the bridge with the sad news that Ancano's actions have claimed a second victim, [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") who died attempting to foil Ancano's catastrophic scheme. When you have used the Staff of Magnus to break down the barrier, Ancano will shout:

:   *"You've come for me, have you?, You think I don't know what you're up to? You think I can't destroy you? The power to unmake the world at my fingertips, and you think you can do anything about it?"*

When Tolfdir casts a spell on him that shows no effect, he'll proclaim:

:   *"I am beyond your pathetic attempts at magic. You cannot touch me."*

Tolfdir will tell you to use the staff on the Eye, after which Ancano will exclaim:

:   *"Enough!"*

Then he'll paralyze the Master Wizard and continue:

:   *"Still you persist? Very well. Come then. See what I can do now."*

With this the Eye will open up to release its full power. Ancano will attack you and you will have to use the staff to remove the source of his power by shutting down the Eye. Ancano will defy you throughout the battle:

:   *"You dare approach me here? Are you mad? You cannot hope to defeat me!"*
:   *"You dare challenge me?"*
:   *"No! You will not deny me this!"*
:   *"No! The Eye is mine!"*
:   *"You cannot take this away from me!"*
:   *"I cannot be defeated!"*
:   *"I will end you!"*
:   *"Die, insect!"*
:   *"My power is supreme!"*
:   *"Die, worm!"*

If you try to hide from him, he'll exclaim:

:   *"Now you die!"*
:   *"You cannot escape!"*

If you cause him to panic and flee, he'll yell:

:   *"Damn it, no more!"*

As his health depletes, Ancano will desperately yell:

:   *"No..."*
:   *"Noooo...."*

## Rumors

Mirabelle is not the only person at the College who displays suspicion or dislike toward Ancano. You may hear the following comments:
**[Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon")**: *"I know I don't like the way he looks at me. I can't tell if he expects me to blow myself up, or to try and murder him. But he clearly doesn't trust any of us."*
**[Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund")**: *"I know he's from the Thalmor, and that he claims to be here simply as an advisor. I also know that no one really believes that. I've been trying to avoid him, honestly."*
**[Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane")**: *"He's asked far, far too many questions about my research. I think the Thalmor are trying to steal my work! I haven't told him anything, of course. What I'm doing is far too important. Can't breathe a word of it."*
**[Nirya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirya "Skyrim:Nirya")**: *"Don't trust that one. He's up to something. Most here are up to something, of course, but in his case, it's not good. I haven't figured it out yet, but I will. He is rather handsome though, isn't he?"*

## Notes

- Ancano is voiced by musician [Alexander Brandon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Brandon "wikipedia:Alexander Brandon") ([IMDb](http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0999472/ "imdbname:0999472")).
- Be careful when using [Dead Thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Thrall "Skyrim:Dead Thrall") on Ancano past level 40, since he keeps leveling up with you past that (up to Level 50) even in death. From that point on, Ancano's corpse will resist Dead Thrall.
- Ancano may be hostile toward minions summoned using the [Bone Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Forge "Skyrim:Bone Forge")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall "Skyrim:Gallows Hall").[*verification needed*]
- Ancano also [appears](/wiki/Legends:Ancano "Legends:Ancano") in the [Heroes of Skyrim](/wiki/Legends:Heroes_of_Skyrim "Legends:Heroes of Skyrim") card expansion for *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*.
- You can attack Ancano openly without fear of hostilities from the other College members, though he himself may become hostile and retaliate. Since he is essential until the final quest of the College's main questline, he can be used to grind skills and leveling.
- If you do not want to talk to Ancano during "Hitting the Books", you can paralyze him (via spell, the [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") shout, or an arrow tipped with a paralysis poison) or ragdoll him with the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") or [Cyclone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyclone "Skyrim:Cyclone") shouts and escape through the side door to the roof. When you complete the quest and come back, he will act as if nothing happened and the questline proceeds as normal.
- Ancano will resort to unarmed combat if he runs out of magicka for his spells. Even if there is a weapon nearby (on the ground or on a corpse), he will not pick it up and use it.

## Bugs

- Ancano won't become hostile if you hit him even though he will show up on the compass as an enemy upon being hit.
- You will not be kicked out of the college if you attack him.
- Arrows pass straight through Ancano's head as if it weren't there. Unlike shots to any other part of his body, head shots do not inflict damage.
- Ancano's special ability is never active because it was set to the wrong archetype.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

Ancarion

**Ancarion**, a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Wizard_(class) "Skyrim:Thalmor Wizard (class)"), is the leader of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"). He is attempting to locate a source of [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") for the Thalmor. The [Stalhrim Source map](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source_Map "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source Map") can be pickpocketed from him, taken from his dead body, or given to you by him in order to complete the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim").

## Related Quests

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
- **[Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sell_Stalhrim_Armor_and_Weapons_to_Ancarion "Skyrim:Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion")**: Sell [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") equipment to Ancarion.

### A New Source of Stalhrim

His greetings:

:   *"You are interfering with official Thalmor business. You will leave immediately if you value your well-being."*
:   *"Meddle in our affairs, and your end will be swift and painful."*
:   *"Get out of here, before I lose my patience."*
:   *"Leave at once! Do not test me, or I promise that you will regret it."*

Speaking to him:

:   **I'm here about the Stalhrim map.**
:   *"So you know my purpose here, then? I suppose you must have found that dullard of a blacksmith. Unfortunately for you, my mission here is also a secret. To protect it, I have no choice but to silence you. Now, give me one good reason that I should not kill you where you stand."*

Three options are available. Note that successfully completing the third option and starting the [hidden quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Sell_Stalhrim_Armor_and_Weapons_to_Ancarion "Skyrim:Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion") requires a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of at least 75.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **The blacksmith won't talk. You're wasting your time.** **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"I admit, we are not making the progress I'd hoped. Perhaps you are right, this venture might be more trouble than it's worth. Very well, you have convinced me. We will depart the island shortly and seek our weapons elsewhere."* **Failed**: *"You dare to question me? That insult will be your last!"* | | | | **Passed**: Gives map to player. **Failed**: Attacks player. |
| **Leave this island now, or your life is forfeit.** **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"I can see that is no idle threat. Very well, we will depart the island once we have loaded the ship. No weapon is worth dying for, not even a weapon forged from Stalhrim. Here, give this map to the blacksmith. I have no further need of it."* **Failed**: *"You dare threaten me? For that insolence, I will flay the flesh from your bones!"* | | | | **Passed**: Gives map to player. **Failed**: Attacks player. |
| **You want Stalhrim weapons, and I think I can help you get them.** *Ancarion:* *"Here to make me an offer, then? Very well, what do you have in mind?"* *Player:* **The smith said he'd teach me how to make Stalhrim weapons.** *Ancarion:* *"And you will sell them to me. I suppose I'll have to give you the map first?"* *Player:* **Yes, otherwise he'll teach me nothing. You can trust me.** **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"I might not trust you, but I will trust your greed. Very well, take the map. Return here with Stalhrim weapons and armor, and I will pay you a fair price for them. Tell the blacksmith whatever lie you will. We have no further need of him."* **Failed**: *"You expect me to just hand you the map, so you can deliver it to the blacksmith and laugh at the foolish Thalmor you so easily outwitted? You have made a grave miscalculation, and now you will pay the price!"* | | | | **Passed**: [New Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Sell_Stalhrim_Armor_and_Weapons_to_Ancarion "Skyrim:Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion") **Failed**: Attacks Player |

Whatever result you gain from negotiation with Ancarion you will always end up with the [Stalhrim Source map](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source_Map "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source Map") in hand.

### Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion

His greetings:

:   *"Back with more Stalhrim items, I trust?"*
:   *"Unless you have more Stalhrim weapons and armor for me, we have nothing to talk about."*
:   *"Ready to do more business?"*

Speaking to him:

:   **Shall we do some business?**
:   *"What do you have for me?"*

His goodbyes:

:   *"You have kept up your end of the bargain nicely. I admit, I wasn't sure that you would."*
:   *"I'll be here when you have more Stalhrim weapons and armor."*
:   *"There is more coin if you wish to claim it. You know what I want."*
:   *"Do not think we are now friends. I have tolerated you, nothing more."*
:   *"You are alive only at my pleasure. Do not forget that."*
:   *"I am done with you. Go on, get out of my sight."*
:   *"Nothing more to sell me?"*
:   *"I was hoping you'd have more."*
:   *"Is that all?"*

## Spells

Ancarion knows the following spells:

[Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")
:   [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh")

[Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")
:   [Banish Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Banish_Daedra "Skyrim:Banish Daedra"), [Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Expel Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Expel_Daedra "Skyrim:Expel Daedra")

[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")
:   [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Incinerate](/wiki/Skyrim:Incinerate "Skyrim:Incinerate"), [Thunderbolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Thunderbolt "Skyrim:Thunderbolt")

[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")
:   [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward"), [Turn Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Undead_(spell) "Skyrim:Turn Undead (spell)")

## Gallery

- 

  Ancarion's ship at the dock.

## Notes

- Ancarion does not have unique facial data. Instead, he uses the default male High Elf face.

## Bugs

- Ancarion is unaffected by the [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader") perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- If you kill Ancarion after agreeing to sell Stalhrim items to him, the quest objective is never removed.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Ancestor Glade

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Ancestor Glade

The **Ancestor Glade** is a small glade in a cavern east-southeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It contains only one zone, *[Ancestor Glade](#Ancestor_Glade)*.

The glade is one of several on [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") and the only one in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). It is so named for being home to swarms of [ancestor moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Moth "Skyrim:Ancestor Moth"), and is the only location where such moths can be found. It also features the rare [yellow mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Yellow Mountain Flower"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, the waters of the glade are home to the rare [angelfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Angelfish "Skyrim:Angelfish")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"), [pygmy sunfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Pygmy_Sunfish "Skyrim:Pygmy Sunfish")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"), and [spadefish](/wiki/Skyrim:Spadefish "Skyrim:Spadefish")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"). The cavern is central to the quest [Unseen Visions](/wiki/Skyrim:Unseen_Visions "Skyrim:Unseen Visions"), although it can be visited at any time.

## Related Quests

- **[Unseen Visions](/wiki/Skyrim:Unseen_Visions "Skyrim:Unseen Visions")**: Perform a ceremony to read the Elder Scroll.

### Exterior

The entrance is high in the mountains, above the snowline east of Falkreath, south of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). A few paces to the northeast of the entrance, behind a large rock, is an old campsite complete with an extinguished campfire, with two pots hanging over it. One contains a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and the other a [venison chop](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop"). Beside the campfire are an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt"), a [snow bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Bear Pelt"), a dead [ice wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), an unowned bedroll, and a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Everything in and around the campsite is marked as owned and, as such, taking anything is considered stealing, although you can skin the dead ice wolf without committing a [crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime").

### Ancestor Glade

The entrance descends into an overgrown passage that leads to a dead end. Another path on the left follows the wall, leads you across a fallen tree, and then into another short tunnel opening up to the main glade. If you have not yet started the quest Unseen Visions, you'll be ambushed by three [spriggan earth mothers](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Earth_Mother "Skyrim:Spriggan Earth Mother") in the first area of the cavern, regardless of your level. During the quest, there is a wooden gate that will close behind you as you enter the main glade, to prevent you leaving prematurely. There are many piles of rocks, all found against the outer walls of the main glade, which have items of treasure on top. The items can easily fall off, so it's worth scouring the ground nearby and downhill from them if an item is missing.

The following harvestable plants can be found in the area. [Hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") is entirely within the initial cavern, while most other plants are found within the glade itself. (Note: this is one of the areas that was targeted for extra plants in Skyrim Special Edition, so the counts are much higher in that version of the game and are listed separately from the counts for the original game.)

| Ingredient | Original | SE |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") | 9 | 17 |
| [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") | 8 | 8 |
| [Hanging Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") | 18 | 18 |
| [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") | 11 | 11 |
| [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") | 5 | 18 |
| [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 5 | 20 |
| [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") | 6 | 6 |
| [Yellow Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Yellow Mountain Flower")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | 27 | 55 |

Ancestor Glade interior

There are five Canticle trees found within the glade, which appear as trees covered with white and pink blossoms. During the quest, they can be harvested for their [bark](/wiki/Skyrim:Canticle_Bark "Skyrim:Canticle Bark"). Before the bark can be harvested, you will require the [draw knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Draw_Knife "Skyrim:Draw Knife"), which is found by following the path from the entrance to the main glade as it descends several flights of stairs. At the bottom, a path passes under several square arches formed by a flat stone being placed atop two upright stones a few paces apart. In the center of an island surrounded by hot springs and shallow water is a strange stone shrine, with the knife in the center. It is only obtainable during the quest. One of the Canticle trees and several yellow mountain flowers are nearby.

Another Canticle tree can be found by following the outer wall to the left of the entrance to the main glade. Continuing past this, you will find a large pile of rocks against the outer wall with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") and leveled [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") on top. Back from the entrance, following the outer wall to the right, you will come to another pile of rocks with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top. Continue following the wall down to the western corner of the glade and on yet another pile of rocks is a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") or random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") and random enchanted [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). Follow the stream toward the springs until you reach the shrine. From there, the stairs to the southwest lead up, curving to the southeast before coming to a flat, stone landing. Turn southwest just before the landing, passing across several more heated springs, to the third Canticle tree. To the west of it is a pile of rocks with a random enchanted [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") on top.

Ancestor Glade interior

Return to the landing and follow the stairs and path to the east as they curve northeast, bringing you to another Canticle tree. Following the outer wall beyond this tree, you will find a pile of rocks with a random bow on top. From the fourth tree, there is a path to the southwest just left of the one you got here by. This one leads upwards past a pile of rocks topped with a filled random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") in a holder. On a lower rock are four loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst") and a [silver jeweled necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Jeweled_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Jeweled Necklace"). Beyond these is a spring coming out from under the outer wall before dropping over the edge and forming the largest waterfall in the glade. Across the stream is the fifth and final Canticle tree. Just past this, concealed by a fir tree, is a final pile of rocks where you will find a random enchanted helmet and a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"). You will be above the first turning of the stairs, with a short drop from here.

Treasure found within

There are multiple swarms of ancestor moths all around the area, as well as a few gatherings that land on the flora around the glade. The former can only be interacted with during the quest, while the latter you are able to harvest like other insects for their [wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Ancestor Moth Wing") for use in [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"). Near the first tree, to the left of the entrance, are the most that can be caught individually, either landing on flora or flying on their own between patches of flowers.

Once you've collected the knife, harvested the bark and attracted seven swarms of ancient moths, you will need to enter the beam of light near the shrine in order to read the [Elder Scroll of Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll_(Blood) "Skyrim:Elder Scroll (Blood)"). After reading the Elder Scroll, you will be attacked by a leveled group of either [Dawnguard soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") including an [armored troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Armored_Troll "Skyrim:Armored Troll"), or [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") including [vampire's thralls](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall"), depending on your chosen side. These enemies will continue to respawn every few days, like any other dungeon inhabitant. They spawn in a group of five to six at the foot of the stairs leading into the glade.

## Notes

- It is highly recommended that you save before entering the glade, especially during Unseen Visions, due to the number of reported [bugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Unseen_Visions#Bugs "Skyrim:Unseen Visions") relating to the quest.
- During Unseen Visions, the glade is unoccupied. However, enemies from the opposing faction arrive in the glade as soon as Unseen Visions ends.
- This location contains the most (and only non-quest-locked) yellow mountain flowers, and the only place in the game for gathering ancestor moth wings.
- The Draw Knife does not appear in its holder if the *Dawnguard* quest has not been initiated. Attempting to harvest bark from the trees will have the game telling you that "you lack the proper item".
- If you use [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") while the moths are following you, the moths will become ethereal as well.
- The music that plays inside is environmental music instead of cave music.

## Bugs

- You may only find the ancestor moth swarms but no ancestor moths that you can catch, leaving you unable to collect any ancestor moth wings.
- During Unseen Visions, the vampire or Dawnguard attackers who get enabled are never disabled again after the quest is over. This leads to some of them respawning here later when they aren't supposed to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The location name, parent location, and worldspace map marker settings for Ancestor Glade may be missing.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Ancestral Worship

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his [aunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his [ancestral barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb") |
| Reward: | [Hillgrund's Tomb Crypt Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb_Crypt_Key "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb Crypt Key"), leveled [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), Golldir as a follower |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir")) |
| ID: | dunHillgrundsTombQST |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

[Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") attacking the [defiler](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") of his ancestral tomb

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") outside [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").
2. Accompany him as he tries to rescue his aunt [Agna](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") from [Vals Veran](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran").
3. Find a way into the room where Vals Veran is hiding.
4. Kill Vals Veran.
5. \**(Optional)* Protect Golldir.

### Necromancer in the Barrow

Within the antechamber of [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb"), you'll encounter a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") named [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir"). He explains that a necromancer named [Vals Veran](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") is inside his ancestral barrow, defiling it. His aunt [Agna](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") went in to put a stop to this, but Golldir was too scared to go with her. If pressed, he will explain that he has been terrified of the barrow ever since his father locked him in it as a child. If you accept, he will accompany you into the barrow to help rescue his aunt and kill Veran.

### Rescuing Agna

The tomb is very linear and any offshoots are only small, dead-end rooms. As you continue down the stairs, [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") will attack in small waves. Several varieties will be present in each wave. Like all normal barrows, exploration into the burial sites will lead to more attacks as entombed draugr come to life. Golldir may raise a vocal objection to you looting his ancestors, but concedes to allowing it since you are helping him. There is no chance of successfully rescuing Aunt Agna; at the bottom of the room you'll find her corpse. The door to the burial chamber where Veran is located is barred shut.

### Reaching Vals Veran

With more resolve, Golldir will lead you through the abandoned section of the barrow to find a secret way into the chamber where Veran is hiding. This section is full of his disgraced ancestors and the draugr numbers are larger here. Stronger varieties of draugr are entombed in the walls, but should only appear singly. After passing through a room with a single spider ambush, a simple puzzle will present itself. Before you leave the spider room look for a Sanctified Mace behind the web on the left of the room. In order to pass the puzzle the plaque with a bear on it must be located. A chain hanging from that plaque will open a secret door that leads to the main chamber.

### Confronting Vals Veran

If you've had problems up until now, this next area may prove very troublesome. The room is a large tiered burial chamber with sarcophagi all around. As you approach the top, Vals Veran will come out and start speaking of death's beauty. Whether you try to talk to him, attack him, or let him finish his speech, he will eventually disappear and teleport across the room. Attacking him at this juncture is futile as he will simply teleport across the room and heal. If you are quick, you can kill him with a single power attack before he teleports, but you will still need to fight off the waves of draugr. You can also kill him using a sneak attack almost as soon as you enter the room, if your [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") and [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skills are high enough—but once again, you'll still have to deal with all the draugr. A goal is also to keep Golldir alive through the battle, to earn the gold reward.

If you don't manage to kill Veran instantly, you'll need to focus instead on the waves of draugr. They can quickly swarm you and any followers while Veran casts [damaging Frost magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Damage "Skyrim:Frost Damage") from afar. The third wave of draugr will contain a boss-level draugr that must be dealt with. After dispatching it, Veran will continue to summon more draugr (but in lesser numbers), but most importantly, will stop teleporting. He can now be hunted down and killed. Golldir will thank you for your help and state that he will remain close by the tomb and spend his time hunting.

### Reward

Killing Vals Veran will grant you the [Hillgrund's Tomb Crypt Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb_Crypt_Key "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb Crypt Key"), which can be found on Veran's body. The highest reward is only granted if Golldir is kept alive. If he survives, he will give you a large leveled amount of gold and a [Hillgrund's Chest Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Chest Key"), which opens an augmented loot chest, located just beyond the main burial chamber (where the battle with Veran took place), through the door at the top of the stairs. Beyond the chest is the barred door leading to the room in which Aunt Agna's body was found. If you do not receive this key, you can loot it from Golldir's corpse or just pick the expert-leveled lock on the chest. After you exit the tomb you can speak to Golldir again (if he's alive) about becoming a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). This dialogue option will not open up until after you leave the tomb.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- If you are a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf"), Golldir will comment "*No offense, I mean...I'm sure you aren't into any of that kind of stuff*" after he speaks of Dark Elf necromancy when explaining what is going on in the tombs.
- If Golldir sees you looting items from his family tomb, he will say *"Hey! Those belong to my family! Sigh... fine, take whatever you want, so long as you help me get rid of Vals."*
- If you are having trouble dealing with the draugr swarms during the final battle, you can lure them back to the secret door and pick them off one at a time, since the draugr are unable to pass through the door.

## Bugs

- After reaching Vals Veran and after the brief dialogues between Veran and Golldir, Veran disappears with an invisibility spell but may never come back. If so, then only the initial attack from the draugr will take place. Something may trigger his appearance script again, but once again he becomes invisible forever.
- If Golldir is killed, the quest will still act as if it's active and that you can still "talk to Golldir" to finish the quest. The quest marker will even hover over his dead body.
- It is possible that Golldir may drop his war axe and shield in the battle before entering the main chamber, if a Draugr Deathlord uses the "Unrelenting Force" shout on him (or if you do accidentally). If this occurs, he will not pick them up again, even if you drop a weapon and shield in front of him, although he may pick up a different weapon in the battle with the Draugr in the main burial chamber.
- When Vals Veran teleports away he goes to a small room east of the main chamber (reachable by turning off clipping with the console). If he is killed while teleporting then his body can end up stuck there.
- The *[Note from Agna](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_from_Agna "Skyrim:Note from Agna")* says that Golldir was locked in the tomb by his brother, but in dialogue Golldir says it was his father who locked him in.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Ancestral Worship (dunHillgrundsTombQST) | | |

| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |

| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Speak with Golldir |
| 100 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 5, 15, 20, 30, 35, 36, 38, 40, 45, 50, 80, 81, 95, 101, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunHillgrundsTombQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunHillgrundsTombQST`.

Ancient Dragonborn

The **Ancient Dragonborn** will appear if your health falls below 50% when the second or third word of the [Dragon Aspect](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Aspect "Skyrim:Dragon Aspect") shout is active. He appears as an invisible man equipped in a set of spectral armor identical to the armor that you gain from using Dragon Aspect. The Ancient Dragonborn will behave like a normal follower, but cannot be interacted with and can't be talked to. Once he has killed all visible enemies within close proximity, he will disappear.

In combat, the Ancient Dragonborn will attack with a [Nord Hero Battle Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Hero_Battle_Axe "Skyrim:Nord Hero Battle Axe") and can use the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath"), [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath"), and [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [dragon shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Notes

- He cannot be attacked; magic and weapons pass straight through him.
- He can be disarmed by draugr using the Disarm shout, such as deathlords.
- There is a destruction ritual spell named "Conjure Ancients" which is not available in the game. It summons an Ancient Dragonborn, and per every 5 dragon souls an additional one is summoned.
- The Ancient Dragonborn is not affected by the Twin Souls perk meaning the player can have two summons and an Ancient Dragonborn at the same time.

# Skyrim:Ancient Ice

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Bring a murderer to justice in northern [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading *[Skjol's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjol%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skjol's Journal")* |
| Location(s): | Camp south of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"), [island](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Solstheim#Horker_Iceberg "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Solstheim") northeast of [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=28333&y=99959&zoom=16&legacy=true) |
| Reward: | Set of [Stalhrim Fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Stalhrim Fur Armor") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE057\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Stalhrim Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Stalhrim_Fur "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Stalhrim Fur") |

A Skaal has been murdered

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Skjol's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjol%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skjol's Journal")* at the camp southwest of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") near the lake by [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").
2. Journey to the [Horker Iceberg](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Solstheim#Horker_Iceberg "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Solstheim") northeast of [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing") and kill [Skjol the Tongueless](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjol_the_Tongueless "Skyrim:Skjol the Tongueless").
3. Claim the [Stalhrim Fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Stalhrim Fur Armor") for yourself.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Your icy reward

### Cold Blooded Murder

Travel to a camp south of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"), just across from [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") on the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). There you will come upon the body of a dead [Skaal villager](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Villager "Skyrim:Skaal Villager"). The murderer's name is [Skjol the Tongueless](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjol_the_Tongueless "Skyrim:Skjol the Tongueless"), as revealed by the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjol%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skjol's Journal") left at the scene of the crime. Skjol does not appear to be too bright, and killed the villager after learning the location of a [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposit north of [Castle Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag").

The deposit in question is on an [unnamed island](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Solstheim#Horker_Iceberg "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Solstheim") just northeast of [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=28333&y=99959&zoom=16&legacy=true). Usually home to angry [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"), you will instead find it to be occupied by a much angrier Skjol wielding an enchanted battleaxe. He will attack on sight, so put him down and claim the hoard for yourself: a rare deposit of [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") and a full set of [Stalhrim Fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Stalhrim Fur Armor") lying in a sarcophagus. Take the set to complete the quest; you will now begin to see Stalhrim Fur items showing up as random loot in the world.

## Notes

- The location is not on the map. To find the camp, travel north from Thirsk Mead Hall, along the lake.
- Stalhrim Fur armor uses the same model as [Stalhrim armor](/wiki/Blades:Stalhrim "Blades:Stalhrim") in *[Blades](/wiki/Blades:Blades "Blades:Blades")*.
- The island where Skjol makes his last stand can be difficult to climb onto from the water. If you use [Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Boots_of_Waterwalking "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Boots of Waterwalking"), found in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") elsewhere on Solstheim, you can attack Skjol with ranged attacks while avoiding his battleaxe, or jump from the water's surface onto the shore and avoid being attacked while in the water as you struggle to climb out.
- Stalhrim Fur Armor will appear in leveled lists once the quest has been completed, sometimes being worn by [Reaver Lords](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver_Lord "Skyrim:Reaver Lord").

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE057_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE057_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Ancient Power

## Overview

An Ancient Vampire's Head.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri").
2. Retrieve the [Ancient Vampire remains](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Vampire_Arm "Skyrim:Ancient Vampire Arm").
3. Return to Feran Sadri.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to [Feran Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Feran_Sadri "Skyrim:Feran Sadri") and he will tell you his theory that adding the blood of an ancient [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") to the [Bloodstone Chalice](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstone_Chalice "Skyrim:Bloodstone Chalice") can lengthen the amount of time its effects last. He will send you to a random location, telling you to retrieve one of five petrified [vampire parts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Vampire_Arm "Skyrim:Ancient Vampire Arm") from a boss level chest at the location, and infusing the remains' lingering magical essence into the Bloodstone Chalice.

Report back to Feran Sadri to conclude the mission, ending with him telling you the effects of the Bloodstone Chalice will last longer now.

### Reward

Drinking from the Bloodstone Chalice grants the [Blood of the Ancients](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_of_the_Ancients "Skyrim:Blood of the Ancients") ability which augments the [Vampiric Drain](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampiric_Drain "Skyrim:Vampiric Drain") spell when in Vampire Lord form to absorb stamina and magicka as well as health for one day by default.

| Body parts | Duration(see [Notes](#Notes)) |
| --- | --- |
| Default | 1 day |
| 1 | 3 days |
| 2 | 5 days |
| 3 | 7 days |
| 4 | 9 days (maximum) |

## Notes

- The same body part can be requested more than once.

## Bugs

- The in-game description of the 'Blood of the Ancients' spell is not directly linked to its duration. The duration of the spell is calculated based on the `DLC1VampireChaliceStopDay` script and affixed to a specific day, while the description shows the effectively meaningless magnitude of the spell. This means that the [Necromage](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromage_(perk) "Skyrim:Necromage (perk)") perk, which increases the magnitude and duration of spells cast on undead (such as your vampiric self), causes the description in your 'spells - active effects' menu to display that its duration is increased by 25% (which in turn is caused by the perk's effect on magnitude, not duration), but the spell actually lasts only as long as calculated by the Chalice's level (as indicated in the table above).

It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RV05`.

Ancient's Ascent

**Ancient's Ascent** is a mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") southwest of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Word wall

The route to the word wall is through [Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage"), a short cave. The word wall can also be reached by using a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") to climb the mountains around the area or on foot by approaching from [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"). There are three [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") plants to the right of the path after exiting Bonechill Passage. There are a couple wide flights of stairs leading up to a plateau in front of the word wall, with lit braziers at the bottom and top of each flight.

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the word wall will be guarded by a few leveled enemies.

After the dragons' return, the word wall will be guarded by a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"), which will attack as soon as you approach from the cave.

Regardless of whether [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, the boss chest is by the base of the platform holding the word wall.

## Notes

- Ancient's Ascent is one of the locations suggested by [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel") as a place to find [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") for her [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Cold "Skyrim:Ice Cold").
- [Climbing](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") the rocks behind the wall provides a shortcut to [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne").
