# Skyrim:Ancient Technology

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Retrieve Dwemer schematics to improve technology for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard") |
| Location(s): | Radiant |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted items; ability to craft and buy [Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") upgrades and bolts |
| ID: | DLC1RH05 |
| --- | |
| |  | | --- | | **Prerequisites:** [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") | | **← Previous** [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") | | ← Previous | [A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order") | | |

Your rewards...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Sorine Jurard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorine_Jurard "Skyrim:Sorine Jurard").
2. Travel to the target location.
3. Retrieve the requested schematics.
4. Return to Sorine.

## Detailed Walkthrough

One of the schematics

### Find the Schematic

Speak to Sorine Jurard in [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") and ask "*What can I do to help?*" to receive this quest. She will instruct you to travel to a random [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") or [bandit hideout](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps "Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit Camps") (this includes locations added by [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")) and retrieve the Dwemer schematic specifying a new [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow") design. The schematic will be located in the boss chest in the location. If it is a bandit area, the note [Dwarven Haul](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Haul "Skyrim:Dwarven Haul") will be found in the chest as well.

Once you have the schematic, return to Sorine to receive your reward of a leveled enchanted item. In addition, she will also teach you how to craft an [Enhanced Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Enhanced_Crossbow "Skyrim:Enhanced Crossbow") at a forge (as long as you possess the [Steel Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Smithing "Skyrim:Steel Smithing") perk).

This quest can be completed a further five times (six in total). In addition to a leveled enchanted item, each time Sorine will teach you how to craft a different item. After the [Enhanced Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Enhanced_Crossbow "Skyrim:Enhanced Crossbow"), these will be [Exploding Steel Bolts of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Steel_Bolt_of_Fire "Skyrim:Exploding Steel Bolt of Fire"), [Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Steel_Bolt_of_Ice "Skyrim:Exploding Steel Bolt of Ice") and [Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Steel_Bolt_of_Shock "Skyrim:Exploding Steel Bolt of Shock"). After the fifth run you will be able to craft a [Dwarven Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Crossbow "Skyrim:Dwarven Crossbow") and [Dwarven Bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Bolt "Skyrim:Dwarven Bolt") (as long as you possess the [Dwarven Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Smithing "Skyrim:Dwarven Smithing") perk), and Sorine will also begin selling [Exploding Dwarven Bolts of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Fire "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Fire"), [Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Ice "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Ice") and [Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Exploding_Dwarven_Bolt_of_Shock "Skyrim:Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Shock"). After the final run, you will be able to craft an [Enhanced Dwarven Crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Enhanced_Dwarven_Crossbow "Skyrim:Enhanced Dwarven Crossbow"). For more details on the required components for each time see [Steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Smithing "Skyrim:Steel Smithing") and [Dwarven Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Smithing "Skyrim:Dwarven Smithing").

## Notes

- This quest is not available if you sided with the Volkihar, or if you are in the Dawnguard ranks but are currently a vampire.
- With the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on, if the item happens to be found on Solstheim, there will be no quest marker. Traveling to Solstheim will make the marker appear in the relevant location.
- You cannot craft standard Steel Bolts unless you ask Sorine how to craft a crossbow, and you also cannot craft Dwarven Bolts until you have done the part of the quest where you find the Dwarven Crossbow Schematics and return them to her. You can craft both Dwarven and Steel elemental bolts of each element after you turn the schematics in for them.

## Bugs

- If you advance in the Dawnguard questline the quest marker may disappear off of the radiant location where the schematics are located. The quest marker will instead be back over Sorine's head and will remain there.
  - If you have the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on, head to Solstheim and activate the quest. This may resolve the issue.[*verification needed — Does this work for others? Worked for 2 others; failed for 2 other*]
- Rarely, after obtaining the first several upgrades, you will not be presented with the option to repeat the quest and retrieve further schematics. This may be caused by starting the quest [Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment").
  -  It is possible to manually add the missing recipes with the following console commands (which add all the recipes from exploding fire bolts onwards—only the ones that are actually missing are required):

:   :   ```
        Set DLC1TechXbowBoltsExplodingFireChanceNone to 0
        Set DLC1TechXbowBoltsExplodingIceChanceNone to 0
        Set DLC1TechXbowBoltsExplodingShockChanceNone to 0
        Set DLC1TechXbowDwarvenChanceNone to 0
        Set DLC1TechXbowDwarvenEnhancedChanceNone to 0
        ```

- You can get stuck with the "Help Sorine with her project to improve the crossbow" and the dialogue item "What can I do to help?" that gives the "Ancient Technology" doesn't appear on Sorine.
- Rarely, the schematic is not in the indicated location.
- Bandit hideouts that were picked to hold Dwarven items for the quest will continue to spawn them (minus the "Dwarven Haul" note) in the boss chest on subsequent trips to said areas, even when the Ancient Technology quests are over. **?**
- The schematic for the Enhanced Dwarven Crossbow may appear on the ground or floor next to the boss chest after the Ancient Technology quest is done and the area it was first picked up in respawns. It can be picked up, but is translucent when dropped and will fall through any piece of furniture it is placed on (such as a table). **?**
- This quest may run more than 6 times despite that fact that there are exactly 6 schematics to retrieve.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Ancient Technology (DLC1RH05) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Sorine Jurard has sent me to retrieve the <Alias=Item> from <Alias=Dungeon>. She will be able to use it to master new technology to provide to the Dawnguard members. *Objective 10:* Retrieve the <Alias=Item> from <Alias=Dungeon> |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Return to Sorine Jurard |
| 255 | ☑ | Sorine Jurard sent me to retrieve the <Alias=Item> from <Alias=Dungeon>. She will be able to use it to master new technology to provide to the Dawnguard members. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1RH05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1RH05`.

# Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve [Andurs'](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay") from the [catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") |
| Location(s): | [Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)"), [Whiterun Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Catacombs "Skyrim:Whiterun Catacombs") |
| Reward: | 15 gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 (Andurs) |
| ID: | FreeformWhiterunQuest04 |

Andurs' Amulet on the table

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs") in the Hall of the Dead.
2. Retrieve [Andurs' Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay").
3. Return the amulet to Andurs.

### His Badge of Office

[Whiterun's](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") is overseen by [Andurs](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs "Skyrim:Andurs"), priest of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"). When you first meet Andurs he will ask if you believe in Arkay and his sway over life and death. This is an opening gambit which he uses to determine how best to persuade you to retrieve his [amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay"), which he left behind in the [catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Catacombs "Skyrim:Whiterun Catacombs"). Andurs assures you that he would get it himself, however, strange noises are now coming from the catacombs and he fears the restless dead.

### The Restless Dead

Ready yourself for a fight and enter the catacombs. You will encounter a few [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), who are immune to poison and paralysis, and resistant to frost. When you move forward, quickly turn to your right, as the first skeleton stands in wait here. Dispatch it as quickly as you can, because a second skeleton, who stands at the bottom of the stairs here, will rush to its aid. After this, there is a third and final skeleton behind the closed door to the left of the entrance. If you were unable to quickly kill the first two, then it may have already detected you and emerged to try and flank you.

### Amulet of Arkay

Follow the stairs down by the second skeleton and go through the door; the amulet lies next to a wreath on the right-hand table. Before you leave, head to the base of the other set of stairs, and locate the [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") in one of the alcoves. This gem is related to the quest [No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned"). Ascend the stairs and enter the room where the third skeleton stood; a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")* can be found on one of the tables.

Return to Andurs and hand him the amulet. He will be very grateful... and reward you with 15 gold.

## Notes

- If you don't have the amulet when you speak to Andurs to return it, e.g. because it's still in the inventory of your (former) follower, you can still finish the quest. The amulet will disappear from the follower's inventory and appear in Andurs'.

## Bugs

- If you already have an Amulet of Arkay when you begin the quest, you will not be able to complete it. To avoid triggering the bug, make sure you drop any existing Amulets of Arkay before you pick up the quest version. Just complete the quest and go back to where you dropped them and pick them back up again.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.5, fixes this bug.
- Even if you finish the quest, everything in the Hall of the Dead may still be marked as owned. **?**

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformWhiterunQuest04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformWhiterunQuest04`.

# Skyrim:Andurs

## Overview

| Andurs (RefID: 0001A68D) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | | |
| House | [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001A68D | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013BA8 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 75 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 70 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech"), [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleSlyCynical](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleSlyCynical "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleSlyCynical") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionWhiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun"); [TownWhiterunFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction "Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction") | | |

Andurs

**Andurs** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay") living in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") located in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). He tasks you to find his [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay") which helps him perform the death rituals. The amulet was unfortunately dropped in the catacombs within the halls of the dead and Andurs will not go in due to strange noises.

Andurs lives a secluded existence inside the Hall and never sees the light of day. His bedroom is located in the western wing and he sleeps there every night between 8pm and 8am. After waking up he wanders about all day long until his bedtime, at times sitting down on one of the benches to relax, eat, or sleep.

Andurs wears a set of [monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Monk Robes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Andurs' Arkay Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Arkay_Amulet "Skyrim:Andurs' Arkay Amulet")**: Retrieve Andurs' [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay") from the [catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)").
- **[Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage")**: Help [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") make peace with her dead father.

## Dialogue

Andurs is quite eager when he sees you, saying:

:   *"I spend so much time among the dead, I sometimes forget how much I miss the company of the living."*

He will discuss the impact of current events on his job:

:   *"With this terrible [war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), I'm a bit overwhelmed. As are the catacombs."*

He'll also talk about his life's work:

:   *"As Whiterun's priest of Arkay, I spread his word whenever I'm able. In the meantime, most of my hours are spent with the city's dearly departed."*

When exiting conversation, he'll say one of the following:

:   *"The blessing of Arkay be upon you."*
:   *"Walk always in the light, in these days of darkness."*

### Pilgrimage

During [Pilgrimage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrimage "Skyrim:Pilgrimage"), [Alessandra](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra "Skyrim:Alessandra") will ask you to deliver her father's [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Alessandra%27s_Dagger "Skyrim:Alessandra's Dagger") to Andurs. When you bring Andurs the dagger, he'll be touched:

:   **I have Alessandra's dagger here.**
:   *"She finally decided to return it to her father. Bless her heart. I will make sure this finds its way to his tomb as soon as possible. Thank you for bringing it, my child."*

### Andurs' Arkay Amulet

When you first meet him, he'll ask you a question. No matter what option you select, you will be able to ask him what he lost.

:   *"Tell me, do you believe in mighty Arkay, god of life and death?"*

You will now have three options:

:   :   **The god of death? I know him well.**
    :   *"I'm glad to know that, because I need your help. You see, I've lost something precious."*

:   :   **The gods aren't a big part of my life.**
    :   *"I see. Well, perhaps you'll take pity on a humble priest who has lost something precious."*

:   :   **I'm not sure. Tell me about him.**
    :   *"Well, as I said, Arkay is the god of life and death. You'll find his temples and Halls of the Dead all across Tamriel. Priests of Arkay such as myself perform rites for the dead and sometimes console the bereaved. We also keep a constant vigil against those who practice the vile arts of [necromancy](/wiki/Lore:Necromancy "Lore:Necromancy"). I asked the question because I was hoping you might be able to help me recover something I've lost."*

:   :   **What did you lose?**
    :   *"My [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Andurs%27_Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Andurs' Amulet of Arkay"). It's the source of my divine powers and also a sacred badge of office. I misplaced it in the catacombs. I'd look for it, but I've been hearing noises down there. I fear the dead have become... restless. Without that amulet, I'm powerless to confront them. Would you be willing to search for it?"*

        :   **I'll find your amulet.**
        :   *"I'll just wait here and make sure nothing foul escapes the catacombs."*
        :   **You're on your own, priest.**
        :   *"So be it. I'm sure Arkay will find it in his heart to forgive you... eventually."*

Once you bring back his amulet, he'll be grateful.

:   *"Oh, thank Arkay. Please, take this gold for your troubles."*

## Unused Dialogue

An unused line of dialogue exists for Andurs. You were supposed to be able to pick up his amulet without talking to him and bring it as a surprise. However, the amulet will only spawn when he has given you the quest, so the dialogue can never be heard:

:   *"Can it be? You've brought me my amulet? Oh, thank Arkay. And thank you. Oh, dear friend, please, take this gold for your troubles."*

## Bugs

- Andurs doesn't have a Boss reference marker like the other temple priests.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Anga's Mill Common House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Anga's Mill Common House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anga%27s+Mill+Common+House)) | | |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| AngasMillCommonHouseLocation | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

The Common House

**Anga's Mill Common House** is a home in the small settlement of [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill"), located next to [Aeri's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri%27s_House "Skyrim:Aeri's House").

It is the home of the two unhappy and ever-nagging sawmill workers, [Kodrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodrir "Skyrim:Kodrir") and [Leifur](/wiki/Skyrim:Leifur "Skyrim:Leifur"). It consists of one area, *[Anga's Mill Common House](#Anga.27s_Mill_Common_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Kodrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodrir "Skyrim:Kodrir")  [Leifur](/wiki/Skyrim:Leifur "Skyrim:Leifur") |

## Exterior

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  2 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

## Anga's Mill Common House

Interior view

The front door opens to the sight of the fireplace, which holds three gold coins on the mantel and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") at its base, where Leifur often cooks in the evening. In the southwestern area sit three respawning food barrels along with a well-dressed dinner table with two loaves and one piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and one bottle of regular [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Atop one of the barrels is a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). Across from the cooking pot stands a non-respawning cupboard with clutter, with some [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") and a [pile of salt](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top. At the foot of the cupboard is a basket containing three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and a respawning food barrel.

Next to the fireplace is a kettle containing four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and another dinner table with plenty of food: three slices of [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), two potatoes, a cluster of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and three loaves of bread. Above the table hangs more food, some [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), two samples of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). There are also some game underneath the ceiling, two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). On the same wall stands a set of shelves with two bottles of wine and one of alto wine, and the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")-related book *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*. Next up are a non-respawning dresser with clothes and a small non-respawning chest with very minor loot. The dresser stands behind one of the three owned beds in the sleeping area. Next to the first bed, a non-respawning end table contains clutter and has a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") on top.

Behind the next owned bed sits a respawning food barrel and a non-respawning wardrobe with a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") on top. Opposite the wardrobe is a small table with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). In the eastern corner are another non-respawning end table with clutter, a hidden medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"), a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000330b3 "Skyrim:Hat"), and a [potion of haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"). The respawning chest at the foot of the bed contains minor loot, same as the non-respawning end table in the opposite corner. Two respawning food barrels are nearby. The end table has four gold coins on top, as well as a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Biography of the Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_the_Wolf_Queen "Skyrim:Biography of the Wolf Queen")*.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Anga%27s_Mill_Common_House "Skyrim:Key to Anga's Mill Common House") to which is carried by both Kodrir and Leifur.
- There are three respawning food barrels near the door, two to the south and one to the north. A [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") rests atop a crate on the north side.
- Leifur and Kodrir never sleep; they just return here and idle around all night, be it eating or just standing about.

# Skyrim:Anga's Mill

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Wood Mill.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Wood_Mill.png) | Wood Mill: Anga's Mill ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Anga%27s+Mill)) | | |

| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Anga's Mill

**Anga's Mill** is a small wood mill built along the north bank of the [River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim"), west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It consists of two houses and a sawmill. The mill is owned by [Aeri](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri "Skyrim:Aeri"), a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") woman who inherited the sawmill from her father who died in the Great War. A short distance along the western road is the camp where [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Ennodius Papius") lives.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Aeri](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri "Skyrim:Aeri")  [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Ennodius Papius") †  [Kodrir](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodrir "Skyrim:Kodrir")  [Leifur](/wiki/Skyrim:Leifur "Skyrim:Leifur") |

† Only during the quest [Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius").

## Related Quests

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Kill Ennodius Papius")**: Kill [Ennodius Papius](/wiki/Skyrim:Ennodius_Papius "Skyrim:Ennodius Papius").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The mill has two houses, [Aeri's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri%27s_House "Skyrim:Aeri's House") just across from the saw mill structure and [Anga's Mill Common House](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill_Common_House "Skyrim:Anga's Mill Common House") up the hill to the west.
Outside the mill, [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") range freely. There are two [wood chopping blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). There are five barrels containing food and [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). You can buy [sawn logs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") here after installing [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") by speaking to Aeri. You can also cut your own for free if she has given permission to do so.
Up the hill, two nests with [chickens' eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg")  are outside the Common House. A [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found here as well.

## Notes

- If you travel west a short distance down the road from the Mill, you will come across the tent that Ennodius Papius sleeps in during his related quest.
- There is a waterfall in the [River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim"), due west of Anga's Mill, with a dry alcove behind it. The alcove holds an adept-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a barrel containing alchemical ingredients, a lootable skeleton, two quicksilver ingots, a weapon on top of the crate, and a buried lootable chest. A third ingot is underwater a few paces downstream. Nearby there are mudcrabs, Nordic barnacle clusters and a camp. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=102440&y=30783&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- Five [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") veins can be found around the area:
  - One can be found along the bank of River Yorgrim.
  - One lies across the river, opposite the mill.
  - Two are located near Ennodius' camp; one to the south and the other to the west.
  - One can be found just northwest of Aeri's house.

## Bugs

- Part of the waterfall treasure stash may be inaccessible due to being placed behind the cliff face.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Angarvunde (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Discover the treasure of [Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Medresi Dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Medresi_Dran "Skyrim:Medresi Dran") |
| Location(s): | [Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde") |
| Reward: | [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for the Shout [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") |
| ID: | dunAngarvundeQST |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

Medresi has a task for you

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter [Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde") and speak to [Medresi Dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Medresi_Dran "Skyrim:Medresi Dran").
2. Kill three [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") in the main chamber.
3. Return to Medresi.
4. Follow Medresi.
5. Enter Angarvunde Catacombs to open the gate.
6. Enter Angarvunde Ruins to open the gate.
7. Follow Medresi into the treasure chamber.
8. Discover Angarvunde's treasure.

### Angarvunde

Upon entering [Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde"), you will encounter [Medresi Dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Medresi_Dran "Skyrim:Medresi Dran") complaining about her cowardly work force who fled as soon as they encountered some [undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead"). Until the path is clear, Medresi is unable to reach the treasure she seeks. If you offer to assist her, she will in turn offer to split the treasure with you.

First, Medresi needs the three leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") cleared from the main chamber. Head down the ramp from Medresi and follow a short corridor; the main chamber is the first large room you come across. Kill the three draugr here and make your way back to Medresi, who will be walking down towards you.

Tell her that the draugr are dead, and she will race off to the main chamber. Follow her to the locked gate at the far side of the chamber. Talk to her, and she will give you a key that will open the doors to the sides of the main chamber.

Head up the ramp on the southeast wall of the chamber and open the door to the Catacombs.

### Angarvunde Catacombs

Follow the path downwards until you reach a broken spiral staircase leading further down. Drop down here, listen to a patrolling draugr to time it when he isn't right there. There is a burial urn next to a broken chair. Follow the path still further down and you will encounter another Draugr in the wide corridor. There is also a trapped chest up the stairs to the left.

Another draugr awaits when you turn the corner to the left. There is a bookcase on your left with clutter and a burial urn. You will then encounter a group of four as you follow the corridor into the burial crypt, one is roaming and the other three are upright in alcoves asleep. There is also a locked chest and a random potion. The corridor will open out into an overgrown cavern containing a single draugr, four giant Canis Roots and an unlocked chest, behind the first Canis Root on your left as you enter you will find a Corundun vein as part of the wall. Exit this cavern to the left, in front of you is a random potion, continue following the path. Watch for the [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") on the floor halfway up the stairs, past a burial urn on your left. There is another dart trap halfway up the second set of stairs. Both traps are easily avoided by waiting for the darts to stop and neither seemed to reset. You can use the second trap to your advantage dealing with the draugr which is patrolling here.

You will emerge in yet another overgrown cavern containing two draugr. after turning the corner to the right on the top alcove of the second set of alcoves on the left is a petty soul gem, and just after this on the same side are three burial urns. Turn to the left and the last alcove on the left before the stairs is another burial urn. Half way up the stairs there are a couple more burial urns. Several draugr may awake from their slumber here, so be careful. Make your way through the next two large burial chambers and you will reach the door back to Angarvunde. Just before the door there is an urn on the right and a corner table on the left with a random potion and Wraith's Wedding Dowry book.

Head straight to the end of the corridor, past a couple of urns and an unlocked chest and pull the lever. The spikes to your left will lower, allowing you back into the main chamber and opening the first gate. Head up the stairs on the northwest side of the main chamber to access Angarvunde Ruins.

### Angarvunde Ruins

Follow the winding corridor down two flights of stairs. Directly at the foot of these stairs is a corridor containing four [trap triggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") on the floor, which will release [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") if activated. The next room contains a solitary draugr, and iron door concealing a couple of standard burial urns, and a number of paths blocked off by spikes. There is also a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* on the table. There is also a locked chest behind the table in the corner.

Continue through the only available path into a two-leveled chamber containing two draugr. Follow the upper pathway around to the right and jump across the crumbled bridge to reach a [magicka poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Magicka_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Magicka Poison") on a [pedestal](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate")—be warned, though, that this will release a [spike trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the ceiling. Heading downstairs and up the path will bring you face-to-face with yet another draugr, and eventually will lead you to the other side of one of the blocked paths encountered earlier. Pull the lever here to release two sets of spikes—one containing a locked chest, the other leading you back into the first room.

Directly opposite, you will see that the third set of spikes has also retracted. Head down the pathway they have revealed. At the foot of the stairs and round the corner to the left, there is a floor trigger for a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") overhead, and another two draugr.

Two more draugr will spring from the upright coffins on your left as you enter the next three-leveled chamber. Claim the [healing potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") between them if you wish. On the opposite side of the room there is an unlocked chest, an urn and a burial urn. Veer right and up the stairs to find a path that will bring you to the third tier of this chamber. One draugr awaits in the center of the bridge.

In the room directly beyond the bridge, there is a bookcase to the right containing some potions and leveled armor and three burial urns. Further down the stairs and along the corridor, there is also a leveled weapon, some coins, a ruby (maybe random gem) and a coin purse beneath three black statues in an alcove. Deal with the final draugr on the stairs to the right, at the top of the stairs there is another burial urn next to a brazier. The door leads back to Angarvunde. Once through the door there are a couple of burial urns, and magicka potions on your right, then walking towards the lever to lower the spikes you will pass an urn and an unlocked chest on your left.

### Medresi's End

The word wall at Angarvunde

Head left to the end of the corridor to find a chest and a lever. Pull the lever to lower the spikes to your right and open the final gate. Jump down and walk towards Medresi, who will excitedly run through the open door, only to be killed by a crushing spike trap. Luckily for you, her activation of the trap also reveals a pathway down.

The chest contains a coin purse and a broken steel sword handle. Head down the revealed stairway to find the real prize—a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for the [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout "Skyrim:Shout"), a boss-level chest, and an enchanted two-handed weapon.

## Notes

- If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), they may not follow you all the way down the spiral wood staircase within Angarvunde Catacombs. Because the staircase has broken away at the bottom, you must drop down a few feet to reach the ground below, and your follower may remain stuck on the staircase. In this case, you will be forced to clear this area alone, and your follower can be found back in the main chamber when you return to open the gate.
  - This can be solved by waiting, as all followers are loaded next to you afterwards.
  - You can also use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to push them down.
- You can tackle the Catacombs or the Ruins in either order once you receive the key from Medresi; however both levers must be activated before the final chamber can be reached.
- If Medresi Dran's body gets stuck on top of the trap, climb on top of one of the carvings with a face and jump to her, or use the unrelenting force shout to knock her off.
- Only Medresi can trigger the final trap. If you beat her to it, you and your followers cannot trigger it before she arrives. There is therefore no way to complete the dungeon without letting her die (or using console commands).

## Bugs

- If you pickpocket the key from Medresi and explore the Catacombs and Ruins sections without the relevant quest, Medresi will stand in front of the open gates, insisting that they need to be opened.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
  - To fix this, talk to Medresi so that she "gives" you the key, then re-enter both the Catacombs and Ruins by their exit doors, and re-trigger both levers.
  - Killing Medresi will also trigger the final trap and advance the quest.
- The Questmarker is on Medresi, the Journal tells you to talk to her after opening the big gate, but she still tells you that there is only one door left to open. **?**
  -  To fix this use *setstage dunAngarvundeQST 71* to advance the quest, and she will run ahead and get crushed, opening the entry for you.

## Quest Stages

| Angarvunde (dunAngarvundeQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Destroy the Draugr in Angarvunde (<Global=dunAngarvundeDraugrKilledCount>/3) |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Talk to Medresi in Angarvunde |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Find a way to open the gates |
| 61 |  | *Objective 61:* Open the other gate |
| 62 |  | *Objective 62:* Open the other gate |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Return to Medresi |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Discover the treasure of Angarvunde |
| 254 |  | *(All objectives completed)* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 30, 35, 40, 55, 56, 60, 65, 66, 71, 80, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunAngarvundeQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunAngarvundeQST`.

# Skyrim:Angarvunde

## Overview

For the quest, see [Angarvunde (quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde_(quest) "Skyrim:Angarvunde (quest)").

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Angarvunde

**Angarvunde** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains three zones: *[Angarvunde](#Angarvunde)*, *[Angarvunde Catacombs](#Angarvunde_Catacombs)*, and *[Angarvunde Ruins](#Angarvunde_Ruins)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde_(quest) "Skyrim:Angarvunde (quest)")**: Discover the treasure of Angarvunde.

### Exterior

The path leading from the road to the entrance is the natural habitat for several leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). The entrance is little more than a tunnel leading into a cave, and is marked by broken arches and fallen masonry. Outside of the entrance is a campsite, complete with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging over the blazing campfire, two unowned bedrolls next to the fire, and a barrel of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") with a lantern on top beside them. There is a wooden platform behind the fire, with a third unowned bedroll under a lean-to, and a square wooden table and chair beside it. On the table is a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")* and [Medresi's notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Medresi%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Medresi's Notes"), a journal that foreshadows the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde_(quest) "Skyrim:Angarvunde (quest)") awaiting inside the ruins.

### Angarvunde

The entrance leads directly into a narrow passage descending to the southwest. As you begin to explore, you will overhear [Medresi Dran](/wiki/Skyrim:Medresi_Dran "Skyrim:Medresi Dran") complaining, presumably about a mining crew she was to hire, mentioned in her journal, being cowards. You will encounter her at the top of some wooden scaffolding with ramps leading down to a wider passage. She will initiate a conversation with you, offering to split the treasure with you in return for clearing out the undead infesting the place. She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde_Key "Skyrim:Angarvunde Key") that is required to completely explore the ruins. Although it can be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") with a high enough skill, this can lead to difficulties (see [bugs](#Bugs)). There are numerous [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") and [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") found throughout the ruins.

From the bottom of the scaffolding, follow the passage as it takes a couple turns, before eventually leading to a room containing a broken sarcophagus and many large urns, most of which are broken. A door in the southern corner leads directly into the main chamber, where three leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") roam, including a magic-user. There are raised platforms on either side as you enter the chamber, and broken masonry and furniture all around the room. The only item of worth in this room is a single burial urn behind the first pillar on the left. There are three further exits from the room: a sequential pair of gates in the middle of the southwest wall that lead to your ultimate goal, a broken walkway on the southeast side leading up to a balcony and an iron door to *[Angarvunde Catacombs](#Angarvunde_Catacombs)*, and opposite, on the northwest side, a passage with stairs leading up to an iron door to *[Angarvunde Ruins](#Angarvunde_Ruins)*. On the raised sections at the rear are passages blocked by spears and windows looking through to shortcut exits from each of the side zones.

Dispatching the three enemies in the first room will result in Medresi catching up with you and offering the key. The key opens the doors to both zones. Levers that can only be accessed by traversing each side zone must be activated, raising the two gates to the southwest and giving access to the final chamber. Each lever opens one of the gates, and also lowers the spears to allow access back into the main chamber from the respective side area. You can explore the side zones in either order.

The word wall

Medresi waits for you to clear out both side zones in front of the two gates to the southwest. As soon as you use the second lever, Medresi rushes ahead and meets an untimely end. Her death is scripted; you can save her from the trap by sprinting to catch up and using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout, but she dies anyway. The trap she triggers is a circular section of the floor that rises and meets a section of stake-studded ceiling that lowers, killing her instantly. The chest she was rushing toward is wide open, and contains only a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and the [broken steel sword handle](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Steel_Sword_Handle "Skyrim:Broken Steel Sword Handle"). The section of floor stays in the raised position, but you can use some fallen masonry to access and loot her corpse for the few [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and other items she carried. Once that's done, inside the raised section is a flight of spiral stone stairs leading down to the true treasure room, containing the word wall, which teaches a word for the Animal Allegiance shout. In front of the wall is an unlocked boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a random enchanted weapon. When you're done, backtrack to the entrance, as there isn't a shortcut.

### Angarvunde Catacombs

Through the door are stairs descending to a short wide passageway with a cave-in at either end, and a narrower passage leading off to the southeast with a large urn in front. This turns southwest and enters a cave containing a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") with a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") by the top of a stairwell in the middle of the room, with spiral wooden stairs leading down. Below you can hear another draugr patrolling. The stairs stop a short distance above the ground, requiring you to drop and find an alternative route back out. [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") may refuse to accompany you, although they will be waiting by the spears in the main chamber.

Once you drop down, you will be faced with a leveled draugr who is patrolling up and down more stairs to the northwest. The room under the stairwell contains little of value except a burial urn by a damaged throne. At the bottom of the stairs is a second leveled draugr, who is likely to be alerted to any fighting with the first. You are actually on the other side of one of the cave-ins passed in the previous wider passage. The passage continues to the northeast, passing a short flight of stairs on the left with an apprentice-trapped chest at the top, and another cave-in behind. Opening the chest without disarming the trap will trigger [poison darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to shoot from the side walls in front of the chest. The main passage turns a short distance after the stairs, and passes a set of shelves holding a burial urn and some [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"). A magic-using draugr patrols this section of passageway.

After another turn, you can see the start of catacombs ahead, and a leveled draugr slumbering in an upright alcove. There is also another leveled draugr patrolling just out of sight, who is likely to be alerted to any fighting. In an alcove to the right of the first draugr is a burial urn with three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the ground in front. Around the corner, stairs descend to the northwest. At the bottom, you'll find another draugr in an alcove on the right. Opposite is a broken sideboard with a burial urn in front. The passage continues through to the next area and another draugr, in an alcove behind a novice-locked chest on your left. Take care, as opposite this alcove is an open doorway into a room where another leveled draugr is patrolling. To the right of the doorway is an alcove containing a random healing, magicka, or stamina potion.

The next room contains four huge [canis roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), one in each corner, an unlocked chest behind a broken pillar, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the southeast wall. The exit is to the northwest, and leads back into catacombs. Opposite is an alcove containing a random healing, magicka, or stamina potion. There are stairs leading up to the northeast, with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") partway up that triggers poison darts from the floor. There is a burial urn by a turn with more stairs, and another pressure plate and more poison darts from the floor. The traps can be used to your advantage, as the room at the top contains three leveled draugr, which at higher levels can all be deathlords and present a challenging fight. The room is full of vegetation, but holds nothing of interest, and climbs to the rear, before stairs lead up to wider catacombs with horizontal alcoves along both sides. Some of the alcoves hold dead draugr that can be looted for random [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") or minor loot, some hold burial urns, and some hold slumbering draugr. Around the first corner, an alcove on the left above one of the slumbering draugr contains an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"). Work your way through these catacombs, dealing with the draugr as you go, until you reach an iron door at the top. There is a large urn to the right, and a sideboard to the left, with a copy of *[Wraith's Wedding Dowry](/wiki/Skyrim:Wraith%27s_Wedding_Dowry "Skyrim:Wraith's Wedding Dowry")*, a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), and a random potion on top.

The door leads back to *Angarvunde*, to the room behind the spears and seen through the window. The room contains two whole large urns, an unlocked chest, and a lever that both lowers the spears allowing access back to the main chamber and also raises one of the gates to the final chamber to the southwest.

### Angarvunde Ruins

Through the door is a narrow passage that takes several turns, descending flights of stairs and passing a large urn before you reach the first of several pressure plates in the floor, each of which triggers a row of [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") to swing once in each direction. The passage leads to a room containing a draugr. There is a stone table in the middle of the room with a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* and a burial urn on top, and behind the table, against the wall, is a novice-locked chest. Three large urns are also found in the room. There are two sets of spears blocking two passages from this room to the northeast and southwest, an iron door to the northeast to the right of the blocked passage, and an open doorway to the northwest. Behind the iron door is a cave-in with two burial urns among the rubble.

To the northwest is a short passage leading to a split-level room, with a leveled draugr on a walkway opposite from where you enter. There are wooden stairs leading down in front of you to the lower level of the room. At the bottom of the room is another leveled draugr patrolling in and out of a passage to the southwest. Staying on the upper level and following it around to the right leads to the walkway the first draugr stands on. This crosses first to a pillar, then originally to a balcony on the far side of the room, but part of the walkway has collapsed; the balcony can easily be reached by jumping, however. On the balcony is a pedestal with a leveled [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") on a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") that triggers [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") to shoot from above and in front of you; to avoid damage, stand to the side, use [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"), or knock it off with a ranged spell or [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"). If the poison is accidentally knocked off, it can be difficult to find, due to the lower level being filled with vegetation, but there is nothing else of interest in the lower level.

Through the doorway to the southwest is a wide flight of stairs with a magic-using draugr patrolling backwards and forwards along the passage at the top. This passage takes a couple turns before climbing a flight of stairs up to a room behind one of the sets of spears blocking access in the first room of this area. There is a lever opposite, between two sets of spears. The lever lowers both sets here and the other set on the far side of the room. Behind the set on the left is a novice-locked chest, while the second set gives access back to the first room, and the third set back in the first room gives access to the passage to the northeast. On your right when passing back into the first room of this area is a large urn.

Beyond the spears to the northeast are three burial urns by a flight of stairs leading down. The passage turns back on itself, then turns again before opening into a wider passage. On your left is a cave-in, while to the right is an urn and a set of shelves, holding only clutter. Once past the shelves, the passage turns again, and you'll encounter a draugr patrolling the next section. By the corner is a pressure plate that triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"), which can be used to your advantage. At the far end, the passage staggers to the right, where a leveled draugr is lurking just out of sight. This draugr is normally alerted to fighting the previous draugr.

At the end is another cave-in and a doorway into a large chamber with two levels of walkways above. On the lower of these is a draugr magic-user. There are two upright sarcophagi against the left-hand wall. Upon entering, both sarcophagi will burst open and leveled draugr will emerge. There is a sideboard between the sarcophagi holding two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Health "Skyrim:Fortify Health"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Stamina "Skyrim:Fortify Stamina"), another random potion, and a dagger. In the southeastern corner is a burial urn, an urn, and an unlocked chest, while against the northeast wall, wooden stairs lead up to a balcony and the first walkway. This crosses the room before a series of stairs leads up to the higher walkway. This leads across to a room containing a set of shelves holding a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a large coin purse, and two random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina. There are also three burial urns in the room, and stairs descending to the southeast.

At the bottom is a wide passage with several opened sarcophagi lining the walls patrolled by a leveled draugr. At the other end, around the corner to the right, are several statues with a random two-handed weapon, a medium coin purse, a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), and nineteen loose septims in front of them. To the left of the statues are stairs leading up to the southwest. At the top by a lit brazier is one last burial urn, and on the left is an iron door.

The door leads back to *Angarvunde*, similar to the end of the Catacombs zone, to the room behind the spears. The room contains a broken sideboard with another two random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina, and two burial urns. Continuing into the room, you will find a large urn, an unlocked chest, and the lever that lowers the two sets of spears granting access back into the main chamber and raises one of the gates to the southwest.

## Notes

- This location is marked as cleared when the related quest is completed. Clearing the location is not triggered by killing its boss enemy, unlike most other dungeons, but rather by discovering the word wall.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, addresses this issue. It adds a draugr boss near the word wall with the scripts to mark the location as cleared.
- You can also kill Medresi as soon as you enter, which will still allow you to progress the miscellaneous objective.
- A room in *Angarvunde Catacombs* contains four giant canis roots. Most canis roots are roughly one foot tall, while these four are the size of trees and taller than you.
- There is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") southeast of the camp.
- There is a small storage area with a [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), and potions farther up the mountain south-southeast of the camp.
- The Prima guide identifies Angarvunde as a temple.
- A [dragon mound of the same name](/wiki/Online:Angarvunde_Mound "Online:Angarvunde Mound") appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- Clearing this location does not increment the number of "Dungeons Cleared" displayed in your journal, and therefore does not contribute to the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- If you pickpocket the key from Medresi instead of talking to her, she can get stuck: you can open the gates, but Medresi will refuse to go through them. In this case, you must kill her to progress.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- When chasing Medresi into the last room, the floor trap might open, immediately close again, and then remain closed, so the final room with the word wall cannot be accessed.
  - If you retreat to the main chamber and reenter the final room a second time, the floor trap may open for you.
- The room boundings for Angarvunde near the word wall may be slightly too small to prevent portions of that part of the dungeon from disappearing from the screen.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.3, fixes this bug.
- The barrel and camp may respawn despite the dungeon being classed as a "No Reset Zone". **?**
- In *Angarvunde Catacombs*, past the canis root and when you get to the resting draugr, the sound effect for the stone steps in the area seems to be the sound effect for wooden steps. **?**

Angeline Morrard

**Angeline Morrard**, a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorApothecary "Skyrim:VendorApothecary"), is the proprietor of [Angeline's Aromatics](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Angeline's Aromatics") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Her niece, [Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis") assists her in the store, and takes over ownership of the store if her aunt dies. Angeline used to sell perfumes for use in homes before the war, hence the store's name; she now caters to adventurers and soldiers.

Angeline wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#0004223b "Skyrim:Hat"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Angeline%27s_Aromatics "Skyrim:Key to Angeline's Aromatics") to her store, and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

If you ask Angeline for [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers"), she declines, saying she's just a simple herbalist, and refers you to [Lami](/wiki/Skyrim:Lami "Skyrim:Lami") in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") or [Arcadia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia "Skyrim:Arcadia") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

Angeline will ask you if you have been to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). If you tell her you have, she will [ask for news](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News") about her daughter. If you say you have no news but are willing to bring some back to her, Angeline will mention that her daughter was stationed in Whiterun after joining the [Imperial Army](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). She asks you to talk to [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") for information about her daughter.

## Related Quests

- **[No News is Good News](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News")**: Find out about the fate of Angeline Morrard's daughter from [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis").
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### No News is Good News

She can start the quest with either of these lines:

:   *"You're a traveller, correct? Have you been to Whiterun?"*
:   *"It's good to see a fresh face. You wouldn't have happen to come from Whiterun would you?"*

You can answer her question with:

:   **No, sorry. I haven't been to Whiterun before.**
:   *"Ah well, it was a long shot."*

:   **Actually, yes.**
:   *"Wonderful. I hadn't really hoped to run in to someone who had been there."*
:   **You mentioned something about Whiterun before?**
:   *"My daughter, Fura, was assigned to Whiterun after she joined the Imperial Army. I was hoping you might have met her.
    I haven't heard from her lately. I've tried talking to Captain Aldis but he hasn't been any help."*

:   :   **I'm sorry, I've never met her before.**
    :   *"Ah, well I guess it was unlikely. I'm sorry to waste your time."*

:   :   **I haven't met her, but I could try to get more information.**
    :   *"Oh that's very sweet of you. Anything you can find out from Captain Aldis would be welcome news."*

When spoken to after returning from speaking to Captain Aldis:

:   **I have some news about your daughter.**
:   *"You got Aldis to tell you something? I knew you would. What did he say?"*
:   **Angela *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*... Mrs. Morrard... your daughter is dead.**
:   *"I told her. I told her the imperial*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *army would kill her. That this was a war of Jarls and Imperial Generals and we had no part in it.
    She just wouldn't hear it.
    It was brave of you to come to me with this. I can't thank you for it, not for this, but you have done me a service."*

## Dialogue

When approached:

:   *"Ah, welcome to Angela's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Aromatics. Can I help with some herbal needs?"*
:   *"Feel free to look around. We have a fine selection of herbs here at Angela's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Aromatics."*
:   *"So, what are your needs? Perhaps a pinch of this, and a bit of that? Hmm?"*

When spoken to directly:

:   **Can you train me in Alchemy?**
:   *"No, no. Mostly, I'm just a simple herbalist. Lami over in Morthal should be able to help you."* **or** *"No, no. I'm just a simple herbalist. You'll want to see Arcadia, over in Whiterun."*

:   **Aromatics? So you sell perfumes?**
:   *"We mostly carry herbs and alchemical ingredients, that sort of thing. Before the war, our stock was mostly used for aromatic use in homes, yes.
    These days, we have more people like you coming in, looking for healing and the like."*

You can [invest](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Investor "Skyrim:Speech") in her business:

:   **I'd like to make an investment in your business.**
:   *"Splendid! With the extra coin, I'll be able to purchase twice the volume in supplies that I normally do."*
:   **Let's see what you can do with this.**
:   *"I'll call upon my suppliers this very evening and arrange to double my orders."*

When exiting conversation with her she can say:

:   *"Thanks again for finding out about my daughter."*
:   *"Don't forget me next time you need herbs and potions."*

## Conversations

Angeline may have some short conversations with her niece Vivienne in her store:

**Angeline**: *"Vivienne, could you check out supplies of mandrake root?"*
**Vivienne**: *"Which one is that again?"*
**Angeline**: *"It's the root that looks like an ugly little man."*
**Vivienne**: *"In that case, I'm pretty sure it tried to buy me a drink last night."*

## Notes

- Angeline refers to herself as "Angela" in her dialogue, and she is referred to by that name during the quest [No News is Good News](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News") as well.

## Bugs

- When investing gold in Angeline's store, the chat option does not disappear. Therefore it is possible to invest repeatedly in her shop. However, because of the way the script works, she does not retain this gold. Consequently it is impossible for her base gold to be raised by the investing perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - You can use the console command `set PerkInvestorSolitudeApothecary to 0` to invest in the store.
