Angeline's Aromatics

**Angeline's Aromatics** is the [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") shop in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The proprietor, [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard"), trades potions, food, ingredients, and books, and has 500 base gold. If anything happens to Angeline, her niece, [Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis"), runs the store in her place.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary")  [Vivienne Onis](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary") |

## Related Quests

- **[No News is Good News](/wiki/Skyrim:No_News_is_Good_News "Skyrim:No News is Good News")**: Find out about the fate of [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard")'s daughter from [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis").

## Angeline's Aromatics

The entrance leads directly into the shop with the counter across in front of you. On the counter are three common books, a couple of open crates displaying various merchandise, with a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of dried [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging above the counter against the west wall (which is all merchandise). Above the counter at the other end are two further garlic braids and two more bunches of dried elves ears (which are also merchandise). There are also a [petty](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and [lesser](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") for sale on a ledge and stand. Against the south wall, to the left of the entrance is a low table holding three more common books and some more merchandise, with a small non-respawning wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") next to it with an open crate on top. There is then a narrow table with two more open crates, one on the narrow table and the other on the floor in front of it, beside two black kettles. These all contain merchandise for sale.

To the right of the entrance is a wooden bench beside a set of shelves with more displayed merchandise and a pair of boots. North of these is a set of double doors leading to the residence, with an alcove to the east containing an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and to the west access behind the counter. Against the north wall, behind the counter are four sets of shelves mainly holding various displayed merchandise, along a set of blue mage robes and an empty petty soul gem. Under the counter are more items that are sold. At the western end of the counter is another alcove with more merchandise displayed on a set of shelves and a cupboard.

The door to the north leads to a dining area with a long wooden table with a chair and a wooden bench pulled up to it. It is laid for three people with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), some [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), some [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), and some [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"). Against the south wall are two sets of shelves holding clutter. Against the east wall is a narrow table with a bowl of bread, a plate holding an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and a plate of [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), with a wall shelf above holding a bottle of alto wine and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the left is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand, while in the northeastern corner is a small non-respawning cupboard. Against the north wall is a bookcase holding eight common books, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"). By the door, against the west wall is a wooden bench where you can often find [Angeline Morrard](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") sitting down.

Climbing the stairs there is a large vase containing a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush half way up. At the top of the stairs is a landing with a small cupboard on the left holding a bottle of alto wine and three bottles of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"). Along the north wall is a wooden bench and a low table, and a door leading to [Angeline Morrard's](/wiki/Skyrim:Angeline_Morrard "Skyrim:Angeline Morrard") bedroom opposite. There are two more doors to the east, and around the corner against the south wall is a narrow table with a [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a stone bowl containing a sprig of snowberries, a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), a [Hagraven feather](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), and a [Hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw") on top. There are two wall shelves above, holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [potion of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), a [weak aversion to shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Shock"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a copy of *[Pension of the Ancestor Moth](/wiki/Skyrim:Pension_of_the_Ancestor_Moth "Skyrim:Pension of the Ancestor Moth")*, and a copy of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*.

Angeline's bedroom is a large bedroom with a wooden bench opposite a small non-respawning wardrobe containing fine clothes on either side as you enter. There is a four-posted double bed coming out of the south wall opposite, with a non-respawning end table on either side. On the right-hand one of these is a copy of *[The Amulet of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Amulet_of_Kings "Skyrim:The Amulet of Kings")*. Against the west wall is a table [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a bowl of bread, and a plate with a [sliced Eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") on it. A wall shelf above holds a bottle of alto wine. At the foot of the bed is an unlocked long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items. To the left of the bed are two wall shelves holding a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") and a set of [novice robes of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Robes_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Novice Robes of Illusion"), as well as a sprig of lavender. There is a chair in the southeast corner with a non-respawning tall wardrobe to the left along the east wall. In the northeast corner are two bookcases, a wooden bench and a low table with a bunch of tundra cotton and two common books. The bookcases hold a set of [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes"), a bunch of elves ears, a sprig of snowberries, a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") and three more common books.

The left-hand door on the east wall of the landing leads into [Vivienne Onis'](/wiki/Skyrim:Vivienne_Onis "Skyrim:Vivienne Onis") bedroom containing a single owned bed in the northeastern corner and a non-respawning end table to the right, as well as a small non-respawning wardrobe against the south wall holding a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"), a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina") and a common book. Further to the right is a chair by a narrow table which is holding an iron dagger, a bowl of bread and a plate with a sliced Eidar cheese with a wall shelf above with two bottles of Nord mead and a bottle of alto wine on it. There is a tall non-respawning wardrobe and washbasin on a stand opposite, against the north wall. The right-hand door leads into a study of sorts with a wall shelf and two bookcases against the north wall. There is a potion of plentiful healing and a sprig of lavender on the wall shelf. On the bookshelf are eleven common books as well as copies of *[2920, Sun's Dusk, v11](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dusk,_v11 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dusk, v11")* and *[2920, Evening Star, v12](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Evening_Star,_v12 "Skyrim:2920, Evening Star, v12")*. There is also an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items. Against the south wall is a large round wooden table and two chairs, with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top.

Descending the stairs to the cellar leads to a storage area with several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels around the cellar. Against the north wall is a cupboard holding a bowl of [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), several pieces of cheese, a few loaves of bread, two [sweetrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"). Further to the right is an unlocked chest containing random items with a garlic braid, two bunches of dried elves ears and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") all hanging from the ceiling above. To the east is a small unit with a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and against the south wall is another non-respawning cupboard holding a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), more loaves of bread and many more pieces of assorted cheese. Finally in the southwest corner is a long wooden table with a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a bunch of tundra cotton, a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), some [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), some dried elves ears, a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), some [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") a loaf of bread and a plate with a red and two green apples on top.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Only items players are likely to want to purchase are listed. Other items may also be present in the store, but they are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Ingredients: 1 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), 1 [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), 2 [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), 1 [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), 7 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 1 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), 2 [Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), 1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), 1 [Garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), 1 [Glow Dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), 2 [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), 1 [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 1 [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), 2 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), 2 [Juniper Berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), 8 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), 2 [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), 2 [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), 1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), 1 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), 2 [Slaughterfish Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), 1 [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), 1 [Thistle Branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), 4 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), 3 [Void Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), 1 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat")
- Ingredient (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 2 [Orange Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing")
- Poisons: 1 [Weak Aversion to Shock](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Shock "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Shock"), 1 [Weak Paralysis Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Paralysis Poison"), 2 [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), 1 [Weak Stamina Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Stamina Poison")
- Poison (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 3 [Frostbite Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom")
- Potions: 1 [Potion of Extreme Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina"), 2 [Potion of Haggling](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Haggling "Skyrim:Potion of Haggling"), 5 [Potion of Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), 3 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 1 [Potion of Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), 7 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Minor Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), 2 [Potion of Plentiful Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), 2 [Potion of Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), 2 [Potion of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), 1 [Solution of Strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength")

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the store's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ~11 | Common [Ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") | Max 15 (15@75%) |
| 1 | Common [Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes") |  |
| ~8 | Leveled Fortify Skill [Potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Healing Potions | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Other Potions | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Resist Potions | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~8 | Leveled Poisons | Max 10 (10@75%) |
| ~1 | Poison Recipes | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| 1 | [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease") |  |
| ~4 | Rare Ingredients | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~1 | Rare Recipes | Max 1 (1@50%) |
| 1 | [Salt Piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |  |
| ~8 | Uncommon Ingredients | Max 10 (10@75%) |

## Notes

- Most of the food, [beverages](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") out in the open (with the exception of hanging bunches of herbs) around the residence and shop are sold by Angeline, in addition to the displayed merchandise. Because of this quirk, the shop has one of the largest sets of wares for sale in the game.
- Approaching the alchemy lab will cause Angeline to follow you to it, as if you were in the private living quarters of the building, even though you are still well within the shop limits.
- In [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online"), the building was occupied by a [bank](/wiki/Online:Bankers "Online:Bankers") called [Haafingar Hoard](/wiki/Online:Haafingar_Hoard "Online:Haafingar Hoard").

## Bugs

- When investing gold in Angeline's store, the chat option does not disappear. Therefore it is possible to invest repeatedly in her shop. However, because of the way the script works, she does not retain this gold. Consequently it is impossible for her base gold to be raised by the investing perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
  - You can use the console command `set PerkInvestorSolitudeApothecary to 0` to invest in the store.

# Skyrim:Anger

## Overview

Anger

**Anger** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardImperial "Skyrim:GuardImperial") who is an aspect of [Pelagius the Mad's](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_the_Mad "Skyrim:Pelagius the Mad") mind. He only appears in [The Mind of a Madman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_a_Madman "Skyrim:The Mind of a Madman") during the related quest. He will be beating up the much smaller [Confidence](/wiki/Skyrim:Confidence_(NPC) "Skyrim:Confidence (NPC)"), and you will be tasked with evening the odds with the help of the [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack").

Anger is equipped with [studded Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Imperial Armor") along with [Imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots"), [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Light Bracers"), and a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet").

## Related Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").

# Skyrim:Angi's Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shack.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shack.png) | Shack: Angi's Camp ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angi%27s+Camp)) | | |

| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 12 |
| Occupants | |
| [Angi](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi "Skyrim:Angi") | |

Angi's Camp

**Angi's Camp** is a cabin and camp southeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). [Angi](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi "Skyrim:Angi"), a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") from [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), is the only occupant. She is in hiding due to her killing the two drunken [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") soldiers who murdered her parents. Angi is very skilled with the [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), and is willing to teach [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") for free through target practice competition. For each of six subtasks, you will gain one skill point in Archery, providing an easy way to train the skill. Mastering all six tasks additionally yields [Angi's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Angi's Bow"), a unique non-enchanted [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow").

For details on the archery training you can perform here, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi#Archery_Practice "Skyrim:Angi").

## Getting There

Getting to Angi's Camp can be difficult. It's high up in the mountains, and the marked paths there do not start close to the camp itself.

Starting from [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"), head south across the main road and onto a side road marked by stacked stones to the right. Follow this path to a pond, then head west along another side road until you reach a dead end. At this point, turn around and take the unmarked higher path, keeping the stacked stones to your left (two of them will have flags attached) until you reach yet another path. You'll soon reach a fork; the left path goes to a small hunting camp (along with [Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade"), if [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") is installed), while the right leads on. The main path comes to another fork after a while. Going straight will lead to [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), while going right will finally lead to Angi's Camp (watch out for bear traps).

Alternatively, start at Bloodlet Throne and head west along the road to reach the final intersection before Angi's Camp.

## Exterior

The shooting range

The camp is really a shack with no front door, and the windows are just holes with shutters. There is a firepit outside to the west, with a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") by the fire and a lean-to full of firewood behind it. There is a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") outside to the right of the doorway against the side of the shack, with a food barrel and a small set of empty shelves beside it. To the left of the doorway on the wall of the shack are three weapon racks together. There is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush by the northern corner of the shack, as well as a path heading north and down two flights of stairs to Agni's archery range where she is willing to give you free lessons. The range is marked out with wood, and has four targets at different distances. There is a second snowberry bush beside the range.

## Angi's Camp

Shack interior

Inside the shack, on your left as you enter against the northwest wall is a long wooden table and bench. On the table is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). In the northern corner is a barrel containing common ingredients, and along the northeastern wall is a firepit with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over it. To the right against the same wall is a non-respawning cupboard. On the shelves are two sacks, a pair of [farm boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"), and a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000cee80 "Skyrim:Clothes"). There is a small bedroom to the right of the cupboard, with the doorway in the southeastern wall, again with no door. There is a barrel and a crate on your right as you enter the shack, and to the left of the crate hanging from a roof strut is a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, a sample of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

In the bedroom area, on your left as you enter is an unlocked chest containing leveled items. In the southern corner is a double bed, and beside this is a non-respawning end table which contains [treasure map V](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_V "Skyrim:Treasure Map V"), while on top is a copy of the Archery [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")*.

## Bugs

- Angi's Camp has no location keyword set. This appears to have led to it not playing any sort of music when visited.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. A previous USKP patch added music to a number of locations, but for some unknown reason, Angi's Camp was left out.

# Skyrim:Angi

## Overview

| Angi (RefID: 000CAB2E) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Angi's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Angi's Camp") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 10 | Class | [Ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000CAB2E | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000CAB2F |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 150 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor")**, [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | Any Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [WIGenericCrimeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:WIGenericCrimeFaction "Skyrim:WIGenericCrimeFaction") | | |

Angi outside her hut

**Angi** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)"), and from what little information she gives, is also an outlaw. She lives in [her camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Camp "Skyrim:Angi's Camp"), which she states she built, and can be found south of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), high upon a mountain ridge. As her story goes, she lives there because her family was killed by two drunken Imperial soldiers, upon whom she then exacted her vengeance. To reach the camp, you will have to travel far to the east, then double back to the west as you ascend the mountain. She wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"), and wields a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") with fifteen [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow").

Angi also offers practice in [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") and each task completed will increase Archery by 1 (up to 6 levels); she is willing to give you a free [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and practice arrows; both of them are outside, to the left of the door to her cabin. This bow can be a valuable asset for her archery challenges due to its rather high draw speed. Upon completion of her training regimen, and assuming you interact with her in a positive and friendly manner, she will give you [her bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Angi's Bow").

Note that in the bedroom of her cabin you will find the Archery skill book *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")* on an end table, and [Treasure Map V](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_V "Skyrim:Treasure Map V") inside it.

## Dialogue

Upon approaching her for the first time she will introduce herself:

:   *"Name's Angi and if you try anything stupid I won't hesitate to put an arrow in your head."*

:   :   **Let's see about that. Time to die!**
    :   *"You chose the wrong girl to mess with."* **(Turns hostile)**

:   :   **Calm down. I'm not going to hurt you.**
    :   *"Sorry, a girl can't be too careful out here. Like I said, name's Angi and I've been living out here for a couple of years now."*

Her normal greetings:

:   *"Looking to practice, stranger?"*
:   *"Great job hitting those targets. You definitely surprised me with your speed and composure."*
:   *"Ready to practice some more?"*
:   *"It's not often I get visitors out here. You lost, stranger?"*
:   *"Lost, stranger?"*

When spoken to:

:   **Why live out here all by yourself?**
:   *"I moved here from [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") after my family was killed. At the time I couldn't stand to be around anyone. They all felt sorry for me and I didn't want them to. It was my problem, not theirs."*

:   :   **Who killed your family?**
    :   *"Two Imperial drunks who thought they were above the law."*

        :   **Want me to take care of them?**
        :   *"Already did. Part of the reason I'm living out here now. Thanks for offering though."*

:   :   **I'm sorry about your family.**
    :   *"Don't be like them. Don't feel sorry for me."*

:   **What are those targets for?**
:   *"I set up those targets a long time ago. I shoot at them from time to time. Don't want to get rusty with my bow."*
:   **Are you any good with your bow?**
:   *"That I am. You know how to use one?"*
:   **No, not really.** / **Probably better than you.** / **Let's just say Hircine would be jealous.**
:   *"Well let me know if you ever want to practice. If you need a bow, there's one on the rack to the left of the door."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"Take care, stranger. Be careful out there."*
:   *"Remember, composure and speed. You don't need to see your arrow hit before moving onto your next target. Trust your shot is true."*
:   *"It was nice to spend time with someone who enjoys archery as much as I do."*

#### Test of Accuracy

Located just outside of Angi's cabin is an archery target area. Angi can provide you with several Archery practice sessions, resulting in a total of 6 level increases. Angi will reveal more of her past and offer her advice during each session. The first test is to hit the closest 3 targets with an arrow. In this first practice round, 1 skill point is provided for each target you hit (3 points total):

:   **I'm ready for some practice.**
:   *"Excellent. Follow me to the targets and we'll begin."*

She will then walk down to the target area while saying:

:   *"My father was rarely home, so it was my mother who actually taught me how to use a bow. She always said composure was the key to a successful archer. If you can remain calm, even in the midst of chaos, your arrow will most likely find its target."*

After she has finished demonstrating:

:   *"OK, let's see what you can do. Remember to stay within the boundaries and only use the practice arrows. I have some if you don't have any. Aim for the middle target."*

If spoken to at this point:

:   **I need some practice arrows.**
:   *"Here you go."*

:   **What are the rules again?**
:   *"It's easy - stay inside the boundaries and only use the practice arrows."*

If you only have 1 training arrow left she will give you 9 more and say:

:   *"Here, take these. Looks like you're running low."*

If you leave the boundary area:

:   *"You need to stay inside the boundaries."*

Hitting the middle target:

:   *"Nice shot! Right on target. Now hit the target to the left."*

Hitting the left target:

:   *"Great shot. Now hit the target to the right."*

Hitting the right target:

:   *"Nice shot! Right on target. Let me know if you want to practice some more. Next time we'll make it a little more challenging."*

#### Test of Speed

Hit the closest 3 targets in 8 seconds. Angi will count down from 3 and yell "Go," at which point you have 8 seconds to hit the 3 closest targets. Completing this challenge will get you 1 additional skill point.

:   **I'm ready for some more practice.**
:   *"Excellent. Follow me to the targets and we'll begin."*

She will then walk to the target section while saying:

:   *"My older brother took me out hunting a lot when I was little. At the time, it was difficult to keep food on the table, let alone have enough left over to sell at the market. So whenever we came across more than one deer in a single location, it was imperative we kill as many as we could. If you can learn to keep your composure and trust that each shot is true, then you should be able to quickly handle multiple targets. When I tell you to, try and hit each of the three closest targets in eight seconds. I'll count to three and then say "go." You have eight seconds to hit each of the three targets. Draw string and get ready. One, two, three... Go!"*

If you don't manage to do it under eight seconds:

:   *"Time's up! Better luck next time."*

If you do manage to hit them under eight seconds:

:   *"You did it! All three targets in eight seconds. Nice job. Let me know if you want to practice some more. Next time we'll make it a little more challenging."*

#### Test of Precision

Hit the farthest target, located in the middle of and far behind the three closest targets. Again, 1 skill point is awarded for completing this task.

:   **I'm ready for some more practice.**
:   *"Excellent. Follow me to the targets and we'll begin."*

She will then walk to the target area while saying:

:   *"We've talked about speed and composure. Now we'll go over precision. Often times you won't be able to get as close to your prey as you'd like and you'll have to settle with a long shot. However, with such a long shot, it's more than likely that's the only shot you'll be able to take before your prey runs off. If you find yourself in such a situation, then you need to make your shot count. Don't rush your shot. Crouch down, get comfortable, and take aim. OK, your turn. Try and hit that target way in the back, far behind the other three. Remember to take your time and make your shot count."*

If you hit the target:

:   *"Nice shot! Right on target. Let me know if you want to practice some more. Next time we'll make it a little more challenging."*

#### Final Test

Hit all 4 targets within 10 seconds. Note that this round can be challenging to complete. As before, 1 skill point is awarded upon completion of the task.

:   **I'm ready for some more practice.**
:   *"Excellent. Follow me to the targets and we'll begin."*

She will then walk to the target area while saying:

:   *"We've talked about composure, speed, and precision. Now it's time to use all three at once. I'm warning you now, this challenge will be quite difficult. Just remember everything I've taught you and you should be able to complete it. It may take you a couple of tries, but that's what practice is all about. When I tell you to, try and hit all four targets in ten seconds. I'll count to three and then say "go." You have ten seconds to hit each of the four targets. Draw string and get ready. One, two, three... Go!"*

If you don't manage to do it under ten seconds:

:   *"Time's up! Better luck next time."*

If you do manage to hit all four under ten seconds:

:   *"You did it! All four targets in ten seconds. Nice job."*

Upon completion of all of these tasks:

:   **I'm ready for some more practice.**
:   *"I think I've taught you everything I know. You might even be as good as me now. Kind of scary if I think about it."*

:   :   **Thanks for helping me out.**
    :   *"It was my pleasure. It's not often I get visitors out here. Let alone friendly ones."*

:   :   **Maybe I can teach you a thing or two about using a bow.**
    :   *"Very funny."*

:   :   **Looks like you're no longer needed. Time to die.**
    :   *"You chose the wrong girl to mess with."* **(Turns hostile)**

If either of the first two options are picked she will continue with:
*"Thanks for sticking around and keeping me company. It was nice to finally meet someone out here who doesn't want to rob you or take off your head. I know it isn't much, but here, take this bow. It was given to me by my family. It's special to me, but brings back too many painful memories."*

She'll give you [Angi's bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Angi%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Angi's Bow").

## Notes

- The trajectory of arrows in Skyrim works much like in real life, as demonstrated by the four targets:
  - For the closest target, the trajectory is flat; aim at or just below dead center.
  - For the target on the left, the arrow lofts or sails; aim at a point about half a target's width on the post below.
  - For the farther target on the right, the lofting is at its highest; aim a full target's width down the post.
  - For the farthest target, the arrow drops back into trajectory; aim about a full target's width above the top of the target.
- To familiarize yourself with arrow trajectory, aim at a post, where the arrow will normally stick, at varying distances noting where you hit. The only thing missing in Skyrim archery is drift and distance drop. The arrow tends to stay aloft, disobeying trajectory, much farther than they would in real life. With a little practice, you can shoot targets several hundred yards (paces) away.
- If you can't see the farthest target, try increasing the object detail and view distance in the options menu.
- The [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") shout helps with completing the quest.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Angi)*]
- In addition to the skill book, you can get up to six Archery skill increases, depending on your starting Archery skill. Therefore, to get the most out of Angi's Camp, you may wait until your Archery skill is 93, or 92 if you have [Scholar's Insight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)"), and then use this location to raise Archery to 100.
- Angi only gives 10 practice arrows at a time. More arrows can be found next to the bow leaning against the corner of her cabin and on the ground next to the corner of the training boundaries. An infinite number may be obtained by dropping the arrows and asking her for more.
- Practice arrows are the only type of arrow that can be used for Angi's archery practice and are the only arrows with 0 base damage, which can be useful when you do not want to kill the target, such as applying a [Frenzy](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_(effect) "Skyrim:Frenzy (effect)") poison or to [Paralyze](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralyze_(effect) "Skyrim:Paralyze (effect)") prior to [Soul Trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

## Bugs

- If a dragon attacks while Angi is walking to the training area for practice, she will not resume walking there after the dragon is killed, and the dialogue option to train with her will be removed.
- Feeding on Angi as a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") with the [Vampire's Seduction](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Seduction "Skyrim:Vampire's Seduction") [power](/wiki/Skyrim:Powers "Skyrim:Powers") can result in the Dragonborn clipping several meters in a random direction while the animation occurs, even into the nearby mountainside depending on position. **?**
- This quest can glitch, especially during the fourth challenge, making it impossible to complete. If Angi says "Watch it!" or similar chastising remarks when you fire at a target, the targets or quest may be glitching. Leaving the area and staying away for a few days in game can resolve this so the quest can be completed. **?**
- Angi never sleeps due to the lack of a sleep package.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Angler Acquaintances

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Begin your fishing journey.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | When player first visits the [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Reward: | None |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Start\_MQ2 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day"), [In A Pinch](/wiki/Skyrim:In_A_Pinch "Skyrim:In A Pinch") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day"), [In A Pinch](/wiki/Skyrim:In_A_Pinch "Skyrim:In A Pinch") | | |

Begin at the Riften Fishery.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Visit the Riften Fishery.
2. Speak with Viriya.
3. Speak with Swims-In-Deep-Water.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The quests starts when the player first visits the [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery"). There they will need to speak with [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya") and [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water"), the two experienced fishermen. Speaking with the two will start the [In A Pinch](/wiki/Skyrim:In_A_Pinch "Skyrim:In A Pinch") and [Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day") quests, respectively.

## Quest Stages

| Angler Acquaintances (ccBGSSSE001\_Start\_MQ2) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | To become more skilled at fishing, I should visit the Riften Fishery and speak to those who work there. In particular, Viriya and Swims-In-Deep-Water are rumored to be highly knowledgeable. *Objective 0:* Visit the Riften Fishery |
| 5 |  | Viriya and Swims-In-Deep-Water are experienced fishermen employed by the Riften Fishery. I should speak to them about how I might be able to help, and improve my fishing abilities in the process. *Objective 10:* Talk to Swims-In-Deep-Water  *Objective 20:* Talk to Viriya |
| 200 | ☑ | I've introduced myself to both of the most experienced fishermen at the Riften Fishery, with the hope that their assignments will help me hone my skill in fishing. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Start_MQ2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Start_MQ2`.

# Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored

## Overview

| Angrenor Once-Honored (RefID: 0001B138) | | | |

Angrenor Once-Honored

Angrenor and Rolff bullying Suvaris Atheron

**Angrenor Once-Honored** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggars "Skyrim:Beggars") who was a former member of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). Upon raising his disposition by giving him a coin, he will become a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

He can be found relaxing in [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall") from 4am to 10am. He then goes to the Stone Quarter, leaning against a wall. At 4pm he patrols Windhelm for twelve hours, then returns to Candlehearth Hall.

Unlike most beggars, he wears a set of prison clothes: a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") with [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps"). He carries an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and a selection of [lower-class items](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming"): Develop your farm.
- **[Quest all Beggars Have](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_all_Beggars_Have "Skyrim:Quest all Beggars Have")**: Take pity on a beggar. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"I was one of the best soldiers in the Stormcloak army, until I took a sword through the chest."*
:   *"I once killed six men, single-handed, while rescuing my brothers-in-arms from ambush by an Imperial patrol."*
:   *"I'd be out there fighting the Imperials right now if it wasn't for my war-wound."*
:   *"Ever since that Imperial craven ran me through from behind, I've had trouble breathing. Don't have any trouble drinking though."*
:   *"I'm not too proud to admit that I need a bit of help from time to time."*

### Conversations

Upon entering [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") for the first time, you will witness Angrenor and his counterpart [Rolff Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Rolff_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Rolff Stone-Fist") harassing a [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Suvaris_Atheron "Skyrim:Suvaris Atheron") and accusing her of being an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") spy, making no attempt to conceal their disdain for elves:

:   **Rolff**: *"You come here where you're not wanted, you eat our food, you pollute our city with your stink and you refuse to help the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")."*
:   **Suvaris**: *"But we haven't taken a side because it's not our fight."*
:   **Angrenor**: *"Hey, maybe the reason these gray-skins don't help in the war is because they're Imperial spies!"*
:   **Suvaris**: *"Imperial spies? You can't be serious!"*
:   **Rolff**: *"Maybe we'll pay you a visit tonight, little spy. We got ways of finding out what you really are."*

## Unused Dialogue

He was meant to have more dialogue once he moved into the [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence"), which will never be heard due to a [bug](#Bugs). He would have defended his claim on the house to you, saying:

:   *"What? Were you hoping to claim this house for yourself? Well, the Aretinos always liked me, so I think I'm family enough to take up here."*

Angrenor also would have referenced Innocence Lost, saying:

:   *"Rumor holds that the Aretino boy brought an assassin here. Sounds like nonsense to me."*

He would also have disparaged his fellow Windhelm residents, saying:

:   *"The milk drinkers in this town wouldn't last five minutes in a real battle."*

## Notes

- He is the only beggar who is able to be married in the game.

## Bugs

- After completing the quest [Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost") he carries around a key to the [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence"). He should have moved into the house after the quest, but the scripting is incomplete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- Once married, Angrenor will still beg for money, even if he is living at your home.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- If their conversation with Suvaris is interrupted by combat (e.g. by a dragon or vampire attack), Rolff and Angrenor will be stuck standing at the main gate permanently.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed by using the command `startscene CD91F`.

Angvid

**Angvid** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who is trying to make a living in [Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine"). However, due to the lack of ore of any kind in the mine, he is wondering if it is still worth it and is losing his faith in both [Thorgar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorgar "Skyrim:Thorgar") and the mine.

He will sleep in one of the bedrolls near the entrance from 8am to 8pm. Once he is awake he will mine the few ore veins, cook, or sit at the table.

He wears a standard [miner's outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") and carries an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When approached, he makes the situation and his doubts quite clear by saying:

:   *"We were supposed to be rich by now, you know. Thorgar insisted we'd be swimming in gold."*
:   *"I'm starting to think we might not even find iron in here. We've been at it for so long."*
:   *"Is it still worth it? When do you decide enough is enough, and just walk away?"*

# Skyrim:Animal Extermination (A)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. .jpg)

An invading Snow Bear lying dead in [Proudspire Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Proudspire_Manor "Skyrim:Proudspire Manor")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") to speak with [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") about work.
2. Clear out the beast invading a citizen of Skyrim's home or shop.
3. Return to Aela for payment.

### The Job

Once you have completed the [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms") quest, you can begin work as a Companion. As one of the group's leaders, Aela the Huntress will allocate jobs to those looking for work. When you approach Aela she will inform you that: *"A citizen of <a location in Skyrim> has asked for our help. It seems a predator has invaded their <home, shop, farm>, and someone needs to clear the beast out."*
Accept the job and your journal will be updated with the location and the type of predator you need to exterminate.

| PC Level | Beasts |
| --- | --- |
| >=1 | [Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") |
| >=6 | [Ice Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"), [Ice Wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [Sabre Cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") |
| >=11 | [Snowy Sabre Cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat") |
| >=12 | [Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") |
| >=16 | [Cave Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear "Skyrim:Cave Bear") |
| >=20 | [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [Snow Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear") |

The location can be any of at least forty-two houses in Skyrim. The list includes most houses (other than inns) that are occupied by standard town citizens. The location will be limited to holds that you have previously visited, so early in the game you may only receive destinations within Whiterun Hold, but later in the game there are many more possible destinations. Note that if you have the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on installed, the location may be on Solstheim, in which case your quest marker will not appear while you are in Skyrim.

| House | City/Town | Victim(s) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Aeri's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri%27s_House "Skyrim:Aeri's House") | [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") | [Aeri](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeri "Skyrim:Aeri") |
| [Fruki's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Fruki%27s_House "Skyrim:Fruki's House") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [Fruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Fruki "Skyrim:Fruki") |
| [Irgnir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir%27s_House "Skyrim:Irgnir's House") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir") |
| [Leigelf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf%27s_House "Skyrim:Leigelf's House") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") |
| [Rustleif's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif%27s_House "Skyrim:Rustleif's House") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | [Rustleif](/wiki/Skyrim:Rustleif "Skyrim:Rustleif"), [Seren](/wiki/Skyrim:Seren "Skyrim:Seren") |
| [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | [Heljarchen Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Heljarchen_Hall "Skyrim:Heljarchen Hall") | [Player's spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") or [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") |
| [Klimmek's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek%27s_House "Skyrim:Klimmek's House") | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") | [Bassianus Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Bassianus_Axius "Skyrim:Bassianus Axius"), [Klimmek](/wiki/Skyrim:Klimmek "Skyrim:Klimmek") |
| [Karthwasten Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten_Hall "Skyrim:Karthwasten Hall") | [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | [Ainethach](/wiki/Skyrim:Ainethach "Skyrim:Ainethach") |

### Reward

Once you have eliminated the invader, return to Aela at Jorrvaskr for your payment. This quest is repeatable.

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
- Aela can also give you the quest if you encounter her while out hunting in Skyrim.
- The animals that spawn will not be restricted to that animal's natural habitat. For example, you could find a snow bear or snowy sabre cat in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") or [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"), even though these places have more temperate climates.
- Sometimes you are technically considered trespassing when you enter one of these homes, even though you have permission to be there. Though you will not get a bounty, your followers will still refuse to speak to you, insisting that *"You're not supposed to be in here."* while in the house. However if the door is locked and you are seen picking the lock, then you will receive a bounty of 5 septims.

## Bugs

- After killing the beast and returning to Aela, your quest will be acknowledged as complete, but it may remain in your quest list. If this happens, Aela will not give you any further quests to do (though it will still trigger The Silver Hand quest if you are far enough in the Companion's Quest Line). This can be circumvented by loading a save prior to reporting back to Aela and using unrelenting force on her before talking to her.
- After killing the beast, the owner of the home will not give any thanks and instead will accuse you of trespassing. If you do not leave immediately he or she will call the guards and you will be [arrested](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime") upon exiting the house.

## Quest Stages

| Animal Extermination (CR01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been tasked to clear the <Alias=Beast> out of <Alias=BeastVictim>'s home in <Alias=VictimHometown>. *Objective 10:* Kill the <Alias=Beast> |
| 20 |  | I've cleared the <Alias=Beast> out of <Alias=BeastVictim>'s home in <Alias=VictimHometown>. *Objective 20:* Return to Aela |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| 250 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR01`.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Request work from Companion leader [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress").
2. Kill the boss beast in the random animal den.
3. Return to Aela.

### Life as a Companion

Once you have completed the [Take Up Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Take_Up_Arms "Skyrim:Take Up Arms") quest, you can begin work as a Companion.
The Companions tradition of service dates back to the mercenary aid given to [Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor "Skyrim:Ysgramor") by the Five Hundred Companions. Since then the Companions have served as a group of impartial and independent contractors, helping out commoner and jarl alike in matters of might, but taking no sides nor making any alliances themselves.

### The Extermination Job

Locate Aela in [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"). She has received a request from one of the [Jarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") that an [animal den](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Animal_Dens "Category:Skyrim-Places-Animal Dens") in their Hold be cleared of nuisance beasts.

When you speak to Aela to ask for work she will reply, *"The Jarl of <Hold > has asked for our help. It seems that predators have taken up residence and have been attacking farmers and travelers. Someone's got to head out there and take care of the beasts."*

When you reply that you can take care of it, Aela will respond with either words of encouragement or caution:

*"I knew we could count on you. Get it taken care of right away. Nobody wants an animal left roaming around in their place."* **or** *"Be cautious. Beasts are not nearly as predictable as men. Give the thing a quick death."*

As she sends you on your way your journal will reflect your new quest and your map will update with the beast den location.
As this is a radiant quest, the boss-type beast will be in any of these 17 locations:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout") [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave") [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave") [Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest") | [Bonechill Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonechill_Passage "Skyrim:Bonechill Passage") [Greywater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Greywater_Grotto "Skyrim:Greywater Grotto") | [Steepfall Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Steepfall_Burrow "Skyrim:Steepfall Burrow") | [Brood Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Brood_Cavern "Skyrim:Brood Cavern") | [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave") | [Clearspring Tarn](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearspring_Tarn "Skyrim:Clearspring Tarn") [Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave") [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave") [Honeystrand Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeystrand_Grove "Skyrim:Honeystrand Grove") [Pinepeak Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinepeak_Cavern "Skyrim:Pinepeak Cavern") | [Cold Rock Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cold_Rock_Pass "Skyrim:Cold Rock Pass") [Graywinter Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Graywinter_Watch "Skyrim:Graywinter Watch") [Greenspring Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Greenspring_Hollow "Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow") [Darkshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkshade "Skyrim:Darkshade") | [Bleakcoast Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakcoast_Cave "Skyrim:Bleakcoast Cave") |

### Reward

Once you have killed the beast, return to Jorrvaskr and speak with Aela again. Let her know you have completed the task, to which she will reply: *"Good work. The mindless cretins didn't stand a chance."* Your reward of leveled gold will then be added.

| Levels[†](#intnote_LevelNote) | Reward[‡](#intnote_RewardBug) | USLEEP Reward |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 100 | 100 |
| 10–19 | 150 | 150 |
| 20–29 | 300 | 200 |
| 30–39 | 300 | 250 |
| 40+ | 300 | 300 |

[†](#note_LevelNote)Level is based on when the player completed the previous quest (or level one for the first quest), not the player's level when receiving the quest or its reward.

[‡](#note_RewardBug)The reward amounts for radiant Companions quests do not progress as intended.

-  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=20007))

## Notes

- Although there may be multiple beasts at the targeted destination, only the boss beast (the one highlighted by the quest marker) actually needs to be killed to complete the quest.

## Bugs

- If the cave that it randomly chooses for you has already been cleared, you may run into a situation where the beast you need to exterminate has already been killed, and the quest marker will point at the corpse, making it impossible to complete the quest. This removes the ability to complete further tasks for the Companions, as they will remark that you have not finished your current contract. Even reanimating the corpse of the beast and killing it again will not fix the issue.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed with the console command `setstage cr02 20`.
  - After enough time has passed for the target location to respawn, the Animal Extermination quest may be moved to the completed section of your journal, even though you did not complete the job. Aela will still be standing by the door inside Jorrvaskr, but she should offer a new job.
  - You might be sent to clear out a Draugr tomb, with the boss being the highest level Draugr there (A Draugr Death Overlord or Dragon Priest). **?**

## Quest Stages

| Animal Extermination (CR02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've been asked to take care of a <Alias=BeastBoss> lair in <Alias=DenHold>. *Objective 10:* Clear out <Alias=AnimalDen> |
| 20 |  | I cleared a <Alias=BeastBoss> lair in <Alias=DenHold>. *Objective 20:* Return to Aela |
| 100 | ☑ |  |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| 250 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CR02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CR02`.

# Skyrim:Anise's Cabin

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Anise's Cabin

**Anise's Cabin** is a small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") west-southwest of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). It contains only one zone, the *[Cellar](#Cellar)*.

The sole occupant is an elderly woman named [Anise](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise "Skyrim:Anise").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Anise](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise "Skyrim:Anise") |

### Exterior

The cabin is near your point of escape from [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). It's also close to [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)") to the north and the [Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones") across the river to the south. The surrounding wilderness often contains friendly hunters or hostile bandits. The latter may engage Anise in combat, in which case she will use [flame spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") and may [summon a familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar").

A [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") grow near the cabin. To the left of the entrance is a chair and a pile of firewood, with a small [vegetable](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Fruit.2FVegetables "Skyrim:Food") garden to the right consisting of three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and two [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants.

The cabin is in a remarkable state of disrepair. To the immediate right on entering is a tall [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") cupboard holding an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). Opposite the entryway is a small wooden chair next to a few sacks and a barrel containing [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). To the left is a long wooden table pressed into the southern corner. On the table is a [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a bowl of [vegetable soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Vegetable_Soup "Skyrim:Vegetable Soup"), with a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid hanging from the ceiling above and hanging from a rack to the right is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). On the floor beside the table is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").

In the eastern corner and along the southeast wall is a single bed, that is marked as owned unless Anise is dead; then it is free to use. At the foot of the bed is small unit holding a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists")*, with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") beside it containing [uncommon ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Leaning against the unit is a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"). Under the head of the bed is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). To the left, against the west wall is a non-respawning dresser and a partially covered novice-locked trapdoor leading to the *Cellar*. There are a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") next to the dresser, and there are [leather bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Bracers "Skyrim:Leather Bracers") as well as a single red mountain flower on top of the dresser.

### Cellar

Cellar

Starting at the bottom of the ladder upon entering and moving around anticlockwise is a cupboard with a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") and a [potent paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Potent_Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Potent Paralysis Poison") on top, with a barrel containing uncommon ingredients and a sideboard next to that. On the sideboard are a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a sample of hagraven feathers, a deathbell, a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), and *[Anise's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Anise's Letter")* that explains Anise is actually a [witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") who is trying to start a coven. Against the south wall is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and to the left an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). To the left of the lab, against the east wall is a small set of shelves holding another apothecary's satchel (containing rare ingredients), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Finally in the eastern corner are a few crates and food sacks.

When you exit the cellar, Anise will become hostile and attack, shouting, *"Fool! None may know my secret!"* This will happen regardless of whether or not you entered the cellar undetected.

## Notes

- When Anise dies, the bed becomes unowned. However, all other items remain owned, and taking them counts as stealing. Also, entering the cellar is always trespassing, which has little effect except that when in the cellar, most followers will only say *"You're not supposed to be in here."*
- As the cellar does not respawn, all containers are [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers") for storage. The cupboard and dresser on the ground floor of the cabin are also standard [safe containers](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Containers "Skyrim:Containers"), but the barrel and apothecary's satchel are not. This makes Anise's cabin a good starter home, since it is a fast travel location with an alchemy lab, an arcane enchanter, a bed, and safe storage.

## Bugs

- Several items in the cabin are owned by the `HagravenFaction`. Stealing these might result in [Moira](/wiki/Skyrim:Moira "Skyrim:Moira") or other random hagravens sending [hired thugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Steal,_Thugs_hunt_player "Skyrim:Steal, Thugs hunt player") after you, even if you have already killed both Anise and the respective hagraven.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.1, fixes this bug.
- The barrel respawns despite being in a "No Reset Zone".
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Anise

## Overview

| Race | [Elder](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") | Gender | Female |

| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50-467 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 100-383 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 25 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")**, **[Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") | | |
| Class Details | [CombatMageConjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleOldKindly](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleOldKindly "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleOldKindly") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Hagraven Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Faction "Skyrim:Hagraven Faction"); [dunPOIWitchAniseCrimeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DunPOIWitchAniseCrimeFaction "Skyrim:DunPOIWitchAniseCrimeFaction") | | |

Anise sitting outside her cabin

*"Fool! None may know my secret!"*

**Anise** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") living in [Anise's Cabin](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Cabin "Skyrim:Anise's Cabin"). She appears to be a lonely alchemist, with several [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), some uncommon, lying around her small home.

Anise will remain in the chair outside of her home until you visit her basement. If you enter her basement, she will be waiting in front of the exit to the cabin.

She wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0001be1b "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") with a [restore magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Magicka "Skyrim:Restore Magicka") effect as well as a dagger ranging in quality from [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") to [daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Dagger "Skyrim:Daedric Dagger").

## Dialogue

Anise will pretend to be a kind, elderly woman if you attempt to speak to her before you learn her secret. Trying to converse with her will have her say;

:   *"I'm just a poor old woman, dear. No need to trouble yourself with me."*
:   *"It's so nice to have a visitor."*
:   *"I get so lonely out here."*
:   *"It's tough, just scraping by out here. But I make do."*

Near the bed inside the cabin is a small hatch to the basement. Inside is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and [Anise's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Anise%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Anise's Letter") revealing that she is, in fact, a witch. After you exit the basement, Anise will attack, yelling:

:   *"Fool! None may know my secret!"*

## Notes

- Anise will attack when you exit the basement, though she won't if you leave the building undetected. However, if you exit [sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") mode, or are sighted, she will initiate combat the moment you are in the doorway.
- Her outfit, `ClothesMageRobesOutfitNoHood`, although not specifically made for her, is only used by her. This results in her being the only NPC with this particular combination of shoes with the blue mage robes as a set outfit.
- Although Anise has a bed, she never uses it, as she has no AI packages set up for sleeping.
- When in combat, she often summons a familiar before unleashing [flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames") or [frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite "Skyrim:Frostbite"). She also has the potential to summon a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") near her highest level.

## Bugs

- If she is killed, her body will remain in the game forever.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
