| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionEastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch "Skyrim:CrimeFactionEastmarch"); [DarkwaterCrossingVernersHouseFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DarkwaterCrossingVernersHouseFaction "Skyrim:DarkwaterCrossingVernersHouseFaction"); [Favor104QuestGiverFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:Favor104QuestGiverFaction "Skyrim:Favor104QuestGiverFaction"); [PotentialFollowerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:PotentialFollowerFaction "Skyrim:PotentialFollowerFaction"); [TownDarkwaterCrossingFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownDarkwaterCrossingFaction "Skyrim:TownDarkwaterCrossingFaction") | | |

Annekke Crag-Jumper

**Annekke Crag-Jumper** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") and former adventurer who lives in [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") with her husband [Verner Rock-Chucker](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_Rock-Chucker "Skyrim:Verner Rock-Chucker"). The couple has put their exploration days behind them, but while Verner is seemingly happy with the more relaxed lifestyle, Annekke has a hard time settling down and will ask you to do some adventuring for her during the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader"). Once you do this favor for her she is available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

She claims to be the one who discovered [Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine"), a likely claim since [her house](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_and_Annekke%27s_House "Skyrim:Verner and Annekke's House") is the only building in town. She sleeps in the house every night between midnight and 6am and always starts the day with a one-hour meal, followed by yet another hour in bed. At 8am she ventures outside and spends three hours wandering restlessly around town until her workday in the mine begins at 11am. After five hours of mining, she leaves the mine at 4pm. She then spends the rest of the day wandering around town interrupted only by a one-hour dinner at 6pm.

Annekke wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00080699 "Skyrim:Clothing") and a pair of [gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#_000261c1 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") with twelve [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Kill the Bandit Leader

When asked if she used to be an adventurer, Annekke will immediately start to tell stories:

:   **You were an adventurer?**
:   *"That's right. Used to explore all over. I'm the one who originally found the mine Darkwater Crossing was built around. I was actually scouting a bit the other day, old times sake. Spied a brigand heading back to his camp. Up for a little hunting? My husband is being a sad stick, so I can't go myself."*

:   **Forget it.**

    :   *"Fair enough."*

:   **I'll do it.**

    :   *"This brings back memories. Come back when you're done and maybe I'll be up to showing you a few tricks."*

When exiting conversation she will remind you:

:   *"Bandits are cowards. Don't strain yourself chasing them all down."*

When you return to her after killing the bandit leader, Annekke will be impressed:

:   *"You remind me of myself a few years ago. Let me show you a little bit about wearing light armor. It's helped me out whenever I was scouting."*

She will then raise your [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill by one point and add:

:   *"Now I've got the itch to travel again. If you're leaving town, I wouldn't mind coming with for a while."*

## Dialogue

When you approach her she can say:

:   *"A traveler? I'll be*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *you've seen some sights. We should swap tales sometime."*
:   *"There's a gorgeous [tree](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary") that grows right up through a cave to the northeast of here."*
:   *"If you're heading to [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"), stick to the road. Some pretty dangerous caves between here and there."*
:   *"Verner used to love exploring before we got married. Now he's become a bit of a milk drinker. Likes to stay home."*
:   *"If you head straight west from where the White River splits towards Whiterun, you can get a look at the [Cradlecrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock") [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant")."*

## Conversations

While Verner is perfectly happy with his new life as a miner, Annekke has a hard time forgetting the excitement of adventuring and their private talks often center on that very topic:

*"You used to love finding new places."*

**Annekke**: *"Verner, you should have come out with me yesterday. I found the most amazing tree growing right out of a cave."*
**Verner**: *"And I found a new deposit of amber. Would have been nice to have some help pulling it out."*
**Annekke**: *"You used to love finding new places."*
**Verner**: *"I still do. I just like to have food waiting for me when I come home."*

**Verner**: *"Ever think about spending more time around town?"*
**Annekke**: *"Not when there's so much to see!"*
**Verner**: *"I guess I should join you more often."*
**Annekke**: *"You should. I miss you."*

**Verner**: *"Sweetheart, did you move my pickaxe?"*
**Annekke**: *"It's at the south end near that loose rockpile."*
**Verner**: *"So you can be helpful sometimes."*
**Annekke**: *"No need to get snippy."*

## Notes

- Although you can't [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") Annekke, you can marry her daughter, [Sylgja](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja "Skyrim:Sylgja")—making her both your follower and mother-in-law.
- Despite them being close family, there is no special dialogue when you visit Sylgia with Annekke as a follower.
- Although listed as a Ranger class, unlike [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") and [Jenassa](/wiki/Skyrim:Jenassa "Skyrim:Jenassa") she cannot dual wield most weapons properly. She will dual wield Forsworn weapons. Also, she can do so if you give her a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), just like [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus"), and will use the pickaxe as an offhand weapon.
- As with all [radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") quests that have multiple quest-givers, you can only have one of them active at a time. If you want to start Annekke's quest and you already have another version of [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader") active, you need to complete it before you can start this one.
- Annekke incorrectly states that Eldergleam Sanctuary is northeast of Darkwater Crossing. It is directly north of there.
- Her husband, Verner, has different interests than his wife and will say:

:   :   *"Annekke used to help more with the mining, but nowadays she's a bit of a bounder."*
    :   *"I do love my wife. Just wish she'd get her head out of the clouds."*
    :   *"If you want some information about the area, Annekke knows it better than anyone."*
    :   *"Sometimes I feel like Annekke cares more about finding new rocks than being with me."*

## Bugs

- It appears that she may attack without provocation either when in the mine or out.
  - This can be resolved by leaving, waiting, and then returning at a later date.
  - Another way to solve this is to get a bounty in Eastmarch and pay it off.
- Her radiant quest may conflict with [a Thieves Guild quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows") depending on the radiant options.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Annekke may not give her radiant quest, ever, even if you have no other active quests that could possibly conflict with it. The other three NPCs ([Ahtar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahtar "Skyrim:Ahtar"), [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") or [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")) that can give a version of the radiant quest appear unaffected, even while Annekke is glitched. This makes it impossible to acquire Annekke as a follower, and she will only give ambient dialogue instead of entering into a conversation tree.
  - Rescuing Derkeethus from Darkwater Pass, having him as an active follower or if you had recently had him as a follower might fix this.(Dismiss your active follower, take Derkeethus as follower, close the dialogue, open up again and dismiss him. Your original follower shouldn't have gone far away and can be asked to follow again even before finding and talking to Annekke.)
  -  Using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to change her [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") to Friend can fix this, allowing her to become your follower.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Annekke_Crag-Jumper)*]

# Skyrim:Anniversary Edition

## Overview

Anniversary Edition box art

| Game Information | | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Setting | [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") (primarily) [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim") [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:Forgotten_Vale "Lore:Forgotten Vale") [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Rielle "Lore:Rielle") [Apocrypha](/wiki/Lore:Apocrypha "Lore:Apocrypha") [Deadlands](/wiki/Lore:Deadlands "Lore:Deadlands") [Revelry](/wiki/Lore:Misty_Grove "Lore:Misty Grove") |
| Development Information | | | | |
| Developer | [Bethesda Softworks](/wiki/General:Bethesda_Softworks "General:Bethesda Softworks") |
| Game Engine | [Creation Engine](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/Creation_Engine "wikipedia:Creation Engine")[[1]](#cite_note-SRTechInfo-1) |
| PC Release Date | November 11, 2021 (Steam)[[1]](#cite_note-SRTechInfo-1) September 28, 2022 (GOG) |
| [Xbox One & Series X|S](/wiki/Skyrim:Xbox "Skyrim:Xbox") Release Date | November 11, 2021[[1]](#cite_note-SRTechInfo-1) |
| [PlayStation 4 & 5](/wiki/Skyrim:PlayStation "Skyrim:PlayStation") Release Date | November 11, 2021[[1]](#cite_note-SRTechInfo-1) |
| [Nintendo Switch](/wiki/Skyrim:Switch "Skyrim:Switch") Release Date | September 28, 2022 |
| Nintendo Switch 2 Release Date | December 9, 2025 |
| [Concept Art](/wiki/Skyrim:Concept_Art "Skyrim:Concept Art") • [Credits](/wiki/Skyrim:Credits "Skyrim:Credits") | |

***The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim Anniversary Edition*** is a comprehensive edition of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") that bundles together the [Special Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition "Skyrim:Special Edition") and a total of 74 [Creations](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") which contain over 500+ new individual elements such as quests, items, armor, houses, and more. It was released on November 11, 2021 to commemorate the 10th anniversary of Skyrim's release.

Anniversary Edition is available in digital format on PC, Xbox One, Xbox Series X|S, PlayStation 4, PlayStation 5, Nintendo Switch, and Nintendo Switch 2. It is also available in physical format for Xbox One and PlayStation 4. Owners of Anniversary Edition or Special Edition on Xbox Series X|S and PlayStation 5 can download a free optimization update with enhanced graphics and faster loading times. Owners of Special Edition on any platform can purchase the Anniversary Upgrade separately, which contains the Creation Club content at reduced cost.

## New Content

Below is a list of the 26 new Creations included with the Anniversary Edition. For the full list of all Creations included, see the **[Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")** page.

- **[Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Plate")**
- **[Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragon_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragon Plate")**

- **[Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup")**
- **[Bloodchill Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor")**

- **[Farming](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming")**

## Notes

- The cover features text written in the [Dragon Language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language"). It reads:
  - Naal Tuz Naal Lah Naal Vulom (By sword by magic by darkness)
  - Naal Thuum Zeim Men Eruvos (by shout through many years)
  - Do Hungaar Mu Los (of heroism we are)
  - Gro Wah Keizaal Ulse (bound to Skyrim for eternity)
- Physical copies of the Anniversary Edition contain a disc with the Special Edition and a redeemable code to download the Anniversary Upgrade.
- Downloading the Anniversary Upgrade changes the tint of the Imperial Dragon emblem on the main menu from silver to gold.
- In addition to the new Creations, many already-released Creations received updates to coincide with the Anniversary Edition's release. The focus of most of these updates was to remove the high number of quests that would automatically be added to your journal upon leaving [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") (or upon installation for existing saves). As a result, much of the new content can be discovered organically through gameplay.

# Skyrim:Anoriath

## Overview

Anoriath

Anoriath defending himself

**Anoriath**, a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [scout](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatScout "Skyrim:CombatScout") and hunter, owns a vendor stall in the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") market, and is co-owner of [the Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman") with his brother [Elrindir](/wiki/Skyrim:Elrindir "Skyrim:Elrindir"). He played a part in the amusing tale of how the combination of shop and pub got its name, although only his brother will tell it. He is one of the targets of a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") [assassination contract](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Anoriath "Skyrim:Kill Anoriath").

From 8am to 7pm, Anoriath operates his butcher's stall, selling many types of meat. He claims to hunt every day, but once he closes the stall he heads to The Drunken Huntsman, where he eventually sleeps.

Anoriath wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothes") with a pair of [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers") and a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") supplemented with twenty [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). He carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Anoriath "Skyrim:Kill Anoriath")**: Kill Anoriath in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Kill Anoriath

As with most Dark Brotherhood targets, you may speak to him before you kill him. He will tell you:

:   *"You're making me... nervous. Is there something you need?"*

You can answer him in three ways:

| Your Options | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Only cowards hunt animals. True game walks on two legs.** | *"Are you... threatening me? Walk away fool. It's not worth it."* | Walks away |
| **I am the predator. You are my prey.** | *"Is that so? We shall see, villain. We shall see!"* | Becomes hostile and attacks |
| **(Remain silent)** | *"Well now, you are a strange one. You remind me a bit of myself, when I'm stalking a deer. I'm not quite sure how I feel about that..."* | Walks away |

If he walks away, attempting conversation with him will only have him say:

:   *"I find your presence... unnerving. Please depart."*

## Dialogue

Upon greeting him, he will say:

:   *"Do you hunt? The plains outside Whiterun are ripe*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *with game."*

When he is running his stall, he will also advertise his goods to passersby, saying:

:   *"The finest cuts, fresh from the wilds!"*
:   *"Chops and steaks fit for a jarl! Come and see my selection of finest-quality meats!"*
:   *"Tired of bread and stew? Had enough of fish and fowl? Treat yourself and your kin to a choice cut of steak or a tender rack of ribs!"*

Talking to him there will have him claim:

:   *"You should try the venison. It's delicious."*

When you end conversation with him, he can say:

:   *"Good hunting."*
:   *"Remember, I've got the freshest meat in all of Whiterun."*
:   *"Right. Till next time."*

If you meet him at the Drunken Huntsman, he can say:

:   *"Need something? Talk to my brother, Elrindir."*
:   *"Remember, I've got the freshest meat in all of Whiterun."*

While Anoriath is at his stall, you may ask him if he kills all this game himself:

:   **Did you kill all this game yourself?**
:   *"Oh, yes. Hunting is my great passion. That's why my brother and I opened a shop to sell hunting supplies. It's the Drunken Huntsman, down by the main gate. He tends the store, and I've got this stall."*

## Rumors

Should you ask, Elrindir will reveal how he and Anoriath came up with the name "Drunken Huntsman":

:   *"Yes, I hear that question often. My brother Anoriath and I came up with it one night after consuming... rather too much mead. After our drinks, we went out for a moonlight hunt. We got separated, and in his drunken state my brother mistook me for a deer. He shot an arrow that pierced my... well, my rump. After such a memorable adventure, we knew we had the name for our shop."*

## Conversations

Anoriath can be seen having random conversations with his brother Elrindir, as outlined below:

:   **Anoriath**: *"I've been thinking of hunting out beyond the boundaries of Whiterun hold."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"Again? You just had an "extended hunt" last month. To the Pine Forest, wasn't it."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"That was three days. I'm thinking more like three weeks."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"Three weeks? You're mad! You can't keep the stand closed for that long!"*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Why not? Business has been terrible. Most folk would rather hunt their own meat than buy ours."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"Nonsense. That's just an excuse for you to avoid working, and "commune with the greenwood like our fathers of old" and blah blah."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Congratulations, brother. You've been living in Skyrim so long, you've become a Nord."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"At least the Nords don't shirk their responsibilities."*

:   **Elrindir**: *"Our stock of arrows is running a bit low."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"All right. I'll fletch some more when I get the time."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"Good. I'll do the same. We've still got plenty of shafts from that Riverwood shipment."*

:   **Anoriath**: *"It's been two months, and no word from father."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"Don't worry, brother. I'm sure he's fine. We've waited longer before receiving a letter."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Might be worth riding out to Solitude, see if a messenger ship's come in."*
:   **Elrindir**: *"If it'll put your mind at ease, then I agree. But not now, all right? We need the business from the stand."*

He may also talk with various customers about his goods at the market:

:   **[Nazeem](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazeem "Skyrim:Nazeem")**: *"Do you have anything even remotely fresh?"*
:   **Anoriath**: *"I can assure you, it's all fresh. I hunt the game myself, every day."*
:   **Nazeem**: *"Hmm. As you say."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Maybe you'd like to try the horker? Or some beef?"*
:   **Nazeem**: *"You don't prepare the meat with any of those strange Elven spices, do you?"*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Ahhhh... No, no Elven spices. Just some salt, to preserve it. You're not afraid of salt, are you?"*
:   **Nazeem**: *"I'm not "afraid" of anything. I simply prefer quality merchandise. No, no this meat won't do at all. Too much fat, and it all smells... wrong."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Suit yourself, then. The woods are that way. Outside the walls, walk straight ahead. Can't miss them. Good luck on your hunt."*
:   **Nazeem**: *"Good day."*

:   **Anoriath**: *"Ah, [Olfina](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane"). How may I help you?"*
:   **Olfina**: *"Got any sausages? I'm cooking a special breakfast for a friend, and they're his favorite."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Would your good friend be named [Jon](/wiki/Skyrim:Jon_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Jon Battle-Born"), by any chance? I've spied the two of you talking quite intimately."* **OR** *"Glad to see you're making new friends. I know Jon's death was hard on you."* (if Jon is dead)
:   **Olfina**: *"Best you forget whatever you think you saw, elf. Such idle talk can prove hazardous to one's health."*

:   **[Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda")**: *"I've got a recipe for venison stew that I want to try out. Will you have venison anytime soon?"*
:   **Anoriath**: *"Certainly. I'll be sure to bring some back for you the next time I go hunting."*
:   **Ysolda**: *"Make it quick, and there might be a bowl of hot stew in it for you."*

:   **Anoriath**: *"I don't suppose you're going to buy something this time?"*
:   **[Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin")**: *"Just browsin' today. If the gods be kind, someone will take mercy on me and spare a few septims."*
:   **Anoriath**: *"If they do, promise you'll actually purchase something for once."*
:   **Brenuin**: *"By Ysmir, I will. Gods know it's been too long since I tasted real meat."*

## Notes

- Anoriath was originally supposed to physically hunt outside of Whiterun. Dialogue was even recorded for him in case you spoke to him: *"Oh! You startled me. I wasn't expecting company out here."* and *"Shhh. You'll scare the deer."* However, the dialogue has been deliberately blocked from being accessed by being attached to a nonexistent quest stage, and Anoriath has no AI packages that take him outside of the city, despite Nazir's Dark Brotherhood contract specifying you could kill him while hunting and not incur a bounty.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, originally altered this. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=15588)) A new hunting AI package was created for Anoriath, and the nonsense condition was removed from his two lines, making them available again. However, the only suitable "hunt and patrol" package to base Anoriath's on was inextricably linked to making the actor who uses it hostile to everything in sight. As such, this created a larger issue and the change was reverted in version 2.0.5a. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=16554))

## Bugs

- Anoriath has the [investment](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") dialogue, allowing you to pay him 500 gold to invest in his store. However, investing in him has no actual effect—his gold is not permanently increased because his merchant chest does not contain the `PerkInvestorStoreUpgrade` bonus gold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, addresses this issue. He can no longer be invested in.
- Anoriath owns [Fralia Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Fralia_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Fralia Gray-Mane")'s merchant chest when it doesn't belong to him.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Two of Anoriath's dialogue topics don't make sense when he isn't at his stand offering services.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.9, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund") |
| Reward: | [Ghostblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghostblade "Skyrim:Ghostblade") |
| ID: | dunAnsilvundQST |
| Suggested Level: | 8 |

Lu'ah Al-Skaven in the Ansilvund Burial Chambers

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").
2. Make your way through the ruin.
3. Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven").

### Fjori and Holgeir

During your adventures, you may come across the rare book *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*, the tragic tale of a huntress and a warlord who fell in love fighting each other during a battle between forest clans. They fought to a standstill until her sword broke his axe and his shield dulled her blade, and their love was so obvious that the battle instantly ended and brought peace to the forest. When winter came, a snake bit [Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Holgeir "Skyrim:Holgeir"), and [Fjori](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjori "Skyrim:Fjori") obtained an elixir from [Akavir](/wiki/Lore:Akavir "Lore:Akavir") to cure the poison. While she was giving the healing elixir to her loved one, instantly curing him, the snake bit her as well, and Holgeir couldn't save her. Out of grief, he built an ancient tomb and took his own life, hoping to rejoin Fjori in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").

The Nordic ruin of Ansilvund is hidden in the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains"), far north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), and can be reached by following an unmarked path east of [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"). Near the entrance you will find the book about Fjori and Holgeir on a table, protected by a hostile [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer"), hinting at unsolved mysteries inside.

### The Excavation Site

Enslaved Draugr

The first area of Ansilvund is an excavation site, complete with mining equipment, wooden structures, and narrow tunnels. Unfortunately, the site is guarded by hordes of hostile [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock#Conjurers "Skyrim:Warlock"), [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock#Necromancers "Skyrim:Warlock"), and [mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Mage#Fire_Mages "Skyrim:Fire Mage") accompanied by a huge number of leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") enemies, so be prepared for a long trek. Through the cobwebbed room, if you are undetected, you will witness the unusual sight of two draugr [mining](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") the blocked path with a seated warlock overseeing their efforts. Obviously enslaved by the warlock, the two draugr will keep hammering on the wall, for reasons unknown. You can either sneak past them or use the [oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") on the floor to your advantage, even if it will alert all enemies lurking in the surrounding areas. Regardless of your choice, proceed forward through the door. In the third room, a disembodied voice will echo through the tunnels with a warning:

***"I am Lu'ah Al-Skaven. Who are you to disrupt my work? Begone, or I will add you to my army of the dead!"***

At the top of the planks, there is another patrolling warlock, and after that is a room with three seated warlocks having a discussion beside a cooking pot and an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"). Their conversation provides a bit of explanation on the hard-working draugr enemies you encountered in the previous room:

**Female**: *"I think it's sweet Lu'ah is so worked up over her dead soldier..."*
**Male**: *"Yeah, but raising Draugr to take on both the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")? That's just crazy."*
**Female**: *"True, but I'm not going to be the one to try to oppose her..."*

If the three warlocks detect you, you will have no choice but to battle them. Proceed forward to the third room, where a beam of blue light will shine down at the corpses, immediately reanimating them. The voice will once again be heard, saying, *"Rise from your graves to defeat this worm!"* Defeat the four draugr enemies and proceed to the next room, but beware the [ceiling spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ceiling_Spikes "Skyrim:Ceiling Spikes") trap. Head to the upper level and take the western path through more narrow tunnels until you reach a room with a conjurer and a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach"). Defeat the foes and examine the area to the north where you will find four rotating pillars and a handle. For a bit of investigation, search the table below the pillars for the unique book *[Lu-ah's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu-ah%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Lu-ah's Journal")*.

### Lu'ah and Saeel

The journal tells the story of yet another tragic love affair, this time between a conjurer named [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") and her husband Saeel. According to the journal, Saeel died fighting for the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") against the [Thalmor](/wiki/Lore:Thalmor "Lore:Thalmor") twenty-five years ago. During her grieving period, Lu'ah learned the story of Fjori and Holgeir, which led her to Ansilvund, hoping to transfer Saeel's soul to Holgeir's body. In order to reach the burial chamber, she started reanimating the dead, using them as vessels to clear the way.

The puzzle in front of you can be solved in two ways, as it is based on the story of Fjori and Holgeir. The book is conveniently placed next to Lu'ah's Journal and, when examined closely, will reveal the following sentences related to the puzzle:

*As the **Eagle** finds its mates, so too did Fjori find hers in Holgeir, and a time of peace came to the clans of the forest.*
*But the **Snake** came and bit Holgeir, its venom seeping deep into the wound.*
*A **Whale** greeted Fjori's view as she came over the snow-covered mountains to the coast.*
*But the **Snake** bit Fjori as she poured the last drop into Holgeir's mouth, and fatigued from her journey, she joined the ancestors immediately.*

From left to right, turn the pillars to match the words in the book. Alternatively, an easier solution is available, as the correct symbols can be found behind the table, mostly overgrown but still visible. With the pillars in place, pull the handle and the door to [Ansilvund Burial Chambers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund#Ansilvund_Burial_Chambers "Skyrim:Ansilvund") will be accessible.

### Burial Chambers

*"Rise from your graves to defeat this worm!"*

The Chambers area starts off with a crypt filled to the brink with traps, all triggered by [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"), so navigate your way to the intersection. Behind the locked gate sits a locked boss-leveled chest and a chain that controls all traps in the area, including the [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") you may encounter in the southern tunnel. The next room is large and is divided into two levels. Make sure to read the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book *[2920, Sun's Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")* found on a booby-trapped pedestal across the room from the entrance, then locate the four sarcophagi in the southeastern area and claim the [Ansilvund Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Key "Skyrim:Ansilvund Key") from the pedestal. As soon as you take the key, a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") will trigger, and five draugr enemies will burst out of their coffins while Lu'ah Al-Skaven speaks once again: *"I shall have vengeance for the death of my husband. Rise!"* Defeat the enemies, then head upstairs and use the key to unlock several gates until you reach a wooden door. The next area sees another enslaved draugr hacking away on a wall, overseen by another warlock. Make your way up and through a door until you end up on a narrow bridge with more pressure plates, designed purely to push you off the ledge. Beware of the attacking draugr and make your way into a crypt where another ray of blue light will reanimate another wave of undead enemies while Lu'ah will speak once again:

***"I could not raise him, but I will raise an army to avenge his defilement!"***

Proceed forward and beware of even more traps until you reach a large iron door, the very entrance to the main burial hall, the location sought out by Lu'ah, and the place where she hoped to reanimate her husband through the body of Holgeir. Apparently, she failed.

### Showdown

Fjori and Holgeir

*"Thank you for releasing us from her spell."*

The burial chamber is large and has a dead draugr lying on an altar, right in front of two closed sarcophagi, as well as a dead skeleton on the floor and several [oil lanterns](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Oil_Slicks.2FOil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Traps") hanging from the ceiling. As you approach the altar, Lu'ah Al-Skaven will appear from the shadows, saying:

***"They burned his body before I could raise him... it should have been returned to me... You will not stop me from killing those who wage this pointless war!"***

With these words the two sarcophagi will burst open and the mummified remains of Fjori and Holgeir will come rushing out, now slaves for the residing, vengeful conjurer. At the same time, Lu'ah Al-Skaven will re-animate the skeleton on the floor, so you will face four enemies at once. Fjori and Holgeir are both strong draugr enemies, and Lu'ah will shower you with a wide array of spells, including [Ice Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Storm "Skyrim:Ice Storm") and [Ice Spike](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Spike "Skyrim:Ice Spike") along with the expected conjurer spells and a [Grand Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Grand Healing") spell for restoration. If you kill either Fjori and Holgeir, Lu'ah will immediately revive them, so go directly after Lu'ah. When she is dead, Fjori and Holgeir will fall to the ground, and blue rays of light will emerge from their bodies. With the curse finally broken, the ghosts of the two lovers will emerge behind the altar, and they will wholeheartedly thank you:

**Fjori**: *"Thank you for releasing us from her spell."*
**Holgeir**: *"Now we can rest in peace once again. Come Fjori, my love..."*
**Fjori**: *"Take this with our gratitude."*

They will both disappear and your reward will be ready on the table behind them: the unique sword [Ghostblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghostblade "Skyrim:Ghostblade"). Make sure to pick up the [Unusual Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), then loot Lu'ah Al-Skaven for [her key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah%27s_Key "Skyrim:Lu'ah's Key") and unlock the northern door. Inside you'll find a boss-leveled chest, the spell tome *[Transmute Mineral Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Transmute_Mineral_Ore "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore")*, and a hefty amount of [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). Lastly, find the *[Imperial Condolences](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Condolences "Skyrim:Imperial Condolences")* letter on the table for a final explanation on what drove Lu'ah Al-Skaven into insanity and why she formed her army of undead allies.

| 100 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 10, 19, 20, 30, 50, 51, 52, 55, 56, 57, 80, 90, 95.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunAnsilvundQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunAnsilvundQST`.

## Overview

Ansilvund

**Ansilvund** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") led by [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven"). It contains two zones: *[Ansilvund Excavation](#Ansilvund_Excavation)* and *[Ansilvund Burial Chambers](#Ansilvund_Burial_Chambers)*.

The ruins are the remains of the tomb built by [Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Holgeir "Skyrim:Holgeir") in memory of [Fjori](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjori "Skyrim:Fjori"), as described in the book *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*.

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in Ansilvund.
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The entrance is guarded by a leveled necromancer, usually found near the [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), inside the ruined tower, or mining ore. In one of the cooking pots is a dead [mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"), with a wooden table nearby which has a copy of *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*, two [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") on top. There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") a short distance north of the cooking spit. Inside the tower is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks, and a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on it. Beside the chest is a hay pile you can sleep on. An [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") is on the opposite wall, built into a table, with samples of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower, a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), and four random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). Beside the table is a bucket containing a random potion of magicka. On top of the tower is an unlocked boss chest, which can only be reached using at least two words of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). To reach it, stand on the small rocky outcropping almost directly above the excavation entrance and face west toward the lowest part of the tower. Alternatively, you can ride a horse to the top of the tower. Immediately to the right of the entrance to the excavation is a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle").

### Ansilvund Excavation

The passage descends to the east, passing a wooden table on the left which holds two [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), two [leather helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), and a leveled [blacksmith's potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion"). At the bottom, as you enter a chamber with a rock pillar surrounded by scaffolding and a raised walkway, there is an iron ore vein on the right. Under the scaffolding, to the south, is a path that ends with a draugr standing guard near some dead [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), with a ledge above that will provide a shortcut back from the final zone. The only way to proceed is up the ramp found on the north side, around the back of the structure. There is a leveled draugr patrolling the wooden walkway. Follow the path around the pillar and along the walkway. Ahead is a ramp leading up, and a passage continues ahead. Before following the passage, climb the ramp to a small landing to find a novice-locked chest.

The passage continues heading east, passing stacks of crates and posts that are supporting the ceiling. As you pass under a wooden slatted section, you can peer through and see a leveled necromancer sitting watching two draugr [mining](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") the back wall. At least one of these draugr is leveled. The floor is coated with an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"), and an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hangs above. There is a stack of barrels against the east wall with a random potion of magicka on top; however, it may become dislodged during the skirmish. To the left of where the draugr were working, next to the passage you just come through, is an adept-locked chest, beside another stack of barrels. There are numerous pickaxes throughout the site, and several of the barrels contain ingredients.

There is a passage to the left of the first barrels continuing east. The passage twists and turns before you come to a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap on the left, which can be used against a conjurer on a platform above you. The path onward is around the corner, on the other side of the pressure plate. The next room has several growths of both [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungi. There is a wooden ramp on the left up to a platform where the mage is found. There is a table with two [mummified draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") and a random potion on top. Beside the table is an apprentice-locked chest, and at the other end of the platform there is a small table and chair, with a random poison on the table. Ahead, there is a draugr patrolling above the next passage, which can either be killed from here with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") or ranged magic or left until later.

If you wish to skip a section of the ruins, the area with the draugr can be reached by standing on the table with the dead draugr and using two words of the Whirlwind Sprint shout. (One word is not enough, while three words will send you through to the other side of the hallway.) Otherwise, proceed back down the ramp and continue along the passage heading east. However, move cautiously, as there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") which triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") in the hallway ahead. As you pass the mace, the ground will shake, and you will hear:

|  |
| --- |
| **I am Lu'ah Al-Skaven. Who are you to disrupt my work? Begone, or I will add you to my army of the dead!** |

This chamber is brightly lit by a brazier in the center of the room, behind which is a platform where you will see another mage and draugr. You will need to pass under the platform to find the ramp up. The front of the platform has a long table with another mummified draugr, while to the rear are several crates, barrels, and five more lootable mummified draugr on the ground. There is also a ramp descending to the south into a chamber containing three leveled mages standing or sitting around a central campfire. On your right, on the platform are three unowned bedrolls, with several crates and food sacks to the right of the ramp. Around the fire on the ground are many bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and against the opposite wall is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top. Under the platform are many crates and barrels with several ingredients and foodstuffs on top, including: two [taproots](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), a bowl of [Spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), several pieces of cheese, some [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and some [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Hanging under the platform is a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid").

Continue to the west into some catacombs, where numerous draugr are slumbering. As you enter, you again hear the voice:

|  |
| --- |
| **Rise from your graves to defeat this worm.** |

The draugr will now rise, which can lead to a challenging fight. Once you've dealt with them, you will see a passage on your right. A short distance past this is a cave-in, with an unlocked chest among the rubble. Return to the passage and follow it. Before entering the next room, take note of the circular floor, and the [ceiling spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ceiling_Spikes "Skyrim:Ceiling Spikes"). Skirt around this area to the wooden stairway. Two large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") are tucked away under the stairs, and three random filled [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") are also in the room: one on a sideboard, and two in stands to the right. At the top of the stairs, an apprentice-locked chest is straight ahead, a sideboard to the right has three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") on top, and to the left are two more large urns and a food sack. A narrow balcony to the northwest holds a potion and a large coin purse. Another draugr can be observed mining down below to the west, and either left or dealt with by ranged magic or bow. Beside the draugr is a small round table with a random empty soul gem and two random potions. Stairs in front of you lead down into this room, and at the bottom, a passage heads south before taking a couple turns.

Descending deeper underground, continue along until you reach a turn to the left by some wooden planking. Here you should take care, as there is a tripwire which triggers some rocks to fall from the right. Looking around, you will see a wooden platform supporting a stone bridge spanning the room. A draugr, a random [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"), and a conjurer are all guarding this area. Before heading down to the wooden platform, look to the right for some candles on a section of stone statuary. A large coin purse is behind this stone structure. Head up the incline on the far side of the room to find four [puzzle pillars](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle "Skyrim:Traps") and an associated lever on one side of the bridge, and an iron portcullis on the other.

On the table below the puzzle are three random potions, *[Lu-ah's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu-ah%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Lu-ah's Journal")*, and another copy of *Of Fjori and Holgeir*. The book contains clues to solve the pillar puzzle. The solution can also be seen carved into the wall behind the table, below the pillars, but the symbols are partially obscured by rubble and weeds. The solution from left to right is **Eagle—Snake—Whale—Snake**. Activate the pillars to arrange them in the correct order, then pull the lever to open the portcullis and proceed across the bridge. There is an additional trap on the bridge; the middle section has a pressure plate that activates a [flamethrower statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") trap from the right. In the next room, an unlocked chest is in a darkened alcove to the right, and the doors straight ahead lead to **Ansilvund Burial Chambers**.

### Ansilvund Burial Chambers

The first of six successive pressure plates is found a few steps into this area, hidden under vines. The first, third, and fifth trigger [dart traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap"), while the second, fourth, and sixth trigger swinging blade traps. All pressure plates are fairly obvious and can be avoided by sticking to the right-hand wall, then moving to the left between the fifth and sixth plates. There are several [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") in this zone. Straight ahead to the east is an adept-locked gate. On the ground in front of the gate lies a skeleton with a dagger and lockpick. The gate opens to a room which contains a chest with a leveled lock. Behind this chest is a pull chain that stops any activated swinging blades, and to the right lies a dead draugr that can be looted. There is another lootable dead draugr in the upper burial space to the left of the chest. There is a seventh and final pressure plate in this area, in front of the next passage; it activates multiple swinging blades in the passage ahead. The chain in the previous room will also stop these blades, and there is another chain to stop the blades on the left-hand side at the far end of the passage. The next room is fairly large, with multiple levels. There are three [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") in a row between the two pillars in the center of the room, one of which may have one or more of the draugr lying on it dead. The pillars support a caged walkway that passes from a balcony to the south to a balcony to the north, passing a caged area. There are also three draugr patrolling here. A copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Suns' Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")* is on a [trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") pedestal, which will trigger poison darts from the pillar behind you. A large urn is nearby. To the west, eight sarcophagi are arranged around another trapped pedestal holding the [Ansilvund key](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Key "Skyrim:Ansilvund Key"). Taking the key triggers more poison darts from the pillar behind you, and all eight sarcophagi open, although only five draugr will rise. You will also hear the voice again:

|  |
| --- |
| **I shall have vengeance for the death of my husband. Rise!** |

Once you have the key, go up the stairs to find an adept-locked chest. A series of stone bridges spans the room. The Ansilvund key unlocks the first master-locked gate to the right. An unlocked chest is in this caged section of the bridge system. Continue across to the balcony to the north, where you find three large urns, and farther along the wall, a set of shelves holding two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). To the right of these is a wooden door. Behind the door is an alcove containing a few human bones, but nothing of interest. Opposite is a caged bridge with another master-locked gate that is opened using the same key as before. The bridge crosses to a small balcony, with a partially buried urn and another wooden door. Through this door is a passage that leads to a room with wooden supports, and a draugr attacking what appears to be a gold ore vein (see [bugs](#Bugs)) with their weapon. Water covers the floor in the next room, and a leveled conjurer will be patrolling on the walkway crossing above. A wooden ramp up to the next level is in the back of the cavern, to the north. At the top of the ramp, on a stone ledge to the right next to some candles, is an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

Across the stone bridge is another door, which leads back to the previous room on a walkway high above. Halfway across is a lit brazier. After the brazier, there are four more pressure plates lining the walkway. The first triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") from the left, the next two trigger two flame spout traps, and the last triggers another spiked wall from the right. Before proceeding, a leveled draugr will run out of the door ahead of you and along the walkway. If you stay where you are, the draugr will likely be killed by activating the traps as it tries to cross. Open the doors at the end of the walkway to find a leveled necromancer patrolling left to right. A random potion of magicka and two burial urns are either on or around a collapsed table on the left, at the bottom of the stairs. Straight ahead is an open area with two thrones. Upon passing the thrones, you hear Lu'ah Al-Skaven again:

|  |
| --- |
| **I could not raise him, but I will raise an army to avenge his defilement!** |

Six more draugr awaken from their slumber. Three of the alcoves by the thrones contain mummified draugr, with a large urn in front. The passage continues to the north. As the room opens up through some scrub brush, you will see a trapped pedestal straight ahead. First, notice another circular floor section with ceiling spikes. If you want to reach the pedestal, skirt around the circular floor. While there is a piece of random [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") lying on the pedestal, taking it triggers a poison dart trap from either side. Up ahead, there is a single draugr patrolling the hallway, which contains a total of three large urns and two burial urns. After several turns, the passage ends with double iron doors that lead to the final area.

Opening the doors reveals the final area of the ruins. Awaiting you is Lu'ah Al-Skaven, a powerful necromancer. Two powerful draugr or [dragon priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"), Fjori and Holgeir, will also emerge from upright sarcophagi that she controls. There are three [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") lying on the ground, any of which she may raise to aid her, and in front of her is an altar with a dead draugr and two random potions of magicka on top. Between the sarcophagi is a stone table with a built-in arcane enchanter, an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), and a plinth where the [Ghostblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghostblade "Skyrim:Ghostblade") will be placed as a reward for releasing the captive spirits of Holgeir and Fjori. After the fight, loot Lu'ah for [her key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah%27s_Key "Skyrim:Lu'ah's Key"). Next, when standing at the altar, facing back toward the entrance, notice two sets of stairs. The stairs on the right lead up to an unlocked chest buried in some rubble. The exit is up the stairs to the left. The master-locked door at the top of the stairs will be unlocked with Lu'ah's key. In the room beyond are two barrels of ingredients, several burial urns, a large urn, an unlocked boss chest, an unowned single bed, an alchemy lab, and a long wooden table with a *[Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Transmute_Mineral_Ore "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Transmute Mineral Ore")*, a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Condolences "Skyrim:Imperial Condolences") (which tells of the death of Lu'ah's husband, Saeel Al-Skaven), two random potions, and a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower on top. To the right of the table is a kettle containing two pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") that you can try the new spell on. To the left of a door on the far wall is a set of shelves holding a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a dragon's tongue flower, two random empty soul gems, a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), a set of [novice robes of conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Robes_of_Conjuration "Skyrim:Novice Robes of Conjuration"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0006b46C "Skyrim:Boots"), and four [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"). The door leads back to *Ansilvund Excavation*, opening to a passage that soon ends at a wooden spiral staircase with a barrel of ingredients and several food sacks at the bottom. At the top of the staircase is a cage with a door that requires Lu'ah's key to open. This brings you to the ledge above the dead frostbite spiders, with easy access from here to the exit.

## Notes

- To the east of the camp is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein"), and farther east is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein"). Between the two, but to the south, is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").
- If you return to the ruin after completing the eponymous quest and the location has reset, most draugr will not respawn. A small number of skeleton enemies will take their place along with the necromancers, making for a much easier path through the ruin.

## Bugs

- A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") that cannot be mined is on the wall to the right just after the room that holds the key and skill book. A draugr is attempting to mine it with a battleaxe.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Holgeir reanimated by Lu'ah may spawn as a dragon priest at sufficiently high player level, in which case he may be pushed out of bounds of the dungeon upon exiting his sarcophagus, making the fight with Lu'ah easier, but also making his loot inaccessible. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Ansilvund Excavation
- 

  Ansilvund Burial Chambers

# Skyrim:Anska

## Overview

| Anska (RefID: 000443F2) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Bandit Wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000443F2 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000443F3 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 35-441 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 100-294 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50-150 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Aggressive |
| [Protected](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs") | Yes | | |
| Voice Type | [FemaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleNord") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Player Ally Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Player_Ally_Faction "Skyrim:Player Ally Faction") | | |

Anska

Anska battling a draugr

**Anska** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") that is found in the first room of [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") and initiates the quest [A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska"). She believes her family's blood can be traced all the way back to [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor") himself, but requires [a special scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealed_Scroll "Skyrim:Sealed Scroll") contained in the ruins in order to prove it. After the completion of the related quest, she will remain in the ruins indefinitely attempting to decipher the scroll.

She wears [fur armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Armor "Skyrim:Fur Armor") and a leveled pair of [light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Light_Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), which may be up to [scaled](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled "Skyrim:Scaled") in quality. She is armed with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") that may be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") in quality and may also carry a random selection of bandit loot and gold. She casts a leveled set of spells from the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") schools, including one [armor spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_(spells) "Skyrim:Armor (spells)"), one [ward spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward "Skyrim:Ward"), at least one [healing spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restore_Health "Skyrim:Restore Health") and at least one of each type of elemental damage spell.

## Related Quests

- **[A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska")**: Help Anska trace her roots in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins").

### A Scroll For Anska

Upon greeting her, she will remark:

:   *"You look strong."*
:   **Who are you?**
:   *"I'm Anska. Are you here to help?"*
:   **Help with what?**
:   *"I've finally located [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)")'s crypt! The scroll I'm looking for just has to be here."*
:   **What do you need from me?**
:   *"Maybe you could help find it, I just know it's in here."*

You can ask more about the scroll she's looking for and other questions:

:   **What scroll?**
:   *"It's probably meaningless to you, but according to family legend it links our bloodline back to Ysgramor himself."*

:   **Vokun?**
:   *"Some old priest buried here long ago. I've been searching for his tomb for a few years now."*

:   **What kind of help do you need?**
:   *"If Vokun is as powerful as I think, I may need a little help um ... dealing ...with him."*
:   **What's in it for me?**
:   *"You can have anything except the scroll of course."*

If you decline:

:   **Sorry, I can't help.**
:   *"Oh alright. Well I'll be here for a bit if you change your mind."*

If you accept:

:   **I'll help.**
:   *"Great, with the two of us this should be easy."*

She will follow you from now on. As the two of you slay [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and explore the ruins, she may muse:

:   *"This is fun."*
:   *"Sometimes I just like to watch them burn."*

Farther into the ruins, you will find a room that leads to the catacombs; its stairway is sealed by a trapdoor, surrounded by four levers. Anska will remark:

:   *"This looks like some sort of lever puzzle. We'll have to figure out the correct order to flip them."*

If enough time has passed before you solve the puzzle, she will give you some advice:

:   *"Maybe the order has something to do with the Symbols up there."*

*"This is fun."*

Once you open the trapdoor, proceed into the catacombs. Eventually, you will see a [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") placed on a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), on which she will comment:

:   *"That gem looks suspicious to me."*

She is correct, as removing the gem will awaken the two draugr nearby. When she enters the hallway decorated with carvings, she will observe:

:   *"These wall carvings are ancient, we must be getting close."*

When you reach Vokun's throne room, the door to his sarcophagus will burst open and he will awaken. Anska will say:

:   *"That's Vokun, the guardian of the scroll. It must be just past him."*

Eliminating him will have her tell you:

:   *"Good riddance. Let's move on, the scroll must be in the next room."*

Go to the next room and she will exclaim:

:   *"There it is! On the table."*

Take the [sealed scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sealed_Scroll "Skyrim:Sealed Scroll") and hand it to a grateful Anska, who will say:
*"I cannot thank you enough for all of the help."*
Hand the scroll to her, and she will reward you with the [Conjure Flaming Familiar spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Flaming_Familiar "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Flaming Familiar"):

:   **Here is the scroll.**
:   *"And here's a little something for helping me out."*

If you ask her what the scroll says:

:   **So what does it say?**
:   *"Let me look. This is a very exciting moment for me.
    Hmm, it's encrypted. It'll take a while to figure this out."*

After you've given the scroll and completed the quest, Anska will express her gratitude to you:

:   *"Thank you again for all the help."*

## Notes

- It is possible to retrieve the scroll without her. To do so, avoid talking to her at the start of the ruins, and once Vokun is dead and you've picked up the scroll in the final chamber, she will run up to you. You can talk to her at this point and say you've "retrieved the scroll" (as if you'd agreed to help her originally), and she will hand over the Flaming Familiar spell tome, starting and finishing the quest right there.
- She has some unused dialogue: *"Looking for work?"* and *"An alchemy lab, it could be in here. It's worth a look."* Game data also indicates an option to deny her the scroll, but the wrong conditions are set, so they cannot be chosen in normal gameplay. When she thanks you for your help in retrieving the scroll, you could have refused to hand it over, to which she would have told you, *"I'm sorry, but I can't let that happen."* You could have also said that you've found this scroll, and she would have been amazed: *"Could it really be? Wow this is what I've been looking for. Can I have it? It's worthless to you, but I can pay."* If you tell her she can take it, she would have replied, *"Thank you so much, this scroll means a lot to my family. Take this for your trouble."*, but if you choose to hang onto it, she would have been angry: *"I'm sorry, I've come too far to lose it now."*
- Even after High Gate Ruins resets, Anska will not leave the dungeon and will stay inside the first chamber.
- It might be preferable to explore High Gate Ruins without accepting her quest if you are a high enough level and have followers along, as she prefers area-of-effect magic and this can anger them if they are hit by her too many times. This can lead to unending battles between Anska and the follower throughout the entire ruin, and will make completing the quest impossible (as she can't be spoken to when in the midst of a fight).
- You cannot pickpocket the Flaming Familiar spell tome from her, and if you kill her, the spell tome is also not in her inventory; the only way to get it is retrieving the scroll for her.

# Skyrim:Anton Virane

## Overview

| Voice Type | [MaleCondescending](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [During sieges, staff and family hide.](/wiki/Skyrim:During_sieges,_staff_and_family_hide. "Skyrim:During sieges, staff and family hide."); [FavorExcludedFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction "Skyrim:FavorExcludedFaction"); [JobMerchantFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:JobMerchantFaction "Skyrim:JobMerchantFaction"); [MarkarthCastleServantsFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthCastleServantsFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthCastleServantsFaction"); [MarkarthKeepFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthKeepFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthKeepFaction"); [ServicesMarkarthCastleCook](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesMarkarthCastleCook "Skyrim:ServicesMarkarthCastleCook"); [TownMarkarthFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction "Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction") | | |

Anton Virane

**Anton Virane** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes#Citizen "Skyrim:Classes") living in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). He was born in [Daggerfall](/wiki/Lore:Daggerfall "Lore:Daggerfall") in [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), which is where he learned to cook. He is the master chef working in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") with his two assistants [Rondach](/wiki/Skyrim:Rondach "Skyrim:Rondach") and [Voada](/wiki/Skyrim:Voada "Skyrim:Voada"), although he considers them both to be worthless. He is often assumed to be a native of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), an accusation which he finds offensive. He is also a close friend of [Balagog gro-Nolob](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob").

Anton wears a [chef's tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Tunic "Skyrim:Chef's Tunic") along with a [chef's hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Chef%27s_Hat "Skyrim:Chef's Hat") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#00018801 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster")**: Assume the identity of the famous [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Balagog_gro-Nolob "Skyrim:Balagog gro-Nolob") in an effort to assassinate the Emperor.

### Recipe for Disaster

During [Recipe for Disaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipe_for_Disaster "Skyrim:Recipe for Disaster"), you will be sent to Anton to discover the identity of the Gourmet, then your task will be to kill him when you're done. When you greet Anton, he'll say:

:   *"Yes, yes, for the hundredth time, I am a Breton. I was born in High Rock. And then I came here. I am not a Reachman!"*
:   *"Who are you? What do you want?"*
:   **The Gourmet. Who is he? Where is he?**
:   *"The... the Gourmet? Never! I don't know what led you here, but nothing will betray my trust. I'll take the secret of the Gourmet's identity to my grave."*
:   **For the Dark Brotherhood, that can be easily arranged.**
:   *"The Dark Brotherhood? Now... now wait a minute. Let's not get hasty. I mean, surely my friend wouldn't want me to endanger my own life. Right? Look, his name is Balagog gro-Nolob. He's an Orc! The Gourmet's an Orc! He's staying at the [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"). That's all I know! Now... now you'll let me go. Right?"*

You'll now have a few options:

| Topic | Dialogue | Response |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Of course, Anton. Thank you. (Lie)** | *"Okay. All right. Wonderful. You're welcome! I'll just be on my way, then..."* | Anton walks away |
| **I'm afraid not. Loose ends, and all that.** | *"No. Oh, please no..."* | Anton runs away |
| **(Remain Silent)** | *"So... we're done?"* | Anton walks away |

## Dialogue

When you approach him for the first time, Anton will make it clear to you that he is not a native of the Reach:

:   *"Before you say anything, no, I am not from the Reach."*
:   **You're not from the Reach?**
:   *"No. I'm a Breton from High Rock, and I refuse to be mistaken for a filthy native. I don't care if we share the same ancestors, these people are savages. Half of them are [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") barbarians, and have you seen what they eat? What have I done for the gods to take me so far from my beloved Daggerfall?"*
:   **So you're from Daggerfall, then?**
:   *"Yes. The finest court in all of High Rock. You think politics here are something? Well, we Bretons invented politics. That is where I learned to cook, and where I belong. Not here, with all these dogs."*

His greetings can be:

:   *"I have meals to cook for the entire castle and almost no help."*
:   *"The Jarl gives me two incompetent assistants. Worthless."*

## Conversations

He can often be seen yelling at his workers:

:   **Anton Virane:** *"Voada, you spilled laundry water in the soup pot again! Do I need to cut off your fingers to teach you a lesson?"*
:   **Rondach:** *"You touch her, and I swear it'll be your fingers that go missing, you stupid Breton!"*
:   **Anton Virane:** *"What was that?"*
:   **Voada:** *"Now now, brother. Arnoit*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *is just being his usual gloomy self, he didn't mean it, did you Arnoit*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*? You're just being silly again."*
:   **Anton Virane:** *"Whatever. Just get back to work. Now."*

:   **Anton Virane:** *"Filthy natives. Get to work. We have meals to prepare and no time to prepare them!"*
:   **Voada:** *"Right away, sir!"*
:   **Rondach:** *"Always another big meal to cook. Figures."*
:   **Anton Virane:** *"Move it. Get to work. Get to work!"*

## Notes

- If you spare Anton Virane during Recipe for Disaster, [Festus Krex](/wiki/Skyrim:Festus_Krex "Skyrim:Festus Krex") will be disappointed, and say *"Good, good. And you've got the Writ of Passage too, I see, so that's done. But why? Why, pray tell, have I received word that Anton Virane is still walking around Markarth, hale and healthy as the day he was born? Back to Markarth with you! Virane must be silenced! He's a potential witness, you witless dagger jabber!"*

## Bugs

- When talking to Anton Virane during Recipe for Disaster, you can exit dialogue before telling him you are going to kill him, then restart dialogue with him and repeat the intimidation check to get additional Speech experience. This can be repeated as often as you like to level your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Anuriel

## Overview

| Anuriel (RefID: 00019DEE) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Race | [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Monk](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk "Skyrim:Monk") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019DEE | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013349 |
