| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionRift](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift "Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift"); [Mistveil Keep Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep_Faction "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep Faction"); [Ruling Government](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruling_Government "Skyrim:Ruling Government"); [Sons of Skyrim Government](/wiki/Skyrim:Sons_of_Skyrim_Government "Skyrim:Sons of Skyrim Government"); [TownRiftenFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction "Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction") | | |

Anuriel

**Anuriel** is a [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") and the [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") to [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). She is usually found at the Jarl's side in [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") and will sleep from midnight to 8am in her bedroom just beyond the doorway to the inner part of the Keep. She is the girlfriend of [Unmid Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmid_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Unmid Snow-Shod"), and you can overhear a conversation between the two about sneaking out for a "training" session. Should the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") take control of Riften and have Jarl Laila [replaced](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar"), Anuriel will be exiled to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings").

Once the Jarl grants you permission, Anuriel can sell you a house called [Honeyside](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeyside "Skyrim:Honeyside") in the city for 8,000 gold. In order to get permission you must complete the quest [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand").

If you side with the Imperial Legion in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), you will be sent by [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") to find material you could use to attempt to blackmail her to obtain information that could assist in the Imperial takeover of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"). In the process, it is discovered that Anuriel is actually a [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") infiltrator put in place by Maven Black-Briar to manipulate Jarl Laila into defending Maven's interests and keep her blind to the activity of the Thieves Guild.

Anuriel wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#000cee80 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#000cee82 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). She is equipped with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality, and carries a selection of [upper-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Imperial)")**: Use a corrupt steward to gain intelligence on the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"Welcome to Mistveil Keep. I'm Jarl Laila's steward, Anuriel."*
:   *"As Riften's Steward I'm afraid I can provide only limited assistance, but speak your mind."*
:   *"If you're here to report any instances of corruption, be confident that we're handling these rumors accordingly."*

Greetings when exiled:

:   *"I'm afraid my days as the steward of Riften has come to an end."*
:   *"The Imperials now control Riften and have placed Maven Black-Briar on the Jarl's throne."*
:   *"Perhaps the Stormcloaks might rally to take back Riften one day. Only time will tell."*

When spoken to:

:   **What do you do around here?**
:   *"As steward, I serve as an intermediary between the Jarl and her subjects. I also handle the less important and day-to-day policies that effect daily life in Riften. Lately I've had my hands full suppressing these ridiculous accusations of corruption in the keep."*

    :   **What are the rumors of corruption you mentioned?**
    :   *"There are those that believe the Jarl does nothing for this city... that it's corrupt and run by the Black-Briar family. I can assure you that this is entirely false. We are fully in control of everything."*

:   **Tell me about the Thieves Guild.**
:   *"I'd hardly call them a Guild. More like unorganized rabble. In fact, I wouldn't say they were a threat at all. No, our resources should be spent on preparations for invasion."*

Her goodbye:

:   *"You're welcome in Riften as long as you continue to obey our laws."*

### Compelling Tribute

:   *"Not here. Come with me. Stay close and the guards will leave you alone."*

She will lead you back into her room:

:   *"I suppose you're here to extort something from me? Is that it? Well, what is it you want?"*

:   :   **You rebels are doing a fine job destroying yourselves. Soldiers running errands?**
    :   *"So. You're an Imperial spy... Interesting... I have no strong love for the Stormcloaks but I can't say I'm all that fond of the Empire, either. This war of yours makes it difficult for a resourceful woman to advance her interests. Perhaps we can find a way for both of us to prosper from this unfortunate discovery?"*

:   :   **What if this letter were made public?**
    :   *"It would ruin me. I have a good thing going here. The Jarl benefits from my more creative arrangements as well, though it'd be impossible for her to admit that. Laila is a simple and traditional woman. Which makes it easy to manipulate her, but impossible to regain her graces once offended. Look. Perhaps we could come to some kind of agreement?"*

Either option leads to:

:   **What kind of agreement did you have in mind?**
:   *"What if I told you about a large shipment of gold and weapons?"*
:   **Go on, I'm listening.**
:   *"Oh, no. I'm no fool. You'll learn what you need to know once we've come to an agreement."*
:   **How much are we talking about?**
:   *"Enough to make a significant difference in the war."*
:   **And what about something for me, right now? (Persuade)**
:   *"Well I... I suppose I'm not much left a choice in the matter, am I? Very well. I trust a hefty purse of septims will suffice?"*
:   **All right, it's a deal. Where can I find this shipment?**
:   *"They're taking it by wagon to Windhelm. If you hurry, you'll catch them before they get far. It'll be a fairly slow moving caravan. The shipment is quite heavy, and guarded by many men. Now, let's pretend we never had this discussion."*

## Conversations

Unmid may discuss the jarl's safety with Anuriel:

:   **Unmid**: *"Anuriel, would you please stop declaring that the city is safe for the Jarl to roam? You and I both know that isn't true."*
:   **Anuriel**: *"I would never knowingly place Laila in danger, you know that too. Why do you always question my judgment? You don't trust me."*
:   **Unmid**: *"I trust you, I'm just concerned about her safety. That's all. Don't be angry with me."*
:   **Anuriel**: *"I'm not angry with you. Tell you what, lover. Meet me in my chambers later and we can discuss the situation in private."*

Anuriel can also be seen talking with Unmid about a "combat training" session. However, she will sound unusually seductive:

:   **Anuriel**: *"Unmid, my sweet. Are we still meeting later for... combat training?"*
:   **Unmid**: *"Of course. Your training isn't complete yet."*
:   **Anuriel**: *"I look forward to it then."*

Laila can regularly be seen discussing court matters with her steward Anuriel:

:   **Laila**: *"Anuriel, a word please."*
:   **Anuriel**: *"Yes, my lady?"*
:   **Laila**: *"It's been brought to my attention that the poison known as [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") may be present in our city. What do you know of this?"*
:   **Anuriel**: *"I believe it to be a falsehood perpetrated by the Empire in order to weaken the citizen's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *confidence in your ability to rule."*
:   **Laila**: *"Excellent, then they'll*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *be no need to devote any resources to stopping it. Thank you, Anuriel. That will be all."*

:   **Anuriel**: *"My lady, Maven Black-Briar has sent word that she requires your seal in order to expand her shipments into [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind")."*
:   **Laila**: *"But of course! Tell her she'll have it. Maven is one of the few people I can trust and I'd be delighted to give her my blessing."*
:   **Anuriel**: *"Yes, my lady. I will pass the good news on to her."*

## Unused Dialogue

- Anuriel was supposed to tell you about the Black-Briar family when asked; however, the conditions for the topic will never be met, so her praise will never be heard:
   **Tell me about the Black-Briar family.**
   *"Maven Black-Briar is the owner of the largest and most profitable business in all Skyrim, the Black-Briar Meadery. We're pleased to have her in Riften. She brings stability, opportunities for employment and strategic value to our city."*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

## Notes

- Even though Anuriel is a Thieves Guild infiltrator planted by Maven Black-Briar, if the Imperials win the war, she will be exiled to the Palace of the Kings instead of moving to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").

Anwen

**Anwen** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") of [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella"). She can be found in the inner sanctum of the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

She becomes available for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") after [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

She wears [hooded monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Monk Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_the_Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Key to the Temple of Dibella") to the temple of Dibella, a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_the_Dibella_Inner_Sanctum "Skyrim:Key to the Dibella Inner Sanctum") to the inner sanctum, and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She also knows a few spells, specifically [conjure familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Conjure Familiar"), [flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames"), and the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spells [heal other](/wiki/Skyrim:Heal_Other "Skyrim:Heal Other") and [fast healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing").

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember")**: Find your lost friend, [Sam](/wiki/Skyrim:Sam_Guevenne "Skyrim:Sam Guevenne"), as you recover from a bad hangover.

### A Night To Remember

She will refuse to speak to you until you clean up the mess:

:   *"I have no words. Talk to Anwen*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*."*
:   *"The temple is still not clean. Get to it."* **(shared with Senna and Orla)**

## Bugs

- When married, Anwen may remain at the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella") even when you ask to move to another place. Because there are no beds in the temple, it is impossible to get the [Lover's Comfort](/wiki/Skyrim:Lover%27s_Comfort "Skyrim:Lover's Comfort") bonus.
  - If [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed, adopt a child, and move her to your house, this may fix it.[*verification needed*]

Aphia Velothi

**Aphia Velothi** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerRestorationJourneyman "Skyrim:TrainerRestorationJourneyman") living in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). She offers common-level [training](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"). She used to be a [Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple") priest, which is how she met [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius"), who was brought to her for care while he was overcoming depression. She eventually married Crescius, and left the Temple over a disagreement with [Elder Othreloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Othreloth "Skyrim:Elder Othreloth") regarding the current status of the [Tribunal](/wiki/Lore:Tribunal "Lore:Tribunal") (Othreloth refers to them as the "false Tribunal"), and she is no longer welcome there. She is worried her husband's obsession with [his great-grandfather](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Gratian_Caerellius "Bloodmoon:Gratian Caerellius") is going to get him killed.

Aphia carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Caerellius_House_Key "Skyrim:Caerellius House Key") to Crescius' house, among [other things](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and wears a [Dunmer outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Outfit "Skyrim:Dunmer Outfit") and [Dunmer shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Shoes "Skyrim:Dunmer Shoes"). If attacked, she defends herself with a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). She knows the Restoration spell [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing").

Aphia speaking to her husband, Crescius

## Related Quests

- **[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)")**: Travel to the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") to find out what's happening there.
- **[The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent")**: Find out what happened to the [great-grandfather](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") of [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").
- **[It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste")**: Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

## Dialogue

When spoken to after hearing the argument between Aphia and Crescius:

:   *"My apologies for Crescius's ravings."*
:   **What were you arguing with Crescius about?**
:   *"That foolish old man thinks he's thirty years younger than he is. He's going to get himself killed traipsing around the mine."*
:   **Why is he exploring the mine?**
:   *"He's convinced himself that there's some sort of conspiracy involving the East Empire Company and the mine's closure.
    We came across some old letters that belonged to his great-grandfather in our house and he believes every word written in them."*
:   **What did the letters say?**
:   *"Crescius's great-grandfather worked for the East Empire Company. The letters mention some sort of discovery he was sent to investigate.
    There's really nothing remarkable in the letters. I don't know what he's so excited about."*
:   **Who was Crescius's great-grandfather?**
:   *"Gratian Caerellius.
    He was an explorer for the East Empire Company. They'd send him all over Tamriel when they had difficulties in a mining operation.
    Poor man... can you imagine doing all that dangerous work just to end up dying at your own doorstep?"*
:   **What happened to him?**
:   *"There was a horrible accident, and he was killed when one of the tunnels collapsed. They were never even able to go down there and recover the body... the East Empire Company sealed that section off to prevent any more tragedies. Crescius is convinced it's a story cooked up by the company to cover up something else, but I don't know."*
:   **You don't agree with Crescius?**
:   *"My beloved is almost eighty years old and I think the shock of finding one of his ancestor's things has left his mind a bit... confused. I love him dearly, and I support everything he does, but I can't let him chase this silly idea or he may end up joining Gratian in a rocky grave."*

She can be asked about how she met Crescius:

:   **How did you meet Crescius?**
:   *"To understand how we met one another, you have to appreciate what he's going through. Crescius is a third-generation miner... all his life, he's lived and breathed nothing else. By the time Crescius came of age, the ebony mine in Raven Rock was shut down. He took that quite hard."*
:   **Why didn't he move somewhere else to find work?**
:   *"Our home has been in his family for over two hundred years. Leaving would have been like abandoning precious memories.
    Instead, he stayed on Solstheim and spent most of his life prospecting for a new ebony source. Sadly, it never surfaced.
    A decade ago, this drove him into a deep depression. He shut himself inside his home and refused to come out."*
:   **This is where you met?**
:   *"It was. After refusing to allow anyone to bring him food, Councilor Morvayn ordered his door to be knocked down before Crescius starved to death.
    I was a Temple priest at the time, and they had me use my healing arts to restore strength to his ailing body.
    I stayed for a while and cared for him, then... I suppose we fell in love."*
:   **You're a priest at the Temple?**
:   *"Far from it. In fact, I'm no longer welcome there."*
:   **Why?**
:   *"In all honesty, it came down to a disagreement between what I believe and what Elder Othreloth believes.
    I'd prefer not to get into the details, but let's just say our opinions about the current status of the Tribunal vary widely."*

Her greetings can be:

:   *"Don't be put off by my husband's mood... he enjoys having visitors."*
:   *"Allow me to apologize for Crescius's behavior, I'm afraid he hasn't been himself lately."*
:   *"It's been tough running the household alone, but Crescius isn't getting any younger."*
:   *"Those East Empire people should be ashamed of themselves for abandoning Raven Rock."*
:   *"I don't know what you did in those mines, but it put a smile on Crescius's face. I've never seen him so happy."* (Once The Final Descent is complete)

### Dragonborn

:   **What's being built outside of town?**
:   *"The Earth Stone is there, and the rest... It's a shrine, but I... Did we build that? I'm not sure."*

### The Final Descent

:   *"Why you're leading Crescius on, I'll never understand."*
:   **I'm guessing you don't agree with Crescius's story.**
:   *"Poor Crescius is aging and I believe it's addled his mind.
    As the years have passed, it's gotten worse. He's become obsessed with his theories of conspiracy."*
:   **Then where's his great-grandfather?**
:   *"I'm sure he's down there somewhere, buried under a mountain of rubble like the East Empire Company claims.
    My greatest fear is that my stubborn mule of a husband will end up suffering the same fate."*

### Reluctant Steward

:   **Do you want to be the new steward of Tel Mithryn?**
:   *"Me? I hardly think so.
    That Telvanni wizard is unhinged. I heard he tries to drink the ash."*

### It's All In The Taste

:   **Geldis Sadri wants you to try his new drink.**
:   *"Well that sounds lovely. Thank you."*

## Conversations

Aphia in Raven Rock Mine

When you first enter Raven Rock Mine:

:   **Crescius**: *"Damn it, woman! I said to leave me be!"*
:   **Aphia**: *"Crescius, last time you explored the mine you almost fell to your death. I'm not spending the rest of my days as a widow!"*
:   **Crescius**: *"And I'm telling you that I'll do whatever it takes to find my great-grandfather's remains. He's down here, I can feel it."*
:   **Aphia**: *"That was almost two centuries ago. There may be nothing left to find."*
:   **Crescius**: *"Just let me go, woman!"*
:   **Aphia**: *"Crescius, you're an obstinate old fool and you're going to get yourself killed."*

She can also have the following conversations with her husband:

:   **Crescius**: *"You're too good to me, Aphia. I only wish I could remain with you longer."*
:   **Aphia**: *"It doesn't matter, my husband. Let's simply cherish the time we have for now."*
:   **Crescius**: *"And what will you do when I'm gone?"*
:   **Aphia**: *"Then I'll simply have to fall in love with some other senile, grousing old fool."*

:   **Crescius**: *"They've laughed at me, Aphia. They thought I was a crazy old fool. But I proved them wrong."*
:   **Aphia**: *"People laugh at things they don't believe. It helps them accept the unknown."*
:   **Crescius**: *"You're too kind to people, always giving them the benefit of the doubt. Don't know how you put up with it."*
:   **Aphia**: *"Well, I put up with you, don't I?"*

# Skyrim:Apocrypha (Epistolary Acumen)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Black Book: Epistolary Acumen | | |
| # of Zones | 4 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 25 |
| Occupants | |
| [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"), [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Black Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") *[Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")* *[Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness")* *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2Book02DungeonNEW | |
| Location | |
| [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") | |

The Epistolary Acumen Black Book in Nchardak

**Epistolary Acumen** is an area of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora")'s [plane of Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Planes_of_Oblivion "Lore:Planes of Oblivion"), [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"). There are four zones (or chapters) in the area: *[Chapter I](#Chapter_I)*, *[Chapter II](#Chapter_II)*, *[Chapter III](#Chapter_III)*, and *[Chapter IV](#Chapter_IV)*.

The [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)") needed to access Epistolary Acumen is found inside [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak"). You must complete the quest [The Path of Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Path_of_Knowledge "Skyrim:The Path of Knowledge") in order to retrieve the book.

The realm is inhabited by Daedra called [Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Seeker "Skyrim:Seeker") and [Lurkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker"). Tentacles constantly breach the acidic dark waters and sometimes whip at you, causing a significant amount of damage if they manage to hit you. The acidic waters with the tentacles are also corrosive and cause damage if stepped in.

## Related Quests

- **[The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men")**: Travel to the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") to learn the rest of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will").

### Chapter I

Chapter I opens on a small platform. In the middle of the platform, two fonts of magicka flank a scrye that lowers a bridge to a corridor moving side-to-side ahead to the west. Proceeding to the far end of the corridor and riding it to the far right leads to a platform with a font of stamina and a scrye that lowers another bridge. Remaining at this end of the corridor and riding it most of the way to the left leads to the new bridge and the final platform, with a font of stamina and the book to Chapter II.

- 

  Opening area
- 

  Book to Chapter II

### Chapter II

Chapter II starts in a tunnel leading to a scrye. The scrye unfurls the walls of the tunnel, revealing a large room guarded by two seekers and a lurker. To the east is a font of magicka and a scrye that opens the gate to the west. In the southeast corner is a pod. In the southwest corner is a table with two random soul gems. Two fonts of magicka flank the gate. Beyond the gate is a small room with a pod, two fonts of stamina, and the book to Chapter III.

- 

  Opening tunnel
- 

  Room unraveled
- 

  Book to Chapter III

### Chapter III

Chapter III starts on a platform in a huge room guarded by two seekers, with one on a platform to the north and the other on a platform to the east. Behind the starting point is a font of stamina. On the platform occupied by the first seeker is a font of magicka in the middle of an acidic pool. At the top of the sets of stairs to the east is another font of magicka in an acidic pool and a moving corridor.

Remaining at the near end of the corridor and riding it partway to the right leads to a platform above a larger platform guarded by a lurker and a seeker. Dropping to the larger platform raises a set of ramps from the floor, allowing access to a pod on a pillar in the middle of the platform. To the south is a font of magicka and a scrye that raises a bridge back to the platform before the moving corridor.

Remaining at the near end of the corridor and riding it to the far right leads to a platform guarded by two seekers. On the platform are two tables, two fonts of magicka, and a pod. On the table to the left are three soul gems (two random and one [black](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem")). On the table to the right is a copy of the [Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Conjure_Seeker "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Conjure Seeker") (only if your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least level 40) and copies of three [skill books](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") for three of the "[combat](/wiki/Skyrim:Combat "Skyrim:Combat")" skills: *[Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness")* ([One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")), *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")* ([Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor")), and *[Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")* ([Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block")).

Returning to the corridor and proceeding to the far end leads to a scrye that opens a pair of gates next to the scrye. Beyond the gates is a corridor leading south guarded by a seeker. Proceeding around a corner to the east in the corridor causes it to move to the left and lower a bridge to another corridor guarded by a lurker. Proceeding to the end of this corridor causes it to move to the left and connect to a platform with a scrye that opens a pair of gates behind the scrye. Beyond the gates is another corridor guarded by a seeker. The corridor passes a font of stamina and a circular room with six empty pedestals, then widens and passes two fonts of magicka, a font of stamina, and three seekers to end at another font of stamina and the book to Chapter IV.

- 

  Opening area
- 

  Chapter III
- 

  Chapter III

### Chapter IV

Chapter IV starts on a platform. Next to the starting point is a table with three soul gems (two random and one black). To the south is a vessel and a scrye that forms a bridge to another platform ahead, where the black book *Epistolary Acumen* and its secrets await. When the book is activated for the first time, Hermaeus Mora appears and teaches you the second word of the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), also offering a bargain in exchange for the third and final word of the shout. To exit this part of Apocrypha, use the non-circular part of the black book.

The three [Abilities](/wiki/Skyrim:Abilities "Skyrim:Abilities") offered by this book are:

- [Dragonborn Flame](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Flame "Skyrim:Dragonborn Flame") — When your [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") shout kills an enemy, a fire wyrm emerges from their corpse to fight for you for 60 seconds.
- [Dragonborn Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Force "Skyrim:Dragonborn Force") — Your [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout does more damage, and using all three words may disintegrate enemies.
- [Dragonborn Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Frost "Skyrim:Dragonborn Frost") — Your [Frost Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Breath "Skyrim:Frost Breath") shout encases foes in ice for 15 seconds.

- 

  Opening area
- 

  Bridge
- 

  Black book

## Notes

- When you read the Black Book associated with this area of Apocrypha for the first time, [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") will say, *"Oh, good. Be sure to say hello to [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") for me if you see him."* He will talk to you again once you return to Solstheim.
